#/ /dus gsum rgyal ba'i mkhyen brtse nus pa'i rang gzugs dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i gtso bo khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa'i ngo bo mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan bstan pa'i rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar dad pa'i rlabs phreng zhes bya ba bzhugs// //

/ /oM swasti siddhaM/ dus gsum rgyal kun mkhyen brtse nus pa'i rang gzugs dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i gtso bo khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa'i ngo bo mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan
bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar dad pa'i rlabs phreng zhes bya ba gdan gsum tshang ba'i dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i zhabs sen zla ba'i
cod pan byang chen mthar thug gtsug tor rtse mor 'ching ba de srid brtse ba chen pos rjes su bzung ste byin gyis brlab tu gsol/ rigs kun bdag po rdo rje 'chang chen mi yi
gzugs su song ba'i gar/ /dang po'i mgon po bsod nams zhing du e wa~M zung 'jug sgyu ma'i 'phrul/ /rnam kun mchog ldan 'gro la rjes brtse bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan legs 'dzin
pa/ /dpal ldan bla ma mkhas btsun bzang po'i 'khor los sgyur de rgyal gyur cig /gdul dka' 'dul la dpa' ba'i snying stobs kyis/ /brgya pa'i tshe dus mchog

gi sprul pa'i gar/ /legs bsgyur shAkya seng ge dkyil 'khor gtsor/ /rab bzhengs dgyes mdzad rdo rje he ru kaH mkha' la mkha' yi sbyor ltar gnyis med yum/ /zag med bde chen bskyed
pa'i bdag med mas/ /rjes bzung rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa/ /paN grub yongs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal/ /mgon de'i dbang gi mtho ris chu bo'i rgyun/ /lo paN
skal ldan shing rtas nyer drangs pa/ /rnam dpyod lto bar 'khyil ba'i drang srong che/ /sa skya'i bla chen rjes 'brang bcas las su/ /gang gi bstan srog rgyu skar 'phreng
ba'i dbus/ /snyan brgyud tshad ma bzhi yi snang ba'i gzi/ /cher 'bar slob bshad 'dzin pa'i bdag chen rje/ /rdo rje 'chang dbang blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal/ /mgon de'i gdams
pa'i bang mdzod kha'u pa/ /kun spangs bla ma'i snyan brgyud zil dngar gyis/ /thugs kyi za ma tog gtams tshar pa rje'i/ /dri med ring lugs yid bzhin dbang gi

rgyal/ /dmar ser dhIHyig bzhu blugs mi yi gzugs/ /'khor lo'i mgon po bsod nams skal bzang dpyid/ /mchog tu mi 'gyur bde ba'i bdag nyid can/ /dpal ldan bla ma khyab bdag rdo
rje sems/ /a ho 'phags bod ris med grub mtha'i srol/ /'dzin pa'i mkhas grub yang srid mtha' klas kyang / /zhing 'dir 'jam mgon bla ma sa skya pa'i/ /bstan pa'i khur chen
rnam dpyod phrag par lci/ /dbang lung rjes gnang rig gtad rgyud bshad zlas/ /gdul bya'i blo yi kunda bzhad pa'i mod/ /grol lam ka spu ra yi gzegs ma'i rdul/ /thabs pas sgrib
gnyis tsha gdung sel la sbyor/ /gcig tu rnam gsum mkhas pa'i bya ba la/ /rtag par 'grus kyang rim gnyis rnal 'byor gyis/ /gang thugs mtshan dpes yongs spras he ru kar/
/bzhengs pa'i cho ga rdzogs pa 'di ko mtshar/ /de phyir mes pos bskal par bsams byas kyang / /gting mtha' dpag par dka' na bdag 'dra bas/ /rtogs brjod smra ba 'dab chags
rtse sgro yis/ /mthon po brag ri zad par byed pa bzhin/ /'on te rnam 'dren dus mkhyen rgyal po yis/ /bde bshegs rtswa mchog bstod pa'i legs byas bzhin/ /rdo rje slob dpon
bsngags pa'i skal bzang 'di/ /grangs med skye bar chos dkar zong gis bsgrubs/ /de phyir rnam par thar pa'i pi wang rgyud/ /bcad lhug tshig gi sor mos legs bskul sgra/
/dpyod ldan rna bar 'jebs pa rdo rje'i glu/ /gzhom med nA da'i dbyangs su blangs 'di nyon/ /de'ang 'jam mgon

sa skya paNDi tas/ /mchod bstod 'dud pa'i bdag nyid can/ /shis pa brjod sogs mi 'gal te/ /thams cad du yang ston pa yi/ /che ba 'ba' zhig ston phyir ro/ /zhes pa'i don ltar
tshigs bcad dpyid kyi rgyal mo'i glu dbyangs sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas gleng bar bya ba ni/ mkhas pa'i gsung las/ gang phyir dge legs thams cad ni/ /rtag tu sbyin zhing
'phel 'gyur ba'i/ /thub bstan dpag bsam ljon shing gi /ngo mtshar gleng la su mi gus/ /zhes bdag cag gi rnam 'dren dam pa rigs dang dkyil 'khor kun gyi khyab bdag mgon po
bsod nams mchog ldan bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po 'di nyid/ byon dang 'byon 'gyur 'byon bzhin pa'i sras bcas rgyal ba mtha' dag gi sku gsung thugs yon tan 'phrin
las thams cad kyi ngo bo/ de dag gi mgur gyi bum pa nas dam pa'i chos kyi phung po zad mi shes pa ljags kyi dbang po legs par bkram ste gdul bya rnams kyi rna bar 'jebs
pa'i sgra bo che yongs kyi snying por gyur pa nang rig pa sde snod gsum dang rgyud sde bzhi'i 'byung gnas de rnams klog pa thos bsam dang spong ba bsam gtan gyi sgo nas
tshul bzhin 'dzin pa'i theg gsum skyes 'phags 'dus pa'i dbang phyug /ris su ma chad pa'i grub pa'i mtha' rgya mtsho chen po'i pha rol tu son pas mkhas pa/ nyis brgya lnga
bcu rtsa gsum sogs nyes ltung gi cha phra mo tsam gyis kyang ma gos par las 'bras la zhib mor dpyod pas btsun pa/ bdag bas gzhan gces pa'i byang chub kyi sems rin po che
thugs la 'khrungs pas gzhan don lhur mdzad pas bzang po/

ma nub dbang gi chu bos thugs rgyud smin pas grol byed bskyed pa dang rdzogs pa'i rim pa ni zab lam la brten nas grub pa'i mtha' snyog par nus ldan rig sngags 'chang ba sogs
gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i yon tan gyi phung po tshangs pa/ dbang phyug /khyab 'jug ste 'jig rten gyi gtso bo gsum dang nyan rang byang sems so skye'i tshogs kyis
gzhal bar dka' ba 'phags pa rnams kyi ye shes kho na'i spyod yul nyag gcig pa bdag 'dra'i blo gros kyi cha phra bas lta ga la zhig /sku tshe'i 'phreng ba du mar thub bstan
rin po che gsal bar byed pa'i mkhas grub kyi skyes rabs mu thi la'i 'phreng mdzes dang / sku tshe 'dir yang lha dang bla ma mang po zhal gzigs shing lung bstan thob pa/
rdo rje chos skyong bran du 'khol ba'i 'phrin las sgrub pa/ sa lam gyi yon tan phul du byung ba ni/ zhu lan nor bu'i 'phreng bar/ bdag gi yon tan sba bya zhing / /gzhan
gyi yon tan bsgrag par bya/ /zhes pa'i don bzhin yon tan mtha' dag rgya mtsho'i gting gi rdo ba ltar mi mngon pa gtso bor 'don pas bsnyel tho dang zhal slob kyi rigs la
gsung 'phros kyi zur tsam yang cher ma gsungs shing / kho bos gsung ngag rin po che zhus skabs mdang rmi lam du po ta la'i li ma lha khang yin rgyu bal ze'u lha khang 'dra
rung ba'i glo skar nas bltas pas rje btsun sa skya pa chen po bzhugs 'dug pa zhig byung ba gsung ngag rin po che 'di'i 'chad nyan la dgyes pa 'dra gsung ba zhib tu zhus
kyang de tsam las mi dran zhes thugs dkyil che bas gsal bar mi mdzad na'ang don du mnal ltas ma yin pas gzigs

snang ngo mtshar ba zhig byung tshod du mchis/ snga phyir mjal ba tsho'i skabs nan tan du zhus na thor bu tsam mi gsung ba'i nges pa mi 'dug kyang rang nyid rtag par 'dzin
pa'i 'ching ba dam pos bcings pa'i dbang gis rje bla ma'ang sku tshe mthar phyin par bzhugs pa gzhir bcas kyi slar rim gyis zhu 'dun la lus song zhing zur thams cad mkhyen
pa dang / rje 'di nyid zhal 'dris ye med pa'i skabs mnal lam la gzims khang shar yin khul du khri mtho bar sa lugs kyi bla ma yin zer ba sku bong che zhing gzi brjid phun
sum tshogs pa zhig la dbang chos mang po gsan pa'i mnal ltas byung ba nas lo gcig tsam gyi thog yar klungs bkra shis rtse chos sder zab chos gsan par glo bur du phebs
par shar ba'i sgo dod cing zhing skyong dbang po'i chos skor rnams gsan nas gung thang du phebs pa'i 'od gsal zhig la ras ljang gu'i ang rag tsam las gos gzhan med pa skra
dang sma ra dkar po byas pa lag tu mi rkang gi gling bu thogs pa zhig na re mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan 'di slob dpon dharma pA la/ gzims khang shar gyi bla ma zhig dang
tshar pa chos rje sogs kyi skye ba yin/ khyod kyis nga la gtor ma re'ang ma chag pa gyis/ nga'i chos skor rnams su rung rung la ma ston zer ba zhig byung snang ba bdag
yid bzhag chungs pas kha che rin cen rdo rje dang dharma pA la gnyis som nyir gyur rung slar dpyad tshe phyi ma nyid du nges shing bka' las/ rjes sor gzims khang shar du
yun ring por stan chags pa dang mdzad pa'i tshul rnams la rjes su dpags tshe tshar

chen chos kyi rgyal po thub bstan spyi dang bye brag rang bstan kha'u brag rdzong pa'i ring lugs 'dzin par sprul pa'i zlos gar bstan pa 'dra phebs pa rdo rje'i gsung bla na
med par go /gzhan du bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rtogs pa brjod pa'i rngo ma thogs na'ang snyigs dus kyi gdul bya smin pa gsum shas chung / sgrib pa gsum gyi bag chags ches
cher bdo ba'i gang zag rnams kyi blo dang 'tsham par rnam par thar pa rgya mtsho lta bu las cher long tsam drung du 'khod pa'i rgyus yod 'dras zin bris su btab cing / rigs
kun khyab bdag zha lu mkhan chen kun spangs pa chen po'i spyan ras kyis btsa' bar mdzad de lam tsam zhus dag pa'i steng nas cung zad 'dri ba ni/ rin po che sdud pa las/
'dzam bu'i gling 'dir chu klung ji snyed cig 'bab cing / /me tog 'bras ldan sman dang nags tshal skyed byed pa/ /ma dros gnas pa'i klu dbang klu bdag brten gnas te/ /de
ni klu yi bdag po de yi mthu dpal yin/ /rgyal ba'i nyan thos pa dag ji snyed chos ston dang / /'chad dang rig pa dag dang ldan par brjod pa dang / /mchog 'phags bde ba byed
dang de yi 'bras thob pa/ /de dag kun kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i skyes bu'i mthu/ /zhes 'dzam bu'i gling gi chu klung sman dang nags tshal sogs klu'i rgyal po'i mthu las
byung ba bzhin thub pa'i rjes 'jug gi tshogs thos bsam sgom pa'i mthu la brten nas 'bras bu thob pa rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs rje las byung bar gsungs pa spyir
sangs rgyas 'jig rten du mi 'byon pa'i tshe mun bskal dang byung ba'i

dus sgron bskal du bshad pas bskal pa bzang po 'di la sangs rgyas stong 'byung bar gsungs pa'i 'o skol gyi ston pa shAkya seng ge'i lung rtogs kyi bstan pa yul dbus 'gyur 'chad
du dar rgyas su gyur pa nas yun ring zhig nas bod du dam pa'i chos 'byung bar lha mo dri ma med pas zhus pa'i mdo las/ nga yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas lo nyis stong
lnga brgya na gdong dmar can gyi yul du dam pa'i chos dar ba 'gyur ro/ /zhes sA la'i nags kyi sman ljongs ri kha ba can gyi khrod du rgyal ba'i bstan pa byung ba'ang spyir
'gro ba mi'i byung tshul lha las phul byung gi bstod 'grel du/ skya seng bu lnga dang dgra ngan dpung tshogs bcu gnyis 'thabs pa'i dus su rgyal po rU pa ti zhes pa dmag
stong phrag gcig dang bcas pa bud med kyi chas su zhugs te/ ri gangs can gyi gseb tu bros pa las 'phel tshul byung zhing rgyal po bka' 'bum sogs thugs rje chen po'i chos
skor rnams su spyan ras gzigs dang sgrol ma'i sprul pa spre'u dang brag srin mo 'dus pa las 'phel bar bshad pa gdong dmar sha zan gyi phrug gu shin tu gdul bar dka' bar
chos la blo mi 'jug pa rnams bka' gdams glegs bam rin po cher/ bod ni rgyal po dag la tshad mar 'dzin/ /mi dbang mdzod la bod khams bde bar skyongs/ /zhes thog mar 'bangs
mtha' dag rgyal po chen po zhig gi mnga' 'og tu bsdus te rim gyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las 'byung bar mkhyen nas bod spyi'i rgyal po la snga ba rje gnya' khri btsan
po nas rgyal rabs rim par byung la/

dam pa 'di'i rigs ni/ bod rgyal po'i dbon du gyur pa'i 'a zha zhes bya zhing de'ang zur mkhar blo gros rgyal po'i shes bya spyi'i khog dbug gtan pa med pa'i mchod sbyin gyi
sgo 'phar yangs por bon gyi gtam rgyud drangs par/ gri gum btsan po'i dus dmag drangs nas kha che'i yul bcoms pa'i tshe yul bye brag pa puNdra sur brag nyung ma ltar gshog
par byed pa'i rdzu 'phrul can gyi mu stegs bye brag pa zhig la 'a zha zer zhes gang zag cig la ngos bzung zhing mi shi ba dang phyugs bsad pa rang gi mi phyugs su skye/
phung po dang mnyam du sbas pa skye ba phyi ma dbang bar lung ston/ sha khrag gis mi ma yin pa rngan nas smreng gis dkrol bas phan par byed pa la bon nam leng tser grags
la/ des ma rungs te rgyal po'ang long ngam rta rdzi zhes pas bkums smra ba gri gum gyi dus bod du 'a zha byung bar 'dod pa 'dra snang ba dang / dpa' bo gtsug lag gis mkhas
pa dga' byed du/ gurNa kha tra zhes bya'i yul khams nas/ /mu stegs bon po 'a zha zhes pa byung / /zhes ngos bzung pa'i rdzu 'phrul can des rgyal po'i mtshan gri gum zhes
btags par brten nas rgyal po grir bkums par bshad/ de nas rgyal rabs nyi shu rtsa bzhi pa dmus long dkon pa bkras byung bar yab 'gro gnyan lde'us ba zha'i yul nas sman
pa bos nas mig phye gsung pa bzhin phye bas spyan byung ste ltag ri gnyan gzigs su grags pa ltar na 'a zha zhes pa yul gyi ming du bshad/ thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya
mtsho'i rnam thar zhal gsungs mar/ khri srong

lde'u btsan gyi skabs/ rje sreg po khyung bzhi lha jo bo lcam dang lnga/ 'bangs ra klog can dang drug /se 'a zha gnyis dang bcas pa rnams/ chad pa mdo khams sgang nas chad/
chags pa g.yas ru shangs su chags zhes pa rnams gungs bsgrigs na gang zag rang mtshan pa zhig la bkar nas rgya gar phyogs na yod tshul khungs dag par mi sems te bon dang
mu stegs mi gcig pas lo rgyus de 'dra dwags brgyud pas bon gyi rjes su 'brangs pa'i sgrung gi bye brag tu snang / spyir 'dzam bu gling pa'i mi rigs phyi bar nang gsum las/
rgyal rigs/ rje rigs/ bram ze'i rigs/ dmangs rigs te phyi rigs bzhi/ rgya gar lha/ rgya nag klu/ hor lha ma yin/ bod spre'u dang brag srin mo ste bar gyi rigs bzhi/ bka'
chems bka' khol mar/ sprel phrug spun bzhi brgya po de tshan pa bzhir 'thabs pa dang mes pos bar mtshams byas te zhing la cha bzhir bgos/ gcig la gcig 'jigs nas tshan
bzhir chad pas se dang / rmu dang / ldong dang / stong ste nang mi'u rigs bzhi rnams bcu gnyis po rigs kyi phyi mor grags/ mi'u gdung drug tu dbye na bod mi khri tho chen
po bya ba de la dgra 'bru ldong lga dang nu bo dpa' rda ste bu drug ces bshad spyan snga lha gzigs ras pa'i yig tshang du/ dga' ldong 'bru gsum dgra dang bzhi/ /nu bo dpa'
mda' gnyis te drug tu gsungs/ /tshal pa thams cad mkhyen pa si tu dge ba'i blo gros kyi hu lan deb ther du spre'u dang brag srin mo las mched pa

ma sangs spun dgu/ rgyal phran nyi shu rtsa lnga/ bcu gnyis/ sil ma bzhi bcus rim gyis dbang byas par bshad pa kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi rnam thar du mi'u gdung
drug gi nang tshan du gsungs pa grong du dngos ming ngos ma 'phrod kyang zhwa dmar thams cad mkhyen pa bzhi pas mdzad pa'i khrus khang lo tsA ba bsod nams rgyal mtsho'i
rnam thar du/ phyi'i rus chen ldong la nang tshan bco brgyad du gyes pa'i rog yin te/ zhes nang gses kyi khyad par du ngos 'dzin pa rnam dpyod dang ldan pa'i gsung 'di
bzhin ltar rus so sor dbye gzhi gcig la dbye ba'i ya gyal mang du byung ba'i rus chen drug gi dang po'i nang gses su gtogs pa gor ma chag /rgyal phran sil ma'i khrod kyi
rgyal por gyur pa rje gnya' khri btsan pos bod spyi la dbang sgyur ba nas mnga' 'og tu gyur cing rje dang gnyen bsres pas dbon du song / lha btsan pos bstan pa rin po che'i
ched du chos kyi bca' khrims mdzad pa'i tshe na rjer gtogs pas rdo ring gi yi ger yang dbon 'a zha zhes rgyal rigs khungs btsun dri ma med pa de las rim par brgyud de
glang dar gyis bstan pa bsnubs rjes so thar gyi bstan pa'i me ro smad nas bslang ba'i tshe 'a zha mgo bo che'i sras 'a zha ye shes g.yung drung gis khams su sdom pa len
par 'byon pa'i zhor du ra sa 'phrul snang gi gtsug lag khang mjal du byon pa'i dus steng khang la 'gro ba'i skas kyi mar zur gdong la dpal ye shes mgon po'i sku gzugs ri
mor bris pa yar 'dzeg skabs yod pa la mar lam bris sku de dpal mgon po dngos su gyur cing thod ba'i

nang na dgra bo'i snying khrag blug pa mi rtsib kyis thur ma byas te gsol ba mngon sum du bstan nas rjes su bzung bar gsol ba btab pas/ khyod kyi mi brgyud dang chos brgyud
bcas pa'i srung ma ngas bya/ khyod khams nas zla ba gcig la 'khor bar gyis zhes gsung gi gnang ba thob pas 'a zha mthu che bar grags shing mgon po 'di nyid rtsis mgon yin
par sems/ khams su byon nas bla chen gyi mkhan bu tre bo mchog bla la sdom pa der bas ma'i rgyun blangs nas sna nam 'dres brda/ 'o yug /gnas po che sogs dge 'dun gyi sde
btsugs pa de dag las gyes te mang du 'phel/ kun mkhyen bu'i chos 'byung du sdom pa chab gtor ma'i rgyun blangs zhes snang / de nas 'a zha lha'i blo gros kyis lha ldan gtsug
lag khang la zhig gsos dang rdo kong bkra shis 'od 'bar phul/ a mes jo sras phur pa 'phel gyis rngog lo rgya gar du 'byon pa'i cha rkyen la gser srang bcu bdun phul/
gegs med par phyir byon nas lo tsA ba'i chos 'khor gyi thog ma yang 'dol chung du bskor/ dpal ayon chen pos byin gyis brlabs shing ma hA kA la dngos su bzhugs pa'i gnas
dang zung 'brel du jo bo blo gros kyis gnas gzhi btab pas rtsis gnas gsal bar grags/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i mnga' thang sgang la rgyag pa'i dus chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa
rin po che dang ti shri kun blo sogs kyi zhabs la/ nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ nam mkha' bzang po/ shAkya seng ge can gyis gtugs par nyang gzhung mtha' dag shes su bcug

pa'i 'ja' sa la gser gyi tham ka /shel gyi nyin shan/ dngul gyi sgor mo lung dang bcas las ka gnang bas gnas gsar stong dpon du grags/ rgyal po/ sngags 'chang / ge sar gyi
yon tan tshang ba'i mi bdag rim byon las stong dpon kun dga' rdo rje'i sras nang so chos kyi rgyal po'i khab tu snyan brgyud kyi mnga' bdag 'jam dbyangs chos rje'i lcam rdo
rje rnal 'byor ma'i sprul pa dpal ldan 'dzom pa byon par lcam sring brgyad byung ba'i bgres pa nang so rnam rgyal dpal bzang slob dpon chen po padma'i rnam 'phrul sku
zhang 'jam dbyangs chos rje nam mkha' rgyal mtshan yab sras gsum bsten nas 'khon gyi yab chos rdo rje phur pas gtsos gsar rnying gi zab chos mang po zhus shing bsnyen sgrub
bzlas sgom mthar phyin/ slob dpon chen po'i bsnyen phur me 'bar bzhin pa rtsis kyi mchod rten nag po nas bzhes/ dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa lngar phebs na'ang skyes dar ma'i
yang rtsal dang lang tsho ltar gyur pa'i grub mtshan ngo mtshar ba ston/ rin chen sgang pa sgos dang yon mchod du gyur pa'i zhal ngo phyi ma rnams kyis rang bstan gyi
srog 'thud pa'i rten 'brel gyi sgo 'grig /de 'og phyag na rdo rje'i sprul pa nang so mgon po rin cen gyis mgon po zhal gzigs shing thal rdeb kyis log 'dren sgrol ba/ ri dwags
sogs la bya glag gis 'tshe ba'i tshe sngags rgya ting 'dzin tsam gyis sar lhung ba/ mi chos la'ang sgyu rtsal 'gran zla dang bral bar grags/ de 'og 'jam dbyangs kun
dga' blo gros zhes gzhung lugs rgya mtshor sbyangs pa che zhing dngos stobs

rigs pas rgol ba thams cad zhum par nus pa'i gnas gsar chos mdzad ces snyan pa'i sgra bo che kun tu bsgrags/ sgrol dkar gyi sprul par rgyal dbang padma'i lung gis zin pa'i
lcam bgres pa khrom ge sar rgyal po'i mag pa'i brgyud pa shar kha rgyal rtse ba'i khab tu byon nas snga 'gyur gyi rgyud 'bum bzheng ba dang bka' gter bstan pa'i sbyin bdag
zla med du mdzad/ de 'og mar pa'i yum bdag med ma'i sprul par grags par lung du zhabs drung 'brug pa dbon rin po che'i jo mor phebs/ rje btsun ma gsum gyi gcig gis bdag
chen rdo rje 'chang chen por gsung ngag rin po che gsan nas sgrub pa snying por mdzad pas 'da' kha ma'i nyams len gyis grub mtha' snyogs/ rnal 'byor ma kun dga' chos ldan
dang ni gu chos sgron ma gnyis kyis ka thog pa bzhag bla ye shes 'bum dang sprul pa'i gter ston padma gling pa gnyis la btugs nas zab lam rdzogs pa chen po'i chos nyid
zad pa'i sar 'khyol/ nang so sku mched gnyis kyi jo mor sa skya'i nang chen lha khang chen mo ba'i sras mo dpal 'dzom bsus pa'i sras nam mkha' rdo rje tshe brtan dpal 'byor
bzang po ni yig rtsis/ brtag pa rnam pa brgyad la sogs pa lugs kyi bstan bcos la mkhas pa/ sgam zhing brtan la blo gros kyi mthu phul du byung ba/ bdag chen chos rje yab
sras gsum/ lce ston seng ge sogs mkhas grub kyi dam pa mang du bsten/ rang gi a ne 'khrul zhig kun dga' chos ldan la rdzogs pa chen po'i khrid gsan

pas nyams gong 'phel gyi rtogs pa klong du gyur/ thos grol dang gcod yul sogs la brten nas sgyu lus rmi lam la rang dbang thob pas lcang lo can gyis mtshon dag pa'i zhing myul/
gam pa rdzong du phyag rdor gyi bsnyen pa'i tshe thun 'tshams su mar me shi zhing thun dngos la rang 'bar du 'gro ba/ byang chub kyi sems bcos min du 'khrungs shing
klu 'bum gnyan khri'i gdan gsal por gzigs pa/ mnal lam du khyod khyung 'di la zhon nas ri rab la skor ba lan gsum byas te lcang lo can du gshegs par 'gyur ro/ /zhes pa'i
lung bstan rnyed/ gnod byed kyi klu gdug pa can btul ba sogs gsang bdag gis rjes su bzung bar brten/ rje mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis/ 'di nas 'pho tshe byang phyogs lcang lo
can/ /zhing der pha rgan drung du thog mar 'gro/ /de nas ayon zangs mdog dpal ri'i rtser/ /skye ba'i rten 'brel bsgrig la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsung pa'i dgongs gzhi yang
de yin la/ seng ge rtse ba'i blon po mdzad pa sogs srid kyi rnam g.yeng dus 'khrug tshe skabs kyang mtshan bcas mtshan med kyi rnal 'byor ye ma bzhag /snyun dam pos btab
pa'i dus khu bo gnas gsar chos mdzad kyis sgrol ma'i rjes gnang mdzad pa'i tshe sgrol ma ri bo tsam pa'i sku gzigs pas snyun las myur du grol bo dong du jo nang mkhan
chen/ rje btsun sgo rum pa chen po kun dga' legs pa rigs kyi bdag por bsten nas bdag lus longs spyod thams cad mchod sprin du phul/ rje zhing gzhan du gshegs khar rigs brgyud
dkar nag gi 'brel pa bzhag

pas mtha' brten pa kun rjes su 'dzin pa'i zhal bzhes zhus/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje dang ngor chen sangs rgyas seng ge la zab rgyas kyi chos mang du gsan/ sras gnyis
la srid kyi bya ba ma lus pa gtad de bskyed rdzogs kyi rnal 'byor bsnyen sgrub bskang ba mdos gtor sogs thugs dam gyis nyin mtshan dus 'da'/ de dag gi tshe rdo rje chos
skyong zhal gzigs pa/ bsreg mkhan med par sha chen dri ngad 'thul ba/ dgun sman raka khol ba/ lingga 'gul pa/ zor gtor 'phar ba/ mdos gtor gyi gseb nas btso rgyug pa/ gam
pa rdzong du thog sdigs mdzub kyi rtse la blangs te gzhan du 'phangs pa dang / bo dong rdzong du babs kyang ma gnod cing sdigs mdzub dang shA sa na'i nus pas hor dmag bros
pa/ rong chung ngu rbab dang tsag sa dkar grur chu rlabs kyi 'jigs pa sdigs 'dzub dang bcas pa'i phaT sgras bzlog pa/ mnal lam la ti phu bas sku tshe'i tshad lung bstan
pa sogs ngo mtshar rnams ches dpag par dka' na'ang zhang ston chos 'bar/ rje mar pa/ mkhas pa g.yu thog pa sogs la'ang las ma dag pa'i skye bo phal cher khyim pa rang
bzhin pa'i mthong las med 'dug pa ltar 'di skabs kyang sde dpon dkyus ma'i rtsing hral zhig gi nyams las med par snang / de'ang mnal lam du ri rab la lan gsum bskor zhes
pa skye ba gsum brgyud dgos rgyur lam zab mo'i nyams len la brten nas dgung lo re brgyad pa khrums zla'i tshes bcu'i nyin gshegs khar tshar chen la

re ltos zhus pas skyabs 'jug shin tu rgyas pa dang khyad par rdo ring rin po cher gsol 'debs shugs drag gnang bas mnal lam du rdo ring pa chen pos khong pa las kyi rnam smin
gyi 'phro zhig gis rgya nag gi mtha' 'khob tu ru dra mo'i mngal du zla ba drug gnas dgos pa chos skyong gis ma de bsgral nas lcang lo can du skye na'ang chos rje pas 'bad
rtsol mdzad na zla ba gcig tsam gyis chog nyen 'dug cing gang ltar do nub mjal du 'ong ba yod gsung ba ltar sngon dus kyi cha lugs ji lta ba dzo ki'i 'khor la brten nas
byung ba bdag tshe 'phos kyang bla ma dang chos skyong gi mthus rgyal kha byung / phyag rdor gyi dbang gnang bar gsol bas sang nas bzung phyag rdor gyi dkyil 'khor du lho
sgo'i cho ga lan gsum mdzad pas nub cig 'od gsal du 'brug sgra dir dir sgrog par gzigs pa na nang 'od kyi rnam pa'i nor bu mig gsum pas gang ba gsal bas sde pa de lcang
lo can du 'brug gi zhon pa can gyi gnod sbyin bde ldan 'od zer du skyes nas drin lan 'jal du 'ongs par mkhyen cing gnod sbyin de phyag na rdo rjes rjes su bzung bar brten
thugs bde bar gyur/ 'di pa'i yum snga mo nas grongs pas chun mar gtsang tshong 'dus mgur mo'i khri dpon gyi lcam sring byang sems bu khrid blangs pa'i sras nam mkha' rgyal
ba lce ston paN chen las dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa nos/ gong gi yongs 'dzin phal cher dang / sprul sku shAkya bzang po/ gnubs chen rin cen dpal bzang / lha btsun legs ldan
bdud 'joms rdo rje sogs dam pa mang du bsten/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal

po la thugs sgrub drag po rtsal gyi chos skor gsan pa gtso bor gyur pa'i bde mchog /gshed dmar/ phur pa/ sgrol dkar sogs yi dam gyi lha rnams kyi bsnyen sgrub dang mkha' 'gro
lnga'i mchod gtor gyi mtshon thugs dam shin tu smin/ sku tshe'i smad la tshar chen gyi drung du rab tu byung zhing dgung lo don gnyis pa'i tshe tshar chen rdo rje 'chang
spyan drangs pa sngas mgor bla ma 'di lta bu phebs nas 'chi ba skal ba bzang tshul sogs dgyes dgyes dang bar dor yang hUM sgra dir dir 'gro gsung / gshegs nas dbu thod
sor bzhi tsam 'phags shing me tog gi char gyis mtshon ltas ya mtshan gshis rtog ge pa rgan po 'ga'i nga rgyal chag pa sogs la dpags na gcen du ma zad 'di nyid la'ang ding
sang gi chos pa bzang por rtsi ba rnams kyis bsgrun dka' bar mchis/ mched gnyis kyi jo mor se ston dpal chen 'bum dang mthu chen nyi ma bzang po sogs yang phur gshin rjes
gtsos lha'i snang ba thob cing chos skyong bran du 'khol ba'i rigs brgyud rje btsun sa skya pa'i dpon por gyur pa 'dar chos rdzong pa don yod rnam rgyal gyi sras mo tshe
brtan bu 'dren zhes bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje sgo rum pas mtshon dam pa du ma'i zhabs pad bsten cing tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po dang 'khrul zh-ig kun dga' chos
ldan la gdams pa'i nying khu nos nas mgon po'i yig bdun ma sa ya gsum dang nA ro mkha' spyod kyi chag med mdzad pas mnal lam du rje btsun zhal gnyis ma gser gyi mdog ldan
gzigs shing phag skad ngur sgras khengs pa sogs grub pa'i mtshan ma brnyes pa bud med phal

pa'i ngang tshul las 'das pa de bsus pa la mched kha yar 'khrungs pa'i dang po zhabs drung bstan pa'i drung ngam bsod nams rab brtan du grags pa/ de 'og chos kyi rgyal mtshan/
de 'og thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug chung ba nor bu bzang po rnams las gcen dang gcung rnams ni sgyu rtsal drug cu rtsa bzhis gtsos lugs dang 'brel
ba'i yon tan gyi mthu phul du byung zhing rje btsun sgo rum pa chen po dang rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje sogs sngags gsar rnying gi mkhas grub du ma'i zhabs rdul nye
bar bsten nas zab chos mang du gsan cing de'ang tshig tsam du ma lus par bskyed rdzogs kyi rnal 'byor bsnyen cing sgrub pa rdo rje chos skyong rnams phyi nang gsang ba'i
mchod pas thugs dam skong ba'i mdzad pa sogs sde dpon phal pa'i spyod tshul dang ye mi 'dra ba'i gong ma'i zhabs rjes zin pa thub pa'i ring lugs 'dzin no cog la dag pa'i
snang ba dang ldan na'ang rang bstan kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bla ma dang chos las bstan dang ston pa gzhan nas mi 'tshol ba'i dam bca' brtan po spang la be phur btab pa'am
rdo la ri mo bris pa lta bu'i dam pa'i ngang tshul dang ldan pa sha stag yin no/ /e ma gangs can dpal mo'i mngal yangs por/ /bsod nams 'bras bu'i khur gyis rab lci ba/ /rigs
gsum sgyu dra'i gar mkhan mi yi bdag /chad me mtho ris chu bo'i spun zla bzhin/ /ded dpon 'od gsal lha babs 'a zha'i gdung / /che gnyan btsun gsum 'dzom pa rgyal po'i
brgyud/ /mthu stobs nus par ldan pa rig sngags 'chang / /dpa' rtsal

gdong ngar che ba ge sar rigs/ /rlung gis mthon por bteg pa'i 'dab chags sgro/ /'gro mangs ral pa'i rtse mor stes dbang las/ /g.yengs min khungs 'brel lus phra'i 'gram chang
gis/ /dpyod ldan blo yi ba ku la de bzhad/ /rdul mang phang par nyal ba'i khri stan steng / /chen por bkur bar mi bsnyengs byang chen la/ /gzhol bas indra bhU ti rna rgyan
gyis/ /ljongs 'dir gzugs can gnyis pa bzung ba bzhin/ /de'ang tshigs gsum pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga
nas kyi yongs grags kyi rnam par thar pa dgung lo sum cu so brgyad yan gyi rtogs brjod rang nyid kyis mdzad pa'i ngo mtshar snye mar gsungs pa smos ma dgos/ de nas kyang
lo phyed drug tsam gyi bar zhing 'dir bzhugs pas 'phro 'thud thub na legs par snang yang zin bris sogs nges tig ma 'byor la/ sku tshe sngon ma rnams su ganggA'i klung gi
rdul snyed las 'das pa'i zhing khams rgya mtshor mchog dman bar pa'i tshul sna tshogs pas 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa'i mtha' ga la rtogs/ 'on te skye ba rim brgyud dang thugs
rgyud gcig pa'i sprul pa sogs kyis bstan 'gro'i sman yon du gyur pa'i rim pa ni/ rje nyid kyi zhal gsungs mar/ na mo gu ru bhyaH rgyal ba sku dngos ayon chos kyi rje/
/rdo rje 'chang dbang kun dga' legs pa'i zhabs/ /sku drin mnyam med blo gsal rgya mtsho sogs/ /skyabs mchog bla ma rnams la gsol ba 'debs/ /ayon drung na lang 'gro dkon cog
'byung / /

dag dang ma dag skye ba 'ga' yi mthar/ /chos dbang gsung sprul padma dbang chen zhes/ /mkhas grub dam par gyur la gsol ba 'debs/ /rdzogs chen rnal 'byor 'od gsal rang grol
dang / /bka' brgyad bka' babs rdor 'chang bsod nams bzang / /'jam dbyangs sgeg pa bsod nams grub la sogs/ /dag pa'i skye bar gyur la gsol ba 'debs/ /rgyal bas lung bstan
zab gter bstan pa'i bdag /'brel tshad don ldan rgyal po'i bla mchod de/ /chos kyi rgyal po ratna gling pa zhes/ /khams gsum grags pas khyab la gsol ba 'debs/ /nyams rtogs
mthar phyin a seng rgyal mo dang / /'phags yul bram ze bhra ma nA tha nyid/ /gangs ri'i khrod 'dir rgyal po'i rigs su skyes/ /mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug nyid la gsol ba
'debs/ /nga yi sku gsung thugs dang yon tan dang / /'phrin las sprul ba shes rab snying rje can/ /rab byung rgyal chen rnal 'byor tshul can zhes/ /padmas lung bstan khyod
la gsol ba 'debs/ /rgyal sras gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug gis/ /yang srid gnyis su pha bu'i 'brel ba bzhag /da dung 'bral med rjes su 'dzin no zhes/ /byin rlabs lung bstan
thob la gsol ba 'debs/ /dgyes pa rdo rje 'khor lo sdom pa dang / /rdo rje phag mo sgrub chen bka' brgyad lha/ /'jam dpal khros pa 'joms byed 'bar ba yis/ /byin rlabs mtshan
ma thob la gsol ba 'debs/ /lha chen dpal 'bar lcam dral pho nyar bcas/ /gur gyi mgon po gnyan mgon rnam sras sogs/ /dam can

rgya mtsho phal cher bran du 'khol/ /'phrin las thog med sgrub la gsol ba 'debs/ /'di nas 'pho tshe byang phyogs lcang lo can/ /zhing der pha rgan drung du thog mar 'gro/ /de
nas ayon zangs mdog dpal ri'i rtser/ /skye ba'i rten 'brel bsgrig la gsol ba 'debs/ /de ltar khyed la gus pas gsol 'debs na/ /dus 'di nas bzung tshe rabs thams cad du/
/nam yang 'bral med mnyes pa kun bsgrubs nas/ /cham gcig gdod ma'i klong du grol bar shog /ces pa 'di snying nas dad ldan gnyos dka' bcu pa chos rgyan gyis bskul ba'i ngo
ma chogs par nged rang gi khong khrag shog bu'i logs la bkod pa yin pas/ thams cad la bstan na nged kyi tshe la gnod pas shin tu gsang zhing sbas pa'i tshul du mdzad pa
gal che che/ dam tshig la dgongs mdzod cing / dge slong chos rgyan la bstan kyang bzod/ tsha bo btsun chung rnams snod ldan yin kyang / na so gzhon pas gzhan la shor nyen
yod pa theng gcig la ma ston mdzod/ sa ma ya/ zhes pa dang shes rab rgya mtsho/ buddha/ sangs rgyas lhun grub/ sbyin pa dpal bzang / dkon mchog legs pa lngas zhus ngor
gnang ba'i kun khyab chos dbyings ma gnyis 'dug pa rgyas bsdus tsam du mthong bas gcig tu byas na sprul gzhi rgyal kun yab gcig 'jam dbyangs/ 'o skol gyi ston pa'i drung
du shes rab can gyi mchog shA ri'i bu/ lha sras khri srong lde'u btsan/ rdzu 'phrul gyis thog chen mda' ltar 'phen pa'i lang 'gro dkon mchog 'byung gnas/ mnga' bdag nyang
gi

sras zab gter chos kyi bang mdzod 'gro mgon nam mkha' dpal ldan zhes bla ma'i bka' babs shing thugs rje chen po dngos su 'grub pa/ gter kha 'og ma gu ru rin po che chos kyi
dbang phyug gi gdung las bla rdzogs thugs gsum gyi bka' babs pa rgyal sras padma dbang chen/ bdud 'joms skye ba rigs 'dzin chen po rgod kyi ldem phrus rjes su bzung zhing
sangs rgyas gnyis pa ayon chen po zhal gzigs nas gdams pa thob pa'i zur tsho rdor 'chang bsod nams bzang po zhes bka' brgyad kyi bka' babs pa/ 'di nyid kyi sku skye yin
tshul gter chen chos kyi rgyal po rigs 'dzin mnga' ris pa chen pos yang yang gsungs pas rdor 'chang pa yan khong rang gi rnam thar du gsungs pa la the mi tshom par ma zad
mnga' bdag yin pa'i khungs/ rigs 'dzin yongs 'dus kyi chos bdag lung bstan skabs su/ chos rgyal khyod sprul me tog ming 'dzin paH dngos las lhag pa'i skyes bu snying stobs
canaH bka' gter chos bdag bong ring lug sprel loH /rin cen phyag rten dgongs kyi dus su 'byung ཿ zhes shin tu gsal/ chos kyi rgyal po klong chen pa'i thugs sras 'od chen
go cha zhes snying tig gi bka' babs pas 'od gsal longs sku'i zhing khams myul zhing tshe dpag med kyis mngon sum du zhal gzigs pa/ mnga' bdag khri srong lde'u btsan gyi
thugs sprul kun mkhyen dol po pa shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis sbyor ba yan lag drug gi lam zab mos grol bar mdzad pa 'jam dbyangs sgeg pa nam mkha' dpal/ zab don gdams pas
yongs

grol bsod nams grub pa/ sras padma dbang chen gyi yang srid gter chen chos kyi rgyal po ratna gling pa'am gter gnas dang lung bstan gyi dbang gis 'gro 'dul gling pa dang zhig
po gling pa ste gter ston gcig la gling pa gsum du grags shing gter kha nyer brgyad zhal phye nas snga 'gyur bstan pa'i srog 'thud par mdzad pa po/ chos kyi rgyal po'i
rnam par sprul pa gha ta nA thas byin gyis brlabs nas drag sngags nus pa mchog tu brnyes shing auDDi ya na'i gnas su rdo rje phag mos dngos su rjes su bzung ba bhra ma nA
tha/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po'i rnam 'phrul 'jam dbyangs dkon cog bzang po'i zab don chos kyi nying khus 'od gsal pha mthar phyin pas thogs bcas kyi bdud las rgyal ba
a seng rgyal mo/ ratna gling pa dang bsod nams grub pa ma gtogs pa'i bzhi po dam pa 'ga'i lung bstan dang bstun/ btsun ma 'di byis pa'i dus wal gyis dran zhes gsol 'debs
kun khyab chos dbyings ma'i mjug na gsungs/ lang 'gro lo tsA ba ni/ las 'gro gling pa'i lung bstan du/ lang 'gro'i sprul pa bka' gter bdag po niH mkhyen brtse'i ming can
rig gnas lngar mkhas paH gtsang phyogs 'di nas 'khor gyi thog mar 'byung ཿ de la gdams pa gtad na bstan pa 'phelaH zhes gsal bar lung gis zin cing ratna gling pa ni lang
'gro'i skye bar yongs su grags/ bsod nams grub pa ni/ gong du gsol 'debs bris par gsal/ 'jam sgeg ni 'dar du zhal gtor chen gyi phyag len zhu ba gnang skabs tshar chen gyi
mnal lam du rje rdo ring pa

dang rdo rje gdan pa gnyis zhal sprod du bzhugs sar byon pa na rdo ring rin po ches chos rje pa kha sang nas gar byon gsungs pa jo nang 'jam sgeg ces par chos shod kyi bsdad
zhus pa'i tshe rdo rje gdan pas rdzun ma gsung gnas gsar chos rje yin gnang ba'i lan rje rdo ring pas gnyis ka mad khong yar klungs pa'i dus su 'jam sgeg da lta gnas gsar
chos rje yin/ zhes dang / gsung mgur du/ ayon thugs rje'i smon lam mthu btsan pas/ /rdo rje 'chang chen tshar pa chos kyi rjes/ /mi nas mir gyur skye ba lnga yi bar/ /rjes
bzung byang chub mchog gi sa bon bzhag /ces byung ba ltar tshar chen rnal 'byor dbang phyug yar klungs par 'khrungs pa'i tshe snyan brgyud kyi gdams pa gnang bar gsol
ba btab pas brag rdzong ma'i 'khrid yig tu skye ba gsum gyi gong nas gsol btab cing / /tshe 'dir longs spyod sgrub pas mnyes par byas/ /dad dang snying rje shes rab mi
dman la/ /kun spangs chos rje'i bstan la lhag par dad/ /ston dang bstan pa gzhan nas mi 'tshol bar/ /ci mdzad khyed shes mos gus lde mig gis/ /gsang chen thugs kyi bang mdzod
sgo phye nas/ /snyan brgyud yid bzhin nor bu kho bos rnyed/ /ces pa'ang 'jam sgeg /bhra ma nA tha/ a seng rgyal mo gsum rim par byung ba la dgongs la/ kun khyab chos
dbyings ma las/ bcu gsum skye bar mkhas dang grub pa dang / /zhu byed sgyur byed rig sngags 'chang ba'i tshul/ /du mar sprul nas sems can skyong mdzad pa/ /zhes pa'i bcu
gsum po ngos 'dzin tshul kha mtshon gcod dka' na'ang

'di bzhin yin nam snyam/ zhal gzigs sogs ngo mtshar ba'i mdzad pa rnams ni tshig gcig tsam yang rlung phyogs su ma grags par bsnyel tho phyag bris ma zhig snang ba'i kha yig
tu/ sprang btsun 'khyams po'i gsang ba'i gtam 'di dag /ji srid 'tsho yi bar du kha tham rgya/ /snying nas dad ldan re re tsam la bstan/ /des kyang snying gi dkyil du a
tham rgya/ /bla ma sangs rgyas dngos dang mjal ba dang / /man ngag rgyud sde'i snying po zab ches pas/ /snying rus med kyang bla ma'i sku drin gyis/ /rang la ngo mtshar yid
ches byung tshul yin/ /zhes kha byang btab nas tshas dang bcas rgya 'byar du zha lu shel tham gyi sgam mkhan po ma bzhugs par kha 'byed srol med 'dug pa der bcug pa de'i
ngang la bo dong du gzugs sku chos dbyings su bsdus pas rjes su mkhan po rtsis sprod kyi dus tham sgam nas byung bar lung med kyang rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan
gyis 'go mjug gi thugs rtsom 'ga' zhig mdzad par lung rgyun kyang 'dug la/ rnam thar 'di dpe rgyun dkon gshis rgyun mi nub par bya ba'i slad du gsung dri ma med pa yi ger
bkod pa ni/ na maHbadzra dhA ra dznyA na da ye shwa ra pA dA ya/ 'phags yul auDDi ya nar padma'i mtshan/ /byang phyogs bho Ta'i gnyen gyur khri srong zhabs/ /snyigs dus
rgyal ba'i rgyal tshab chos kyi rje/ /dbyer med mkhyen brtse'i zhabs pad gtsug na rgyal/ /de la 'dir lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten pa kun gyi gtsug gi nor bu/ snyigs dus
kyi 'gro ba ma lus pa thar pa'i gling du 'dren pa'i sa mkhan/ dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyi mkhyen brtse gcig tu bsdus pa'i spyi gzugs/ sras bcas rgyal ba'i yab

gcig /dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i rigs bdag /rig pa 'dzin pa dang mkhas dang grub pa yongs kyi ded dpon/ rdo rje 'dzin pa kun gyi ral ba'i khri la zhabs kyi padma ngal gso ba/
rje btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal ldan skal ba bzang po'i zhal snga nas de nyid kyi rnam par thar pa ni bsam gyis
mi khyab cing brjod kyis mi lang mod/ 'on kyang mdo tsam zhig brjod na/ rje de nyid kyi mdzad pa'i tshul che long tsam ni rnam thar chen mor rtogs par bya zhing / de bas
kyang ches snying por gyur pa'i gsang ba'i rtogs brjod/ gdul bya snod ldan dad pa dang dam tshig la gnas pa lhag bsam la nyes pa'i dri ma dang bral ba rnams kyi spyod yul/
log lta dang nga rgyal 'dzin pa kun gyi rna ba'i lam tsam du yang mi bsgrag pa'i gsang chen dpa' bo DA ki'i tshogs kyi zab pa bas ches gsang ba'i rnam par thar pa gsang
chen bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun zhes pa de la/ rje de nyid kyis/ sa khyi zla ba dang po'i tshes bcu'i nub rmi lam du/ nga'i mal sa'i 'khris na mgar mo gzhon nu ma zhig gcer bu
skra bshig nas 'dod pa bsten pa'i grabs su 'dug pa nga snying nas ngo tsha zhing 'di 'dra byed du mi nyan snyam nas de la 'ur/ nga rang 'bros pa'i grabs byas pas de tsug
ma byed 'di la skyon med/ khyod kyis yun ring po nas nga bos pa yin mod zer bas/ ngas ni khyod 'bod pa lta ci/ da lam las mthong yang ma myong / sdom pa nyams nas dmyal
bar skye ba las skyon che ba gar yod byas/ nga thong byas sprugs pas/ khyod la mi dgos na nga

'dod chags thams cad dang bral ba zhig yin zer nas nam mkhar 'phags song ba dang / rje btsun rdo rje phag mo zhal gnyis ma phag zhal gyi smin mtshams dang / bha ga'i nang na
dga' 'khyil 'khor ba zhig tu gyur song bas de'i zhabs la 'jus gsol ba btab pas/ da tshe 'dir rjes su 'dzin pa'i skal ba med/ yi ge so gnyis po 'bru 'bum sbyin sreg dang
bcas pa bzlos/ rang sems phag mo'i rang zhal ma yengs par skyongs/ snying rje byang sems kyis 'gro ba la phan thogs/ bar dor rjes su 'dzin no gsungs nas yal song / gnyid
sad pa na skyo snang drag po sngar yong ma myong ba zhig gda'a'o/ /me lug zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i nyer lnga'i nub rmi lam du/ o lo dge bsnyen dang blo gros bzang rogs la khrid
de rdza ri dkar po rtse mo rno ba rong nge ba zhig gi lde bas la phyin nas rgya gar nub phyogs la 'gro rgyu yin zer/ bsam 'grub yin snyam pa zhig gis rta sngon po sga
srab chab pa byas pa zhig gdong la khrid 'gro gi 'dug /ngas bltas pas ri'i logs thams cad la rdo dang bye ma rlung gis btab pa 'dra ba'i skya nyol nyol las grub pa'i yi
ge lAnytsha dang / dbu chen gyi dbyangs gsal dang / aShta dang / bde mchog gi rtsa sngags sogs hram me 'dug /ri gdong de nas mar babs pa'i steng kha zhig na/ dbus na rnam
rgyal mchod rten chen po zhig dang / mtshams bzhi na de'i phyed tsam gyi mchod rten re 'dug /nga'i yid la rje btsun rdo rje 'chang gi phyi rten yin pa la/ da lo khong tsho
dmag gis brel nas sku dkar yang ma gsol ba

'dug /nga bla ma mchod rten la re ba'i dus byung snyam nas mchi ma mang po shor/ skor ba du ma byas gsol 'debs brgya phrag mang po byas shing dad gus kyi lus brnags nas/ mchod
rten dbus ma de la 'jus nas bstan pa dang sems can spyi la phan pa'i smon lam mang po btab khyad par skye ba phyi ma sems can thams cad rje btsun rdo rje 'chang gi zhabs
drung du skye bar smon lam du nges par btab pas/ mchod rten lnga po g.yo zhing ldeg /dbus ma'i khebs gdugs ltar g.yas su 'khor ba las 'od li khri 'dra ba mang du 'phros
nas ngo mi shes pa'i lung pa mang po gang song / dril bu du ma 'dug pa rnams kyang skad snyan pa 'brug tsam sgrog /de'i gdangs las/ su zhig kha tsam ma yin dad pa yis/
/bla ma mchog la phyag 'tshal gsol 'debs pa/ /de ni myur du mngon par 'tshang rgya ste/ /rang nyid grol nas gzhan yang sgrol bar 'gyur/ /zhes thos pas phan yon 'di tsam
yod pa yin byas/ zla bo kun khrid nas skor ba gsol 'debs mang du byas/ ngas rta la zhon blo bzang gis bal dra po tis gang ba zhig khyer nas thur de la babs phyin pas/ nyang
stod rgyal khang yin snyam pa zhig tu slebs pa na/ sde pa nor bzang drung gis spos sna byas/ khang pa g.yabs sgor nyi ma bro ba zhig tu slebs a jo lags sku mched kyis
ja bur sogs kyi bkod pa yang bshams byung / a jo chos kyi zhal nas khyod gang la 'gro rgyu sogs dris byung ba la lo rgyus rnams zhib tu zhus pas/ khong tsho'i zhal nas/ rgya
gar nub

phyogs na 'dul zhing legs po yod pa dang chos ha cang mi dar bas der phyin na phan pa rgya che na'ang / da lam la phar la ma 'byon/ lo kha yar zhig 'di tshor bzhugs la/ chos
bka' nub nye ba 'di pa gsos phan sems rgya bskyed nas gzhan la chos mang du shod/ 'di skad byas na rang gzhan kun la phan phyir dpe cha med pa kun bris/ yod pa kun ltos/
chos thob pa thams cad bed med la ma bzhag /chos bka' dam po byed zer/ nor med pa la mi ster ba dang chos la dpe mkhyud byed mi nyan pas/ sems bskyed rgya chen pos kun
nas blangs pa'i chos nyan pa dang / dpe gzhan la spel ba dang / de'i don rang rgyud la sbyor ba rnams mdzod la/ rim gyis rgya gar nub phyogs su byon/ nged spun gsum yang
khyed gar 'byon sar yong ba yin gsung pa la/ de skad zhu ste/ chos nyan sa yang mi rnyed/ rnyed na yang zhu sa yang mi yong / ngas chos bshad kyang nyan mkhan ni mi yong
ste/ da lam thabs mi gda' bas sdod lags zhus pas/ rta rdzi ngo nag thing byas rta dang bcas pa nub phyogs phar la 'ur sgra dang bcas nas 'phur song ba dang gnyid sad pa mnyam
du byung ngo / /sa sprel zla ba dang po nas rkang pa'i nad de langs nas/ re mig la zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes bzhi la 'gro smon can du phyin/ gcod bka' ma dang gsang ba
rmad byung sbrags nas nyams len gang lcogs byas pas zhag gcig nas rkang pa nas 'drud pa dang khyi nag pos rmugs pa sogs bsdigs ri dang / bud med mdzes ma sngar ma mthong
ba'i byad bzhin dang / gos rgyan phun sum tshogs pas

bslu brid byed pa sogs lhongs tshad bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung na'ang / phung po'i gces 'dzin btang nas nyal bsdad pas/ zhag gsum song ba na nyams snang la bud med byad dmar
byang nge ba bong che zhing skra dmar ba zhig phyag 'tshal zhing / mAthaThArgAnatAshaH zhes pa'i srog snying 'bul ba snyam byed par dam la btags/ tshes bcu'i tho rengs
dge sbyor rnams byed 'phro la gnyid du song ba'i rmi lam du/ g.yabs lho yin snyam pa zhig na dar sman tse'i yol ba rgya che bar btang 'dug pa'i nang na/ sprul sku grang
so gter ston chen po lcam sngon sdud ma zhig bsnams/ rdo rje dril bu gsil zhing bzhugs 'dug /phyag 'tshal nas 'dir phebs pa yin nam zhus pas/ drung pa 'og gdon gyis zhabs
bsnyel gyi 'dug zer phyag rdor gyi dbang zhig 'bul du yongs pa lags/ sgrub mchod bdag 'jug dang bcas pa tshar bdog /da gsan pas chog pa bdog gsungs/ phyag rdor che ba brgyad
skor gang lags zhus pas/ u tsa drag sngags kyis che ba'i dbang yin gsung / sku gzhogs g.yas na u tsa lha bcu dgu pa'i dkyil 'khor zhig bkram/ mar me chen po mang po
spar/ sku mdun na lcog tse'i kha na/ rdo rje dril bu/ bum pa/ cod pan/ mchod rten sngon po mtho gang ba zhig dang / phyag rdor gyi sku shel 'dra ba zhig dang / gzhan yang
phyag mtshan gyi bye brag mang po 'dug /g.yon na rdul tshon gyi gzhal yas khang mtshan nyid tshang ba zhig gi dbus na/ padma phyogs mdog 'dab bzhi'i lte ba la khyung dkar
po gzi brjid 'bar ba/ gshog pa sngon po rdo rje'i rang bzhin me 'od 'phro ba/ g.yas rdo rje 'phyar zhing g.yon

sbrul nag po'i mgo bo za ba'i rked pa nas bzung ba/ 'dab ma shar na sbrul dkar po gnyis/ lho na ser po/ nub na dmar po/ byang na ljang gu gnyis rnams kyi mjug ma bsnol nas
gdan du byas pa/ rked pa yan langs nas khyung gi pus mo'i thad tsam na gdeng ka byas pa zhig 'dug /'di gang yin zhus pas rdo rje mchu'i dkyil 'khor yin gsungs nas/ phyag
rdor la dbang bzhi rdzogs shig dang / rdo rje mchu la rjes gnang rgyas pa zhig gnang ba'i mthar/ 'di rnams kyang khyed la mkho ba yin gsung nas po ti glegs shing med pa mang
du gtad byung / de rnams bdag gis pang du bzhag pas mgo bo dang mnyam por song / res nga rang dpe char 'gro/ res dpe cha rnams nga'i lus su 'gyur/ res nga'i rgyab mdun
du glegs shing bzhag nas skud pas sdom pa rnams byed pa byung ba dang gnyid sad do/ /tshes bcu bzhi'i nam langs khar gnyid du song ba na/ dpon sa tshe dbang pa yin snyam
pa'i bud med dkar dmar mdzes pa zhig gis chang thod pa gang sbyin pa 'thung gi yod tsa na/ blo gros bzang gis skyes pa slog pa gyon pa zhig khrid nas 'di la thod 'phreng
legs po yod pas mjal ba zhu zer/ ston dang byas pas thod 'phreng byu ru ltar dmar ba brgya rtsa gcig bstan nas 'di kha che paN chen gyi 'phreng ba yin zer/ nga la gnang
dgos byas pas lag tu sprad byung tsa na thod pa legs pa khyid gang tsam la 'khor lo sdom pa zhal bzhi phyag bcu gnyis pa yum dang bcas pa'i sku me long la gzugs brnyan shar
ba lta bu zhig gsal bar mthong ba dang gnyid sad do/ /athi-i/ snga mo zhig

rnying ma'i gshed dmar la thugs dam byas na tshe la phan zer ba byung ste zhuu sa ma rnyed/ myug tu sleb nas btsal bas nyi sbug pa la bzhugs zer/ bya lo zla ba lnga pa'i nang
du nyi sbug la 'gro khar/ shangs chu che drags thar sa mi 'dug zer nas bshel ba'i nub rmi lam du lung pa kha lho bstan ri skya hrob se ba zhig gi ldebs rab gsal nyis brtsegs
yod pa'i khang pa zhig na bla ma 'ber mo byin chags shig gi drung na nga 'dug pa na bla ma de'i 'khris na o lo nor bzang pa yin snyam pa zhig gi phyag na rag gi 'phreng
ba rnying pa zhig bzung nas 'di a jo lags rang gi thugs dam dang thog ma nas yin pas/ da dung mdzad na khe che ba 'dug ste the tshom las mi 'dug /deng sang ma bzung
na de nas mi yong zer ba rmis pa nas/ sang de ga chu la ma 'dzems par phyin pas khang pa sogs rmi lam sor bzhag gda'/ gshed dmar nag gi dbang lung rags pa thob/ dbang ma
thob pa zhig gshed dmar gyi rdul tshon gyi drung du btang bas sna khrag dar 'phyar 'phyar byed/ shin tu gnyan la byin rlabs che bar go lags/ de res zhag bcu bsdad/ dbon
po des chos gnang ba'i spyan tshab mi nus par gegs chen po byas/ rin po che'i zhal ta la mdang zhag mnos pa bzhin 'bul mi thub pa 'dug pas phyir byon/ khong tsho me tog la
song shul lta bu 'gol ba zhig la nga rang gis gang thos 'di tshang ma zhig 'bul thub nges byed do gsungs/ zla ba bdun pa'i nang du rmi lam la lho steng gi khang thog yin
snyam pa zhig na/ rin po che'i nyi sbug pa zhal nub gzigs byas bzhugs pa'i drung na bdag 'dug pa la/ gshed dmar gyi skor po ti gcig gi lung rdzogs

par gnang / dpe ris tshon rdzogs byas pa'i legs po mang po bstan nas mdzub khrid mdzad/ khyad par thod pa zhal dbye dang ru mtshon la zhi rgyas mang po gnang ba zhig rmis/
gnyid sad nas kyang shin tu gsal ba 'dug pas zin bris byas na thub nges 'dug ste/ dga' mo zhig thos pa'i ltas yin snyam pa las ma byung bas yi ger ma btab/ de nas me tog
ran pa dang phar 'gro rtsis kyis skor yang la btab ba dang pha gi nas zhi bar gshegs pa'i gsang brtol gyi mi gnang ba lam du 'phrad log byung / bar do ye shes kyi skus rjes
su bzung bar gda' bas bka' drin che/ chu phag sa ga zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi'i nyi ma dros chen tsam la lam zab kyi de kho na nyid la blo bzhag pa'i ngang la gnyid du song
ba na nang thams cad 'od dmar ser li khri 'dra ba zhig gis khengs nas phyi nang thams cad gsal ba'i khrod nas 'ja' tshon kha dog lnga ldan las grub pa'i yi ge dbu chen
mtho re tsam byas pa'i rje sa skya pa chen po'i rnam thar ding sang yongs grags rnams las ches zhib pa zhig yig 'phreng du yod pa so so'i sgra sgrog pa zhig 'dug /de la
dad gus byas tshig rnams sgrogs/ sgra de'ang snyan bzhin pa'i ngang nas sa skya pa chen po'i zhal ras gdong dkyus ring po la sha dkar la snum pa zhal chen po 'dzum bag can
ga ther byas pa zhig yod de snyam mig sngar lam lam yod pa la/ dad gus kyi mchi ma 'chor ba zhig gi ngang nas gnyid sad do/ /chu phag zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bcu'i tho
rengs rmi lam du bo dong rdzong gi nyi 'od 'khyil pa yin snyam pa zhig na a pha lags drung na bza' ring 'gag dkar po gsar pa zhig gi steng na ras sngon

por 'od dang 'phro bzhi'i sku gzan bzhes raka sha'i 'phreng ba zhig bsnams nas bzhugs 'dug pa'i drung du slebs/ snga phyi'i lo rgyus mang po zhus pa'i mthar bdag 'tsham por
gnas khyed gar thegs da nged tsho ci tsug byed zer zhing mchi ma gtong gin zhus pas ma bshum khyed tsho a pha rkyen gyis shi bar byed kyi gda' ste de 'dra min/ sku tshe
rdzogs nas lo lnga song ste sngags kyi dam bca' zhig ma thems pas bsdad pa yin pas de thug bsdad pa'ang ya mtshan che/ da lam a pha lcang lo can du slebs gsang ba'i bdag
po la theg pa chen po'i chos kyi dga' ston rgyun chad med par myong nas myur du 'tshang rgya bar yod/ khyed rang yang lcang lo can du skyes nas sems can du ma'i don byed
par 'gyur/ de'i slad du dge sbyor 'di gyis gsungs nas nam mkha' la je mthor 'od cig la bzhud song bas drung lags zer 'bod 'phro la gnyid sad do/ /lo de'i zla ba drug pa'i
nyer gsum nas rje btsun rdo rje 'chang gi dus chen sgrub mchod btsugs pa'i tshe/ bug sgo'i nang na nged gnyis las med/ thig sus kyang slob ma myong / phyi nas 'bod kyang
ma bde bar gang drag ci drag la song skabs/ thig kyang mi shes pa'i rdo rje slob dpon du khas len pa'i blun po snying kham can nga 'dra snyam dus/ gsol ba btab pas thig
rtsa zhig blo la lam lam byed nas brgyab pas thig shin tu legs/ de'i dkyil 'khor des mar me bzung / zhag bcu gsum bzhag kyang rdul ye ma blangs so/ /zla ba bdun pa'i tshes
brgyad nas zhing gshegs kyi dus mchod la/ 'khor lo chen po'i sgrub mchod sbyin sreg dang bcas pa byed kyin yod dus/ sbyin sreg gi skabs na dogs pa 'dra

yod tsa na rmi lam du/ nga sbyin sreg cig byed kyi 'dug pa la/ de'i pha tshad na rdo rje 'chang chen po dang drung lags gnyis bzhugs nas 'khor chen la sbyin sreg gi yi ge mang
po yod de/ gnyags snying po rgyal mtshan gyis 'di la thugs gtsigs che/ 'di'i skabs su phyag len 'di bzhin mdzad gsungs nas/ 'grig shin tu zhib par gsungs/ dpe cha de'ang
gda' ba 'di khrod na gda' gsungs nas bstan/ de nas drung lags kyis zhu mkhan mdzad nas 'khor chen gyi skor la dka' gnad mang po la bshad pa mdzad pa'i sgang la gnyid
sad pa/ bla ma yab sras gnyis kyi zhal mig sngar lam me ba'i ngang nas tshig de dag kyang blo la gsal por 'dug /sang nyin mdang phyag mdzub btsugs pa'i dpe hrul bral brul
bsdus pa'i po ti de bltas pas sbyin sreg gi dpe cha yang 'dug cing / ji skad gsungs pa bzhin 'dug go /byi lo zla ba dang po'i nyer lnga la sding ma nas 'khor gdong du gtor
ma'i rgyab na bkram pa'i gur me tog ma'i zhal khebs 'od 'bar ba dang bcas pa ja sbyor gcig gi bar lam me 'dug gral grol rjes na zhal khebs sang rtsas khang de bkab 'dug
pas mig 'khrul pa'am ya mtshan can zhig gda'a'o/ /lcags phag zla ba lnga pa'i nang du rmi lam du/ mnga' ris sprul sku dang mjal dpe cha gnang bdog gam zhus pas/ na ning
khyed rang gis bltas pa de nas shog ldebs gnyis las ni ma bris/ dpe chung de gnyis bskur yod gsungs/ spa sgam zhig nas zhi khro'i dpe cha yin snyam pa'i dpe chung zhig nga
la gnang byung bas/ 'di thams cad la ngom dgos snyam dga' tshor tshad med pa'i ngang nas

gnyid sad/ sang phyag dam dpe cha phebs pas de ga sor bzhag 'dug go /yang nub cig a lhun pa yin snyam pa zhig gis sprul skus skyel du btang pa yin zer rag bum mgul chings dar
dkar nog po zhig gis byas/ kha rgyan rma bya dang / shel gyis byas pa zhig dang / po ti bru le dkon rtsos gril ba sprad pa rmis pas sang bka' 'dus kyi phyag dpe slebs
nam la bris pa'i sgang la/ rmi lam du sprul sku byon nas rigs 'dzin gdung sgrub kyi dbang gnang ba byung ngo / /shing glang zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes bcu bdun nas bka' brgyad
sgrub chen sman sgrub dang bcas pa mdzad dus bka' brgyad kyi dkyil 'khor gsum gyi thig 'debs shing / nam mkha' la'ang dkyil 'khor gyi thig rdzogs pa zhig skya ta le 'dug
pa rmis/ yang nub cig nub phyogs kyi nam mkha' la mnga' ris paN chen bzhugs nas/ stong pa stong pa stong gsal 'dzin med yin gsungs nas li ser po'i za ma tog nor bu mig
gsum pa'i dbyibs can zhig bdag la gnang byung ba dang gnyid sad do/ /nub gcig bka' brgyad kyi dpal dgu thog tshad tsam 'od 'bar ba'i mdun na sprul sku bzhugs nas bka' brgyad
kyi rgyud lung man ngag thams cad 'dir 'dus shing khyod rang bdag po yin pas ye gsung po ti gcig nga la gnang byung ngo / /stag lo chos lung sgang gi khang chung der
mtshams dam po'i khong nas dpon sa nam mkha'i drung sogs kha cig la ro snyoms sgang 'dril bug chos byas bshad pa'i grol kha tshes bzhi'i snga dro rmi lam du/ gcung rin po
che sku gzi 'od shin tu 'bar zhing / na bza' kong gzan dur kha zhig bzhes/ 'khor mang chen dang bcas

phyogs la thegs rgyu ba'i rnam pas/ rdzong zhig gi brgya sgo'i phyir phebs kyi 'dug pa'i thegs skyel la phyin phyag 'bul byang bas phyag len mdzad rjes mgul phrag nas zhwa
dmar legs tshad thub yug cig gnang byung nas da 'phrin las yang 'di che ba yong ba 'dug pas da phyis dbu zhwa 'di bzhes las 'gro don mdzad pa zhu gsung ba dang gnyid sad/
zhal ras gsal drags mchi ma mang po shor/ dang po sgom zhwa gon gsung gnang skabs rten 'brel 'phyugs dogs mi mang sa la mang por gyon/ phyis su grol cha zhig zhu snyam pa
ma grub pa'i ngang nas zhing brjes/ da ci drag snyam sems ma bde ba'i ngang la yod pa bla ma thugs rje che bas grol cha gnang bar 'dug bsam mos gus bgyis so/ /na mo gu
ru shrI badzra bhai ra wA ya/ bdag dang po nas dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed la dad po zhig yod do/ /man ngag ma thob pas dge sbyor byed lugs ji lta ba ni ma byung 'dug /myug tu
sleb 'phral bcu gsum ma'i thog nas ya ma rA dza 'bum phrag gcig bzlas pa'i tshe nub cig /rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po zhal phyag yongs rdzogs mi tsam zhig gsal lam ste mthong
ma thag gnyid sad/ sa rta zla ba dgu pa'i nang du/ bla chen rin po che'i drung du gsung chos zhu yin rgya che na yod pa'i nub cig rmi lam du/ bo dong bla brang dkar
po'i tshoms chen gyi dbus na bzhugs gdan shin tu mtho ba zhig la/ lo chen byang rtse yin zhu ba'i sku'i rnam pa da lta bris yod pa'i sku 'dra 'di rnams sor bzhag la/ gos
bem dmar smug nyis brtsegs bzhes pa shin tu gzi brjid che ba zhig dang / de'i sku gzhogs g.yon na bla chen chos dpal bzang po yin zhu

ba zhig bzhugs/ gzhan gral ba mang po byas pa zhig gi drung na bdag 'dug pa na/ lo chen rin po che bdag la ched du gzigs shing / bla chen pa'i rnam thar bsngags brjod mang
po gsungs/ de nas lo chen dang yang yang mjal ba dka' snyam rje bla ma dam pa'i rnam thar lo chen rang gis mdzad pa de'i lung zhig gnang dgos zhus pas shin tu legs de ga
bya yis gsung / gcig la phyag dpe khyer shog gsungs/ len du song ba ma sleb pa la gnyid sad/ sems 'phrang ba'i tshad thub pa zhig byung / bla chen rin po che bla chen chos
rin pa'i skye ba yin 'dug pas de'i byin rlabs yin nam snyam/ lcags sprel zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes gcig nas gzhi bsnyen gyi sngon 'gro bla ma'i rnal 'byor tshugs pa'i tshes
bzhi'i nub rmi lam du/ rje btsun rdo rje 'chang pha tshar pa rje dang mjal/ rta mgrin yang gsang gi dbang rdzogs par gnang / dkyil 'khor gtor ma dbang tshig sogs kyang
shin tu gsal ba dang / phyag len la dogs gcod 'dra zhu rgyu yod pa'ang zhus shing / lan gnang ba zhig byung ngo / /nub cig yang pha bla ma bzhugs khri thog rtsar snyogs
pa zhig gi steng na ber thul nel tsho gsar pa rang zhig bzhes nas bzhugs pa'i sku gzhogs g.yon na bdag 'dug pa la/ a skyabs kyis gsol ja zhus rjes gsol kha zhu yi 'dug pas/
nga'i de khong la drongs gsungs/ gsol kha de bdag la drangs pa zhig rmis/ yang nub cig dbu rtse 'og 'dra ba zhig na khri sngar gyi de las mtho ba zhig la bzhugs nas tshe
khrid kyi tshar chos de gsung rgyu yin snyam pa byas/ bdag sku mdun na 'dug pa la gsung chos ha cang gsal ba ni ma byung / rlung bum

can bzung spyan lta stangs mdzad ha re bzhugs pa gsal po zhig rmis/ yang nub cig bo dong rdzong du bde ba can yin snyam pa zhig na bzhugs gdan mthon po zhig la rdo rje 'chang
sgo rum pa chen po bzhugs/ de'i sku gzhogs g.yon na bdag /bdag gi g.yon na rje btsun dbon bzhugs pa la rin po ches gzh-i len cig mdzad rgyu ba'i ston shom bzang po byas
pa zhig rmis/ nub cig dpal sbug bzhugs khri'i steng na pha bla ma bzhugs gsung ngag rin po che bskyar nas gnang rgyu yin zer zhu mkhan mang po 'tshogs 'dug pa la bslab
gsum pa gsal po 'dug gzhan ngo shes rang ni mi 'dug /khog phub yin snyam pa'i dpe cha shig gi lung mdzad byung ba na/ thod phu'i blo gsal rgya mtsho de/ birWa pa lags sam
zer ba zhig 'dug pa la/ don 'di ga yin te tshig 'di cung sdeb ma shes 'dug gsung / bdag gis thod phu'i rnal 'byor dbang phyug de/ da lta'i blo gsal rgya mtsho yin byas na
bde ba 'dra zhus pas de ga bris pas yong gsungs/ de nas gzhung bshad cig kyang 'go btsugs/ snang gsum kyang btsugs byung nas na ning gi zin bris de la zhu dag byed dgos
snyam pa dang gnyid sad/ bsams pas thod phur byon pa'i rje gha ya dha ra rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi thugs kyi sprul par mnal lam bka' rgya ma nas bshad/ de dang pha bla ma
thugs rgyud gcig pa'i brda' ru 'dug snyam pa byung ngo / /aShta 'bum phrag gsum song ba'i nyi ma shar lhod bzlas pa'i sgang la/ gnyid du cung zad song ba na mdun gyi nam
mkha' la dpal kye rdo rje zhal brgyad phyag bcu drug pa yab yum gnyis ka sku mdog g.yu drug dkar gyi mdog

lta bu dang gsal rnyog med 'od kyi rang bzhin zhig ja dkar yol gang lhod byas 'thung ba'i yun tsam gyi bar la 'dzin med kyi ngang la cham me ba nas mthong / de nas tshogs pa
mang pos phun tshogs 'dod dgu ma 'ur ding gis gyer byung ba'i skad kyis gnyid sad kyang sems bde cham me 'dug go /yang gtum chen gyi mngon dkyil bsgrig pa'i sgang la rmi
lam du pha rdo rje 'chang tshar pa dang mjal nas/ gtum chen gyi dbang rdzogs par gnang / shes rab ye shes bla med spyi dang 'dra ba dang dbang bzhi pa'i skabs su bla ma
rdo rje 'chang gi rnam pa spyi bor gsal btab nas slob ma la bstim/ de dang rang sems 'dres pa'i gnas lugs la ngo sprod mdzad/ de tsam ma gtogs dkyil chog sor bzhag mdzad/
gtang rag gi maNDal tshun tshar nas brgyud pa zhus pas ngas ni rdo ring rin po che la thob/ des mkhyen rab rin po che la gsan pa yin nam gsung / de nas gnyid sad/ yang
nub cig sku ni ma mthong / rje btsun bsod nams dpal ba'i gsung yin snyam pa'i skad gog ge ba zhig gi gtum chen 'di sri'u chung pa'i pha chos thun mong ma yin pa zhig yin
te/ rnam par nyams shing 'thor bar gyur/ 'di khyod kyi legs par bsos shig /ngas byin gyis brlabs kyi gsung ba gsal bar thos/ yang nub cig sprul sku dbang phyug rdo rje yin
gsung pa'i sngags pa zhal ras dmar cham me ba la/ dbu skra sil bu ring shag dkar po dang lcam smug sdud ma bzhes pa zhig dang mjal nas zhib rgyas mang du gsungs/ gtum chen
la gnang ba rgyas par mdzad pa

zhig byung ba rang don med par bstan par bsam pa'i byin rlabs yin nam snyam/ rin po che rong pa'i drung du 'joms byed kyi dbang zhus pa'i dus/ rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gyi
dbus na bcom ldan 'das 'joms byed 'bar ba sku mdog mu men dwangs pa'i mdog lta bu rtsa zhal khrag skam pa 'dra ba'i smug po zhal gsum phyag drug phyag mtshan sogs gam la
cher ma zin/ sku khru gang tsam gsal zhing dwangs la rnyog pa med pa zhig /mig phye ba nas bzung ste/ bum dbang ma rdzogs par mig phye btsum med par dngos su gsal ler mthong
/ de dus sku dang rtsa zhal kha dog so so ba de gang yin nam snyam mod/ de nas yun ring po song nas lce blo ldan seng ge'i thugs dam bris sku mthong ba la'ang kha dog
de ga 'dug cing / 'phrin las kyi tshig gi go ba myangs na de kho na dgos rgyur 'dug pas yid ches rnyed/ rje btsun rong pa'i zhabs de lce'i gdung 'khrul med spyir byin
rlabs che zhing / sgos lha 'di la mnga' brnyes pas de kho na'i byin rlabs su gda'a'o/ /phyi lo myug chos sde'i 'du khang du mnga' ris rigs 'dzin chen po'i phyag phyi byas
bka' brgyad gsang ba yongs rdzogs kyi sgrub chen mdzad dus nyin gcig skor ba byed 'phro la ngal nas snyel byas bsdad pas/ gnyid du hrib tsam song ba na rigs 'dzin chen po/
phebs nas ayon padma'i bka' lung la tshe chu 'di khol zhing 'dug pas dngos grub len ran gsung gi 'dug /da lta tshe dbang byed gsung ma thag gnyid sad/ skor ba la phyin
pas mchod dpon byon nas de ring bka' dbang zhig yod pas zhal ngo tsho gdan 'dren

thong gsung / de 'phral bka' brgyad bde gshegs 'dus pa'i zhi ba'i tshe dbang gnang byung ngo / /yang sgrub dbang chen mo'i chu dbang gi skabs su pha rigs 'dzin chen pos bum
pa thogs nas 'dur dbyangs dang bcas/ bum pa mgo la bzhag pa'i tshe lus sbrid cing shes pa kyi bun pa'i zil chen po zhig byung skabs/ lho nub kyi nam mkha' na tshur gu ru
chos kyi dbang phyug sngags pa sgang yol dbu skra'i thor cog dar dmar pos bcings pa/ sku shag sham thabs dkar po'i steng na tshem ge sngo sang bzhes pa mgul la me long 'od
lam me btags pa zhig phyag na bum pa thogs te/ 'dzum ye re re byon byung nas bum pa'i spyi bor bzhag /nga'i lo tshad kyi steng du lo brgyad bsnan pa'i tshe thub par 'gyur/
mi nyams pa'i slad dang sems can mang po'i don la lo re bzhin 'di lta bu'i sgrub pa chen po ma chag pa gyis shig gsungs nas 'od du yal song / re zhig rtog med du cham
me lus 'dug /sad pa na mchi ma bun pa zhig byung / 'di nas bzung ste nam gsol ba btab res kyis nyams kyi snang ba la mjal byung ba yang pha rigs 'dzin chen po kho na'i
thugs rjer gda'o/ /oM AHhU~M badzra gu ru padma siddhi hUM/ phag lo zab lung du sku 'dra'i sgo drung du zhag bdun mtshams byas nas bla ma bka' 'dus kyi spyi'i bsnyen par
byas pa'i dus/ de bar la ni rmi lam brda 'dra mo tshe 'di'i legs nyes ston pa shas che bar byung / zab lung nas lam zhag gnyis byas g.yang du bsdad pa'i tho rangs mdun gyi
nam mkha' la ayon rin po che'i sku byis pa lo brgyad pa'i tshod tsam sku mdog mi sha kha dmar mdangs che ba/ spyan gnyis shin tu zlum pa ha re gzigs

pa/ phod ka mthing kha/ chos gos dmar po/ padma mthong grol dmar po gsol ba/ sku lcam kha thi smug khra 'dra ba'i padma ldum ris khra chil le ba bzhes pa phyag mtshan spyi
dang 'dra ba zhig gsal bar mthong nas/ de'i zhabs kyi thad tsam du mgo btsugs nas/ nyi ma lta bur ma rig mun pa sel/ /zla ba lta bur nyon mongs gdung ba sel/ /dug gsum nad
sel sangs rgyas sman gyi bla/ /baiDUrYa yi 'od la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zer ba 'di kha nas ston ma thag gnyid sad/ de nas bzung ste tshe 'di'i bya byed 'du 'god thams cad bun
long nge ba 'a'i nam 'chi'am/ byang chub cig ma bsgrub na nam mi 'dug snyam pa'i dung dung ma gtogs blo rgya ye med la/ chags zhen 'jigs skrag ci yang med pa'i zi chod
de ba zhig rgyun du byung ba de/ rin po che la bdag chen gyis ngan byas pa la zhe sdang drag po skyes ma thag gnyid sad pa bzhin yal song / phyi lo bo dong kun ra rnying
mar skye bdun bsgrubs tshe zhal ngo rnams la 'khor ba dong sprug gi lam dbang phul ba'i spyan 'dren gyi tshe/ 'ja' 'od 'khyil pa'i klong na ayon rin po che sngar mthong
ba ltar dang / de'i g.yas na gu ru rin po che chos dbang babs dang mo'i de ga la/ phod ka'i steng na chos gos li khri'i mdog 'dra ba zhig bzhes/ phyag na bum pa bsnams/ g.yon
na pha mnga' ris gter ston da lta'i dbyibs ji lta ba mdun gyi smad tsam na rgya mtsho dge slong ba de me tog dmar po zhig thogs pa rnams ye re re byon byung nas mdun
gyi nam mkha' la 'od bung nge bzhugs/ gu ru chos dbang gi phyag gi bum pa nas bdud rtsi 'o ma 'dra ba re skya

nar nar zhal ngo thams cad kyi dbu gtsug nas blug /dbang gi spro bsdu'i skabs su yang mdun na bzhugs pa de rnams kyi gnas gsum gyi 'od rang gzhan kun la thim pa'i snang ba
dang bcas dbang de ma grol ring nyams kyi snang ba la gsal 'grib med par mthong / de skabs khrom thams cad dad pa 'ur langs/ sa 'phags gnam 'phags la song / zhal ngo 'dra
la de gong du 'chi bltas 'dra gsal bar 'dug pa de nub nas grol byin rlabs yid ches par byung ngo / /de skabs ngan song kun skyob kyi dbang byas pa'i tshe yang babs snga
ma sor bzhag la rgyab na rdo rje gling pa lo chab spel ba'i steng na pad zhwa sngon po bzhes pa/ phod ka sngon po byas pa'i skam seng ba phyag na thod pa bsnams pa zhig bzhugs
'dug pa nyams snang la gsal bar dbang ma grol bar du byung / lcags mo glang lo bde gzar nyen che la nyams dma' ba'i sgang la/ bo dong tshoms chen du dbon rin po che
la gdan bzhugs kyi rgyab chog thugs sgrub kyi las byang bgyis pa'i spyan 'dren gyi skabs su/ drin can ayon chen po sngar kho na 'dra ba zhig gi zhal nas/ 'di 'dra rang gi
sred pa yang byed mi dgos gsungs nas yud kyis yal song / nyams dga' la shes pa 'ur ba zhig byung / de skabs mgon po g.yul bzlog byas pa'i byang shar gyi gyer gyi skabs
su/ sngags srung e ka dza tI sku mdog smug nag ral pa g.yu drug dmar 'dra ba gcig skyes nam mkha'i mthongs su bun ne ba/ dpral bar spyan gcig ong kong ltar dmar bung nge
ba/ rma bya'i sgro thul khra bun bun gyi gseb nas me dmar lhab lhab yod pa/ g.yas snying za zhing

g.yon spyang ki 'gyed pa thog tshad tsam zhig phyer ma grol bar dngos su mthong / de skabs gza' bdud chen po babs sngar yong ba de ga sor bzhag la mig thams cad ong kong btang
ba tsam dmar hur re ba/ kha dgu car mi re khur nas khyu ru ru za ba zhig lan kha re mthong / 'di yan rje nyid rang gi phyag bris dngos las bshus pa yin cing / de man
kha bskang ba yin/ yang skabs shig byang phyogs nas rbod gtong gi ltas shig gis mnal lam du mi mang pos phyag zhabs nas bteg nas mtsho chen po zhig la bskyur grabs byas pa
na/ rje nyid kyi zhabs gnyis kyi bar du mtsho bcug nas ting nge 'dzin la bzhugs pa'i tshe/ dpal mgon chen po zhal bzhi yongs rdzogs gzigs nas rbod gtong kyang rang sa la
zhi/ yang skabs shig thugs nyams la myug yin dgongs pa'i lung pa 'phra shur ba zhig na mar khrag gi chu rgyun chen po 'bab pa nam mkha' nas dmag zor re ma tI zhes pa'i
sgra byung ba la brten/ khrag gi rba klong 'tshub pa'i khrod nas khro mo khrag gi ral pa can 'jigs su rung ba sku rked yan 'thon pa zhig gzigs gsung / stag lo tshar chen
chos kyi rgyal po sku mya ngan las 'das pa'i tshul bstan tshe/ rje nyid kyi gzigs snang du mdun gyi nam mkha' la dbus su rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho/ g.yas su sprul
sku shAkya thub pa/ g.yon du ayon chos kyi rgyal po rnams dngos su gzigs gsung / yos lo zha lur ma he mchod pa la phebs skabs/ las kyi gshin rje yab yum gyi zhal 'bag la
bka' bsgo gnang ba'i tshe las kyi gshin

rje yab yum mdog kham nag shin tu 'jigs pa spel dkar dang mnyam pa zhig la dngos su bka' bsgo gnang gsung / rje nyid zhing 'di'i mdzad pa legs par mthar phyin nas gzugs kyi
sku'i bkod pa chos kyi dbyings su bsdu ba'i tshul ston par mdzad tshe/ mdun gyi nam mkha' la ayon chos kyi rgyal po/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' legs pa/ rje btsun blo gsal
rgya mtsho/ sprul sku bdud 'joms rdo rje/ gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug rnams phebs byung gsung ba dang / de skabs su drung na bzhugs pa'i phyag phyi rnams la khyed rnams kyis
nyi ma 'di kha dog ji 'dra zhig tu mthong / ngas ni nyi 'od thams cad 'od gzer kha dog sna lngar 'dug gsungs/ de ci lags zhus pas/ sbyor drug bsgoms pa'i yon tan rnam
kun mchog ldan gyi stong gzugs shar bar 'dug gsungs/ yang mkha' 'gro ma kha dog sna lnga so so'i sku mdog dang mthun pa'i seng ge la chibs pa rigs lnga dngos su byon nas
spyan 'dren par brtsams pa na/ de nyin bu slob rnams kyis brtan bzhugs phul nas bzhugs gsol btab pa na mkha' 'gro rnams kyang slog yod gsungs nas zhag bdun bar bzhugs pa'i
mthar/ 'brug lo zla ba lnga pa'i nyer gcig gi mkha' 'gro 'du ba'i dus kyi cha la/ gong du brjod pa'i bla ma rnams dang yi dam zhi khro rab 'byams kyi lha tshogs mngon sum
du byon/ dpa' bo dang DA ki'i tshogs kyis gdugs dang rgyal mtshan la sogs pa mchod pa'i tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang bcas pas spyan drangs/ lha

dang rig pa 'dzin pa kun gyis mdun nas bdar/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyis sdun nas bsus/ 'jig rten skyong ba rnams kyis zhabs nas bteg /lha dang lha mo'i
tshogs dpag tu med pas me tog gi char 'bebs shing 'ja' dang 'od kyi lam nas dag pa'i zhing du gshegs par gyur to/ /kye ma yab rje rdo rje 'chang dbang de/ /rtag par zhen
tshe chos dbyings ngang du gzims/ /chad par rlom tshe sgyu ma'i gzugs skur bzhengs/ /kye ma kyi hud thugs rje'i bdud rtsis skyongs/ /khyod sku nyin byed chos dbyings
nub ri'i rtser/ /gzims tshe 'gro rnams lag gi ku mu da/ /'gram pa'i chu mtshor brten pa ngal ba'i lus/ /zhing 'dir khyod sku'i ngang tshul brdas bstan nas/ /da ni srid zhi'i
cho 'phrul sgyu ma'i gar/ /gnyug ma'i ngang nas ro snyoms g.yo med bde/ /khyod sku dag pa'i rang zhal dbyings su mjal/ /a ho snying la bdud rtsi'i ngal gso byin/ /ces
brjod nas/ dam pa 'di nyid kyi gsang ba'i rtogs pa brjod pa'i gtam/ so so skye bo dag gi spyod yul ma yin pa gong du brjod pa dag gis tshad mas grub pa yin mod/ 'on kyang
'di tsam gyi gsang tshig kyang kun gyi blor mi shong ba'i snod ldan re re rnams kyi spyod yul du bya zhing / 'dis mtshon pa'i gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig yod mod/
'dir brjod par ga la nus so/ /dam pa khyod kyi ngo mtshar gsang ba'i gtam/ /bgrang yas rgyal bas bskal par mi gsung na/ /deng 'dir

cha shas rdzogs par mi spobs kyang / /khyod zhal dran tshe yid la dbang ma mchis/ /de phyir dam pa'i rtogs brjod cha shas kyang / /brjod pa'i dge tshogs bla na med do zhes/
/rgyal rnams bden pa'i dbyangs kyis yid drangs nas/ /gsang chen snying po'i gtam 'di phyogs brgyar bsgrags/ /dam pa'i rnam thar zla shel thig ler baiDUr tshon ris 'khyil/
/rmad byung gtam gyi bdud rtsi'i 'od dkar snyan tshig legs bshad cha yi gter/ /rtogs brjod kunda'i rtse la gar byed dpyod ldan mgrin sngon gtsug phud rgyan/ /deng 'dir
skal bzang blo mun sel la e ma ho shar gyi thig le mtshar/ /a ho 'di na gsang ba mi zad pa'i/ /snyan tshig snying gi gdung sel malli kaH /ngo mtshar rtogs brjod li shi'i
ljon pa dag /skal bzang gzhon nu'i grib bsil 'di ngo mtshar/ /rigs brgya'i cod pan rdo rje 'chang dbang des/ /gsang chen ye shes gzigs pa'i rmad byung gtam/ /bdag lta'i blo
chung za zis sems myos nas/ /thun mong gtam du sgrog la gnang ba stsol/ /skye zhing skye ba dag ni thams cad du/ /gang gi mtshan yang bgrang bas bskal pa'i bar/ /rnyed
par dka' ba'i rje btsun chos kyi rje/ /mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug zhabs pad bsten par shog /mkhyen brtse'i dpal mnga' dbang phyug brgyad dang ldan/ /bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan
'dzin pa'i dpal yon can/ /'dren mchog bzang po pha rgod bla ma rjes/ /skye ba kun tu thugs rjes 'dzin par shog /dkyil 'khor rgya

mtsho'i rigs bdag rdo rje 'chang / /ngur smrig zol gyis rol pa'i bka' drin can/ /mgon po khyod la gsol ba btab pa'i dge /ma gyur mkha' mnyam 'gro ba'i don du bsngo/ /skyabs
chen bla ma rnams kyi byin rlabs dang / /gsang chen rgyud sde zab mo'i bden tshig dang / /mthu chen mkha' 'gro srung ma'i mthu stobs kyis/ /rlabs chen smon lam 'grub pa'i
bkra shis shog /shu bha mastu sarba dza ga taM/ 'di na sngon med gsang ba'i gtam/ /mkha' 'gro dpa' bo'i phyag sor rtser/ /bzhugs nas snod ldan bu la byin/ /skal min rna
bar sa ma ya/ /zhes bka' rgyas kyang btab bo/ /sa mA ya gu hya/ rdo rje 'chang dbang rje btsun mkhyen brtse'i zhabs/ /bka' drin mtshungs med dran mchog bslab gsum rje/ /yab
sras zhabs rdul mchod pa'i skal bzang can/ /thugs yid gcig phyung gang des sbyar ba dge /dpe 'di pha bla mas bdag la dgyes bzhin du gnang ba byin rlabs che'o/ /zhes pa'o/
/dbyar gyi char sprin sngon por 'khrigs pa'i rum/ /g.yu 'brug mgrin rnga shugs kyis sgrog byed na/ /dam pa'i rang bzhin rmad du byung ba'i gtam/ /dngos po'i gshis la
mtshar 'dzin byis pa'i blo/ /'jam mgon byin rlabs nya gang 'od dkar nas/ /mkhas grub ga bur gzegs mas sgrib gnyis kyi/ /gdung sel sgyu 'phrul lha lam mtha' rnyed na/ /yon
tan 'di tsam rdul gyi cha las phra/ /gang thugs

bla ma yi dam chos srung dang / /dbyer med mkha' la mkha' yi sbyor ba bzhin/ /so sor med kyang sna tshogs gzigs pa'i tshon/ /kun rdzob dngas shel dngos su 'ja' ltar bkra/ /rnal
'byor dbang mos rjes brtse dril bu'i zhabs/ /skyengs nas mkha' spyod zhing du bros pa dang / /lhan cig tshangs spyod brtul zhugs brtan po yis/ /nye bar 'khor gyi bsnyems
pa chung ngur byas/ /rdo rje chos skyong bran 'khol gnam lcags thog /yid srubs brag ri btags la mtshar du ci/ /dbang bzhi'i lam kyi bgrod pas tshe gcig la/ /sku bzhi'i
go 'phang rnyed der gang gis bsnyon/ /'bum phrag lce yis bskal par brjod pa'i tshad/ /bzung bar nus min bdag blos ga la srid/ /tshangs pas zag bcas bde ba'i gnyid spangs
te/ /bsams kyang rtogs dkas snying las chung ngur gyur/ /'on kyang 'di tsam mthong spel smra ba yi/ /'dab chags grib ltar rjes 'brel yang srid kun/ /tshad ma bzhi ldan
chos dang de ston pa'i/ /bla mas rjes 'dzin skal bzang thob bam snyam/ /zhabs drung brtan pa'i drung ngam bsod nams rab brtan du grags pa la 'dar chos rdzong pa'i sras mo
dpon sa nam mkha'i drung blangs par sras ma byung ba'i chun mar tshe dbang drung bsrus pa'i sras 'a zha nam mkha' phun tshogs la rwa lo'i gdung brgyud sde pa brgya tsho
ba'-i lcam bsod nams 'bo le zhes par sras rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ nam mkha' tshe brtan rdo rje/ nam mkha' mgon po/ nam mkha'

bkra shis dang bzhi bltams pa'i gcen rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyi rnam par thar pa logs su 'bri bar spro bas 'dir ma bkod/ nam mkha' tshe brtan dang nam mkha' bkra
shis gnyis kyang / legs bshad rin po che las/ phal cher bu tsha'i spyod pa ni/ /rigs brgyud snga ma'i rjes su 'gro/ /khu byug phrug gu rgya khra ru/ /'gro ba rgyal lam
srid pa tsam/ /zhes yab mes gong ma rnams kyi chas kyis dpa' zhing bsgrigs kyis che ba sogs lugs gnyis kyi spyod tshul mtha' dag ya rabs bzang po'i ngang tshul kho nar
byung la/ khyad par 'a zha nam mkha' mgon po'i khab tu mnga' ris gong ma'i bla sman pa 'a sras pa'i sras mo tshe dbang bsod nams dpal mo bsus pa'i yab yum gnyis ka'ang che
btsun gdung gis mtho ba'i ngang tshul dang ldan zhing tshe 'di'i don du gtan mdun rgyab tu bskyur ba'i gya gyu'i ngan spyod ye mi mdzad par rje la gus shing 'bangs la byams
pa ngo tsha shes shing khrel gzhung gi bag yod pa/ bsod nams kyi zhing dkon mchog gsum la mchod pa dang ma nus par sbyin gtong / dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams kyi zhabs
rdul bsnyen nas gsang chen zab mo'i nyams bzhes la lhod pa mi mnga' bas phyi'i ltar snang gi cha lugs gcig kyang ding sang gi sde dpon du grags pa rnams kyis dpe zlar
mi 'os pa zhig yin la/ yab yum de gnyis kyi sras su nam mkha' bsod nams rab brtan dang gcung nam mkha' don grub dbang po

gnyis 'khrungs pa'i gcen dam pa 'di nyid lhums su ma zhugs pa'i sngon du yum gyi mnal lam du rdor 'dzom zer ba'i zhing gi tshigs nas krong chung dung gi gang ba rnyed khrod
nas lcam gyi a jos dung dkar g.yas 'khyil legs po zhig tshe dbang bsod nams dpal rang gyis zhes gtad pa sku phag tu bcug pa rmis/ lhums su zhugs pa'i tshe srid pa 'khor
ba'i ngang tshul mtha' dag me 'bar ba'i rlubs ltar sdug bsngal gyi rang bzhin can lha mi'i dbang phyug rnams kyang zag bcas kyi bde bar 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal yid brtan mi
rung ba'i chos can dang / tshul des drangs nas rang nyid gcig pur ma zad khams gsum gyi sems can thams cad sdug bsngal gsum ci rigs kyis mnar bar mi bzod pa'i snying rje
dang skyo shas nges 'byung bcos ma ma yin pa dang / sdug bsngal de dag las thar pa'i skyabs gnas dkon mchog rin po che rnam pa gsum yin par rgyu mtshan shes nas mi 'phrog
pa'i dad pa brtan po gong du 'phel ba sogs yum gyi thugs la 'gyur ba sngar dang mi 'dra ba 'khrungs par brten nas de dag ka mad sum cur gras pa'i tshigs bcad kyang mdzad/
mnal lam du brag mthon po zhig gi rtser thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug phyag na bum pa bsnams te bzhugs pa'i brag rtsar yum nyid 'khod pa'i dbu gtsug
nas bum chu skya nar gyi blug pas lus sems bde bas khyab pa'i nyams shar/ de yang sku bltams pa'i yul ni/ khrus khang lo tsA

ba bsod nams rgya mtshos/ lar dus gsum rgyal ba'i thugs rje dang / /rgyal sras pad dkar zhabs drin las/ /bod kyi yul khams 'di nyid kyang / /'phags yul dang skal ba mnyam pa
snyam/ /zhes sras bcas rgyal ba spyi dang lha gcig phyag na padmas byin gyis brlabs pas dge ba bcu'i khrims dang / bshad sgrub kyi bstan pa rgya gar 'phags pa'i yul las
mi zhan par gsungs shing paNDi ta chen po ga ya dha ra'i zhabs kyis/ da dge sbyor byed pa la rgya gar las bod 'di chu bzang zhing bsil drod snyoms/ srog chags nyung la zas
bcud che bas rgya gar du mi 'gro nga bod du sdod/ ces 'khor 'das dbyer med dag pa'i snang bas 'byams su klas pa'i grub pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba des kyang ches cher bsngags
pa'i bod yul gyi stod pu rong / mar yul/ zangs dkar te gsum po skor gcig /li/ gru sha /sbal sde ste gsum po skor gcig /zhang zhung / khri te stod smad de gsum po skor
gcig rnams mnga' ris skor gsum/ mdo khams la smad khams btags pa khams gcig /mdo smad la g.yar mo thang btags pa khams gcig /btsong kha la gyi thang btags pa khams gcig
rnams smad khams sgang gsum sgang drug zer ba ni bar khams rang la nang gses kyi dbye bar mngon/ bar na dbus ru dang g.yo ru gnyis/ g.yas ru dang ru lag gnyis te dbus gtsang
ru bzhir grags pa'i g.yas ru'i cha shar gong ma'i lung gis bod chol

kha gsum la dpal ldan sa skya pas mnga' sgyur ba'i tshe shangs khri skor gyi nang tshan dang gnam gyis bskos pa'i dpal phag mo gru pa'i dus rdzong chen bcu gsum du grags pa
pho brang chen po rin chen spungs pa'i chab 'bangs su gtogs pa gnubs khu lung zhes sngon dpal bsam yas mchims phur slob dpon chen po padma sam bha was sgrub pa bka' brgyad
kyi dbang bskur ba'i dus rje 'bangs dgur grags pa'i sku 'jam dpal gshin rje'i dkyil 'khor du me tog phog pa gnubs sangs rgyas ye shes rin po che sogs skyes chen du ma
'khrungs shing khyad par khu lung pa yon tan rgya mtshos mtshon gnubs kyi sngags 'chang rim par byon pa'i bsti gnas rje mi las lha rje gnubs chung par drag sngags gza' gdong
dmar nag zhus nas hUM shi phaT sgyel gyi mthus sku dgra'i tshogs chom la phab cing byang khar paN chen rin po che shAkya shrI'i brgyud 'dzin bstan pa'i rtsa ba so sor
thar pa'i 'byung khungs chos lung tshogs par grags pa'i sde tshugs pa/ lho byang gi yul gru rnams kyang / rtogs brjod rin po che las/ gser gyi ba gam gzhal yas khang / /khang
pas bskor ba'i grong khyer ni/ /'od ldan zhes bya bsod nams nas/ /'od ldan mtho ris lta bu yod/ /ces margad gos su klubs pa'i spang ljongs me tog rnam par bkra ba sna
tshogs pa'i 'bru rigs kyi snye mas yongs su dud pa'i zhing gi phyogs mtshams su ljon shing gi 'phreng bas kun nas dkris pa/ grong dang grong brdal gyis khyab pa 'chi med
kyi

dga' tshal la co 'dri bas/ me long mar/ skyed tshal 'phreng 'di bu mo bzhin/ /mdzes ldan sA la kA na na/ /zhes yid du 'ong bar gsungs shing thag ha cang mi ring bar pakShu'i
klung chen po 'bab pa ni/ klu kun tu dga' ba'i zlos gar du/ li shi'i yal 'dab dag ni zos gyur pa'i/ /lag ldan chu yi sgregs pa'i dri bzang gis/ /chu dang ldan pa rgya mtsho'i
rba rlabs 'di/ /rin cen 'od zer dag gis spras te mdzes/ /zhes mtho ris lha'i chu bo ma dag pa'i dri ma 'khru ba la ring du chas pa lta bu/ ba da ra'i gling bgrod kyi
rtogs pa brjod pa'i yal 'dab las/ rtse mo shin tu mtho ba yi/ /shel gyi sa gzhi mdun du mthong / /bya rnams kyis kyang bgrod dka' na/ /'jam pa'i brag ni gcig pu der/ /zhes
lho byang gi ri bo rnams mkha' la bsnyeg pa ltar mtho zhing shel dkar gyi brag ri bcal du bkram pa dang la lar spang dang rtsi shing nags tshal mngon par dkris pa'i
yul gyi cha khu lung gzhis kar yab dgung lo nyer bzhi dang yum bco brgyad kyi bgrang byar babs pa'i tshe 'phags yul du stod 'grel pa'i lugs la sho bha na zhes phyogs 'dir
mdzes byed duu grags shing 'jam dbyangs gong ma'i khab tu gu'i ma'u zhes chu mo yos kyi lo dus ni/ 'phags skyes po'i rtogs pa brjod pa'i yal 'dab las/ de nas yid srubs longs
spyod grogs/ /sbrang rtsi 'thung ba rnams kyi gnyen/ /skal bzang 'khri shing 'khyud byed pa/ /legs

ldan dpyid ni mthong bar 'gyur/ /zhes spyir 'dul mngon dus 'khor nag rtsis rgyal po lo gsar sogs lo 'go 'dzin lugs mang na'ang rgya rtsis rnying ma la bcu gcig pa dpyid zla
ra ba stag tu ngos 'dzin pas kun yid dga' ston ster ba legs ldan dpyid kyi dus la babs pa mArga shI ra zhes pa hor zla bcu gcig pa'i dmar cha'i gang ba gsum pa mkha' 'gro
'du ba nyer dgu res gza' zla ba/ skar ma sogs pa/ nyi shar bum pa'i dus sbyor gyi tshe yum la bsnyun mi mnga' ba'i ngang nas lte ba'i ga sha gsum rim du dkris te a zhes
pa'i rang sgra dang bcas sku 'khrungs/ de'ang kun mkhyen bu'i gsung skyor lung pas drangs par/ don dam gshis kyi gnas lugs la/ /rtsis dang 'bras bu'i spros pa bral/ /tha
snyad las 'bras mi slu bas/ /dge ba'i 'bras bu bde ba dang / /sdig pas sdug bsngal sbyin par byed/ /gza' skar bde sdug byed po min/ /byed can bcu gsum mu stegs smra/ /de
ni log pa'i kun rdzob yin/ /tha snyad slu med bden pa ru/ /rtsis tshul nges par 'dzin dgos te/ /dper na tha snyad dbang bskur dang / /cho ga lha grub byas pa yis/ /don de
'grub par sangs rgyas dang / /paN grub rnams kyis gsungs pa bzhin/ /rtsis tshul rgyud sde mdo mang por/ /rtsis tshul byed par gces par gdams/ /zhes zla ba bsod nams kyi
gza' btsan phyug dang ldan zhing / sog pa chos ldan thos shing las kun mkhas pa sogs rten 'brel gyi sgo 'phar 'grig pa ni/ mdo

sde rgyan las/ skye ba skyed mos tshal 'gro ltar rtogs nas/ /spro ba'i sems drangs dga' zhing de la 'jug /ces dam pa rnams ni 'gro ba'i don du srid par skye ba len pa la chags
ldan gyi skyes bu skyed mos tshal du 'jug pa lta bu'i spro ba dang ldan par bshad pas rje 'di nyid rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje'i rnam par sprul par gdon mi za bas
spyi dang bye brag gi bstan pa'i btsas su mkha' spyod dag pa'i zhing nas nyi ma las 'od zer bzhin du shar yang gdul bya thun mong ba rnams kyi snang ngo dang mthun par
byis pa'i rnam par bstan pa de la rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyis mtshan nam mkha' bsod nams rab brtan du gsol/ de 'phral du zhugs skongs kyi lci shing dang na
