bza'i rgyu'i snam phrug rtsol med du gzhan gyis 'bul mi byung zhing / yum gyi chab zho'ang shin tu mang bas bzhes pa'i lhag ma sman gyi rgyur dkrogs pa dang nyin mtshan bar
ma chad par 'dzag pa na dbang thang che ba'i ltas legs zer/ sku'i dbyibs dpral ba dbyes che zhing zhal khyim sgor ba/ dbu gdugs ltar phug pa sogs mtshan dpe rjes mthun
pas spras shing / mdangs dkar la gsal ba/ sku bong gzhan las che la kun gyi yid du 'ong ba snyun nad gdon zhud kyi 'tshe ba dang bral ba zhig byung zhing gsung ma bye ba'i
dus zhal ngo lhan rgyas su bzhugs pa'i tshe yum gyi sku pang na gral mjug tu yod pa la gsung gtser ba sogs mi dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur bstan pa rmo mos gral gsham

du bzhugs ma 'dod par 'dug gral 'gor bzhugs chug zer ba de bzhin du mdzad pas dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur bstan pa na nye skor du 'khod pa rnams byis pa dkyus ma'i ngang tshul dang
mi ldan pa zhig go snyam ngo mtshar du 'dzin/ dgung lo gnyis 'gro ba'i tshe rje dbang phyug rab brtan gyis sku 'gag gsar pa bzhes nas byang gter gyi tshe dbang lcags sdong
ma stsal ba'i skabs sku'i dbyibs dang na bza'i khyad par sogs thugs la nges te sku na yar phebs nas dran zhes sku 'khor ba tshor bka' stsal pa ni lo ngo gnyis kyi dus
de 'dra gang zag phal par 'byung ba mi srid cing gal te dus der ngo 'phrod pa lta bu'i dbang du byas na'ang rjes su dran gsos par rang cag rnams la mi 'byung ba mngon sum
du grub pas/ mngon pa kun las btus su/ dran pa gang zhe na/ 'dris pa'i dngos po la sems kyis brjed pa med pa ste rnam par mi g.yeng ba'i las can no/ /zhes sku tshe gzhan
du zhi gnas sam bskyed pa'i rim pa'i ting nge 'dzin la goms pa'i nang rtags phyir shar te blo ldan zhig gis dpyad na 'di gcig pu'i rnam thar yang dpag par dka'a'o/ /sngon
med pa'i rdo chung ngu dang 'jim pa spyin po mang po khu lung gi gzhis ka'i ltag nas rnyed pa dang / zan sogs la gtsug lag khang dang dge 'dun gyi sde'i dbyibs/ dkon
cog gi sku gsung thugs rten gyi rnam pa bsgrigs par ting dang kong bu sogs bzos nas mchod pa 'bul ba/ dung dkar bus te dge 'dun tshogs pa/ chos 'chad nyan gyi tshul dang
/ de bzhin du rang nyid kyi bla ma dang

byis pa gzhan rnams gra pa'i tshul du mdzad de chos 'chad pa'i rnam pa/ nga'i ming la btsun chung tshul khrims zer gsung pa/ mdos gtor/ cho ga /bskang bas mtshon pa'i lad mo
sogs bskrun pa sku skye ba mang por 'khor lo gsum gyi bya ba la rtag 'grus su gnang ba'i bag chags kyi mthu brtas pa yin cing dus phyis sku rim la dgos pa'i 'jim pa sngar
shul nas btsal kyang lar ma rnyed pas bka' las nged chung ngu'i dus su blo brid kyi rtse mo'i ched du gzhi bdag gis byin pa yin 'dra gsung / mdor na kun spyod mtha' dag
chos dang mthun pa'i rnam 'gyur ma gtogs byis pa tha mal pa'i ngang tshul ye mi mdzad pas thugs sgam pa'i tshad thub par gleng / dgung lo lnga drug tsam la yum gyis snyan
bad/ gong rna/ sor gdub sogs phul bar mi dgyes shing 'dogs par mi mdzad pa/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes/ la la ba lang ji bzhin spyod/ /kha cig bram ze'i rnam thar
skyong / /kho bo nyan thos spyod pas mdzes/ /shugs 'byung skyong ba bla ma'i drin/ /zhes pa'i don bzhin yang srid du mar nyan thos kyi bslab pa la gnas pa'i bag yod kyi
ngang tshul nyams sad pas khyim pa'i rtags dang cha lugs sogs la thugs mi gzhol bar gnas brtan 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po 'byung ba'i snga ltas so/ /dgung lo bdun gyi steng
du gangs ri'i ljongs 'dir thub bstan yongs su rdzogs pa'i shing rta pa chen po ma byon sangs rgyas gsum pa rab gsal gyi rnam par sprul pa thams

cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che'i gdan sa zha lu ri phug chos kyi pho brang du rigs brgya'i bdag po dbang phyug rab brtan bzhugs pa'i spyan sngar phebs gtsug phud bzhes shing
mtshan mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang por gsol/ rkyen sel rjes gnang ci rigs gsan nas gzhis su thegs/ thun mong zhes pa lcags khyi'i
lo dgung lo brgyad kyi thog slar zha lu ri phug tu phebs pa'i nub snga ma rje bla ma'i 'od gsal du rtsis kyi mgon po chos skyong yid bzhin nor bu'i mngag gzhug dam tshig
srog gi bdag po zab ber dkar po'i gos dang khrab gsol zhing seng ge dkar por zhon pa lag na rgya spos khres kyi chun po dar skud kyis bcings pa spar ba'i tha snyad med par
dri zhim pa phun sum tshogs pas khyab pa zhig khyer nas nam mkhar yud yud 'gro ba byung ba sang nyin bka' las mdang de bzhin byung ba khyed 'byon pa'i ltas su 'dug cing
tshul khrims rnam par dag pa yong ba'i brdar go gsung / rje nyid kyi drung du tshigs snga ma dge tshul gyi dngos por bsgrubs/ mi ring bar rje rdo rje 'chang la stod la chibs
kha bsgyur ba'i zham 'bring mdzad nas gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar phebs 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba dang chos skyong mngon sum du bzhugs pa'i sgo rum mgon khang
sogs la gnas gzigs rgyas par mdzad/ phyir lam lha rtse dang 'dar phyogs su thegs skabs/ sku na gzhon pa la des shing mdzangs pa rnam dpyod kyi mthu phul du phyin pa la
phyogs de'i skye bo rnams ngo mtshar zhing yi rang bar gyur/

de nas sde pa bkra shis rtse ba dang chos sde pa yon mchod nas gdan 'dren byung ba ltar yab sras chabs cig par chibs kha bskyod/ byams chen du rje btsun zha lu ba chen po dang
thog mar mjal/ de nas dbus 'gyur gyi lte ba yar klungs skyid pa'i sman ljongs su phebs/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i gsang chen slob bshad kyi sngags gra bkra shis rtse chos
sder stan chags/ lo shas bzhugs ring rje rdo rje 'chang chen pos gnyug mar gnas pa dang phyogs 'dus kyi dam pa'i chos don du gnyer ba chu'i rlabs 'phreng bzhin yol ba med
pa rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i zhar chos dang / snying po kye rdo rje man ngag lugs/ 'jigs mdzad rdo rje sogs dkyil 'khor du ma'i dbang bzhi/ mkha' spyod skor
gsum/ dmar po skor gsum/ chos skyong che chung nas nyer mkho'i rigs dang gzhan yang rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel ba'i dbang / byin rlabs/ rjes gnang / lung khrid man ngag
mang du gsan cing de dag kyang gsan lo tsam ma yin par sku na phra yang thugs la nges shing byang chub par mdzad/ rje rdo rje 'chang gi dgongs par snyan brgyud mnga' bdag
rin po che bod mkhar nas kyi zhal slob spyan snga mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho'i gdams ngag bum pa gang byor bzhugs pa chos rje rab 'byams pa kun dga' lhun grub gdan sar
bskos nas yab sras gnyis ka gtsang du thegs bzhed de rin po che chos sku ba gdan drangs kyang chos sde ba tsho'i blor babs rgyu ma byung bar brten nged kyi tsha bo 'di chos
bka' 'dra zhu rtsis yin tshul la bsnyad pa'i bka'

chos chag lugs dang dze tA ri'i tshe dpag lha dgu/ khro phu'i 'jam dkar/ phag dkar shes rab gsal byed/ rnam rgyal lha dgu/ rnam 'joms ljang sngon/ seng ge sgra/ nor rgyun ma
ser mo/ khro bo sme brtsegs/ khro mo sme brtsegs dzam ser nag rnams kyi rjes gnang / de dag la mkho ba'i yig cha'i lung / sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang /
mgon pod me 'bar ma'i lung sogs mang du gsan na'ang sku na phra ba dang phyag g.yog grul thub med gshis brgyud yig gi dogs gcod gnang rgyu ma byung 'dug rung 'chad bzang
po yin zhes thugs mos par mdzad/ dgung lo bco lngar phebs pa dmar ser can zhes me mo sbrul gyi lo/ /de'ang mnyan yod mchod pa snga bsnur ba la brten nas bde legs phun sum
tshogs pa byung bas rgya bod kun tu rta chen zla bar mdzad par grags na'ang / rtsa ba'i dus rje mar pas/ cho 'phrul khra yi zla ba la/ /mi kho bo lam du zhugs te mchis/
/zhes sa hor mchod yon gyi zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes lnga gza' skar 'phrod sbyor dge bar dpal ldan shangs pa bka' brgyud kyi chig brgyud rdo rje'i brgyud pa bdun ldan gyi
nang tshan sangs rgyas gnyan ston chen po'i sprul pa'i zlos gar mkhan rin po che gzhon nu blo gros kyi bzhugs khri'i thog tu bstan pa spyi dang bye brag rdo rje 'chang tshar
pa chos rje'i ring lugs rgya cher spel ba'i ched du 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por rigs kyi sras stong phrag tsam yod na'ang thu bor gyur pa rgyal sar dbang bskur ba
bzhin dam pa'i

chos kyi rgyal tshab chen por khyab bdag bla ma dbang phyug rab brtan gyis mnga' gsol bar mdzad nas shis pa brjod pa'i me tog gi char chen po phyogs kun tu bsnyil/ de'i tshe
gtsang sde srid/ sde pa yar stod pa/ bkra shis rtse gsum nas bsko 'ja'/ gra rigs sbyin bdag rnams kyis legs skyes rgya cher bstod/ ljags bsngo gsung dpangs mtho zhing snyan
la brjod bya rjod byed kyi don phun sum tshogs pas de 'khor thams cad dga' mgu yi rang gi sar bkod/ rje rdo rje 'chang gtsang phyogs su chibs kyi kha lo bskyod na'ang
dam pa 'di nyid kyis gra sa'i khur bzhes so ba'i btags ming tsam ma yin par sgrub mchod dang bskang ba gtor sgrub sogs kyi rdo rje slob dpon rje bla ma'i dus ji lta ba'i
phyag len phra rags mtha' dag la thugs zhib cing 'phyugs med kyi dag ther kho na bstar ba ma gtogs 'jig rten bya ba gtso bor bzung ste gal chung chos su smra ba'i thebs
chag ye mi gnang bas rje bla ma kun spangs mdzad par gra rigs rnams mya ngan gyi mes yid gdungs pa'ang dam pa 'di'i mdzad pa'i char chen pos bsil bas gsos sman bla na med
par gyur to/ /ches btsun 'od gsal lha yi gdung ma 'chol/ /mkhas dang grub pa'i byin rlabs rgyun ma chad/ /bstan 'gro'i nyer 'tshor lhag bsam mthu ma nyams/ /rgyal sras
slob mar sprul pa'i mtha' ma rdzogs/ /ma dang mkha' 'gro'i grong du bde chen klong / /gzims la tshad med lha mos yongs bskul mthus/ /zhing 'dir mtshan dpe'i zlos gar mngon
sum du/ /gsal 'di yid can legs byas bye

bas nyos/ /na tshod gzhon nus phal spyod glang po'i mche/ /phyungs te dam pa'i rnam thar mdongs mtha' la/ /zhon nas rgyal bstan mtho ris mdzes pa'i rgyan/ /gdong drug gnyis
pa'i lha gzhan gang du rnyed/ /srid pa chu srin 'byung gnas sdug bsngal rlabs/ /mi yol mtshang rig myang 'das gru rdzings kyis/ /gtan bde'i nor bu len la legs zhugs pa'i/
/nyes med dang po'i phun tshogs cho ga rdzogs/ /sa la mngon sum gnas pa'i 'og min zhing / /sa chen brgyud pa rim byon gzhal med khang / /sa steng zla bral sku gsung thugs
rten rnams/ /sa skya'i bstan 'dzin khyod kyi gzigs mor mtshar/ /tshar chen gdung chos mai tri yab sras kyi/ /mtha' klas snyan brgyud bka' babs kun tu dga'i/ /lam bzang
ston la spobs pa lhun grub rje/ /rdo rje 'dzin pa'i zhabs pad yun du bsnyen/ /mchog gi gdul byar gdams pa gsang chen lam/ /slob bshad bkra shis chos kyi 'dus sde'i khrir/
/yab gcig bla mas bstan pa'i bdag po ru/ /mnga' gsol grags snyan tshangs pa'i yul sar bsgrags/ /'di nas bzung lcags sprel bar phar cher bkra shis chos sde nyid du bzhugs
nas chos sde'i 'dzin skyong spel gsum bca' ba chos khrims/ nang gi grwa rigs dang phyogs 'dus kyi chos don du gnyer ba rnams la dbang / byin rlabs/ rjes gnang / rig gtad/
nyams khrid/ lung man ngag /phyag khrid sogs blo dang 'tsham pa'i re ba skong zhing sbyin bdag skya ser gyis mtshon pa'i skye bo mchog dman bar pa rnams la'ang rkyen sel
gyi byin rlabs

rjes gnang / yan lag brgyad pa'i khrims dang yig drug gi bzlas lung sogs gang la gang 'tsham gyi sgo nas mngon mtho dang nges legs kyi sa bon khyad par can bskrun/ bar 'tshams
mang por zla sbrel du rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs lha bcu gsum ma sogs dkyil 'khor 'ga' dang lha bran du ma'i ljags bsnyen/ bcu cha'i sbyin sreg gis mtshon phra zhib
kyi phyag len bzhin thugs nyams su bstar/ sku mtshams min pa'i skabs kyang bskyed rdzogs kyi nyams bzhes bzlas brjod gtor bsngos sogs mtshan bcas mtshan med kyi thugs dam
la lhod pa cung zad tsam yang mi mnga' zhing shi gson gyi ched du bdog pa dbul bar thugs brtse ba chen pos kun nas blangs pa'i nad gdon las grol ba dang dus kyi chos nyid
du gyur pa rnams 'khor ba dang ngan song gi 'phrang ring po las bsgral te nges par legs pa'i sar bkri ba'i skyabs 'jug ched du gsol bar rigs drug gnas 'dren sogs gshin
po rjes 'dzin gyi cho ga rgyud sde rin po che las ji ltar byung ba bzhin ma gtogs sla chos kyi rigs mi mdzad/ dngos po rnams kyang dkon cog la sri zhu/ dge 'dun la bsnyen
bkur/ nyam thag la sbyin gtong sogs rnam dkar gyi ched kho nar 'gro ba'i zhal ta dang mdor na mgon po byams pas/ yi ge 'dri mchod sbyin pa dang / /nyan dang klog dang len
pa dang / /'chad dam kha ton byed pa dang / /de sems pa dang sgom pa ste/ /spyod pa 'di bcu'i bdag nyid kyi/ /bsod nams phung po gzhal du med/ /ces chos spyod bcu'i

bya ba lhur mdzad pas yar stod smad shar nub kyis mtshon pa'i lho byang gi skye rgu phyogs 'dzin drag po'i gdon gyis ma zin pa mtha' dag dad pa'i sa la 'god bzhin pa'i ngang
nas gtsang phyogs su bteg /lcags sprel khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan mjal bar phebs pa'i tshe gur mgon gyi gsang 'khrid zla ba gsum gyi bar smin rgyas dang / gzhan yang
zab chos mang po lcags bya zhabs phyir bzhugs mu nas klu sgrub chos kyi rgyal mtshan sogs du ma dang lhan cig tu gsang sngags gsar rnying gi chos rgya cher gsan/ gtsang
sde srid nas rje rdo rje 'chang zha lu ri phug gi dbu mdzad chen mor bskyar bskos grub nas sgrub chen dang 'brel ba'i bka' brgyad gsang rdzogs kyi dbang gis thugs kyi
bum bzang gtams nas ston bkra shis rtse chos sder phebs zla shas kyi bar bzhugs nas gtsang du chibs kha bskyor/ bla ma dgon pa skye lung pas rdo rje 'chang skye bdun sgrub
par gdan drangs pa'i phyag phyi mdzad/ yang 'ug gis gtsos pa'i sngags pa mang por bka' brgyad sgrub dbang gnang ba dang lhan du gsan/ rje rdo rje 'chang la bsnyen par rdzogs
pa'i bslab ston zhu ba gnang bar 'di tshor las slob gsang ston kha skong sogs cha tshang bsgrig dka' bar 'dug pas ngor du bsnyen rdzogs kyi gra bzang bas 'gab tshul
phebs pa ltar rnga chen zhes pa chu khyi'i lo yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya seng ge tshes bdun la sku bltams shing tshes bco lngar mngon par byang chub pa
dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i dus chen khyad par can 'byung ba'i sa ga'am nam mthong

zla ba sngon mar grags pa gza' skar sbyor byed phun sum tshogs pa'i skabs yon tan rin po che ma lus pa 'byung ba'i gnas dpal e waM chos ldan gyi gtsug lag khang du mi 'phrogs
pa'i mkhyen rab dang dmigs pa med pa'i thugs rje chen po mnga' zhing brtan mkhas kyi yon tan gnyis dang ldan pa'i gnas brtan 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po bcas pa phra mo las
kyang mi 'da' bas tshul khrims kyi dri bsung phyogs brgyar khyab pas 'phags pa nye ba 'khor sa 'dir 'phos pa lta bu don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos te thams cad mkhyen
pa sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub kyis mkhan po/ sngon rje mnga' bdag gi dus rgyal po'i bla sman stod na bi ji cher rje 'ug pa gsum/ bar na mi nyag brang ti g.yu thog
gsum/ smad na gnya' dang mtha' bzhi stong dang gsum ste dgu'i nang nas mchog tu gyur pa brang ti'i rigs las mkhas btsun grub pa'i dbang phyug thar pa rtse ba nam mkha' sangs
rgyas pas las kyi slob dpon/ dpal ldan sa skya'i shar nub gung gsum du grags pa'i shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/ thams cad mkhyen pa ye shes rgyal mtshan sogs bstan 'dzin
rim par byon pa'i dbon gnas brtan 'dul ba 'dzin pa shes rab 'byung gnas pas gsang ste ston pa'i slob dpon/ dus bsgo ba sgrub khang mnga' ris pa nam mkha' dpal ldan sogs dad
pa'i dge 'dun grangs tshang ba'i dbus su chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che'i las chog gi phyag bzhes sla chos dang rung mthun

sbyar ba tsam ma yin pa'i phra zhib kyi rgyun bzang po mdzad bzhin pa'i steng nas bstan par zhugs la yongs su rdzogs pa dge slong gi dngos po rnam dag tu gyur nas nyes ltung
gi dri mas ma gos pa gnas brtan 'dul ba 'dzin pa rnams kyi mchog tu gyur cing 'di nas bzung ji srid bar lus ngag gi sdom pa las cung zad kyang mi g.yo bas/ thams cad mkhyen
pa'i gsung mgur las/ thub dbang dge ba'i bshes gnyen kun dga' legs pa'i zhabs las/ /so thar sdom pa thob pa nyams su legs par blangs nas/ /nyes ltung dri mas ma gos
ngo lkog med par bsrungs pas/ /btsun pa tshogs pa'i khrod 'dir mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug skyid do/ /zhes gsungs pa'i don dang mthun no/ /bla ma dam pa 'di gsum la zab rgyas
kyi chos snga phyir gsan pa cher long tsam 'dir phyogs gcig tu bsdoms pa la mkhan chen sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub kyi drung du 'dul ba mdo rtsa/ me tog phreng
rgyus/ sum brgya pa/ 'grel pa 'od ldan/ kun mkhyen bu'i las chog /ngor du grags che ba'i mdo chung bcu bdun/ rdor gcod/ sdud pa/ sman mdo brgyad brgya pa/ mkhan po'i mdo
chog /byams chos sde lnga/ spyod 'jug rnams kyi lung / kye rdor Dombhi/ mtsho skyes/ nag po lugs/ bdag med lha mo bco lnga/ gur rigs bsdus/ sambu Ti'i rdor dbyings/ bde mchog
lo nag dril gsum/ 'jigs byed sa lugs dang rwa lugs/ sgrol ma lha bcu bdun ma/ rigs byed ma lha lnga/ phyag rdor 'chi bdag 'joms pa/

'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na lha lnga/ rigs gsum spyi/ mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu/ tshe dpag med dze tA ri lugs rnams kyi dbang dang de rnams kyi mngon dkyil kha shas/ Dombhi pa'i
bdag med ma'i sgrub thabs bdud rtsi'i 'od sogs kye rdor gyi rgya gzhung mang tsam/ jo bo'i chos chung brgya rtsa/ thogs med bka' 'bum rnams kyi lung / rje thar pa rtse
ba'i drung du gsar ma rgyud 'bum/ 'phreng ba skor gsum/ mngon dkyil gyi cho ga thar rtse paN chen gyis mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i rjes gnang lung bcas/ gdong drug
gi dbang dang yig sna kha shas/ ngor chen gyis mdzad pa'i mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i yig sna/ kun mkhyen go bo rab 'byams pa'i bka' 'bum/ gnubs lugs stag zhon/ gnyos trag /dzam
dkar gsum gyi rjes gnang / rje shar pa sher 'byung ba'i drung du kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi rgyu dbang / lam dbang / bde mchog bong zhal can dang tshe dpag med lha dgu
gnyis kyi dbang / dpa' bo gcig sgrub kyi 'jam dbyangs/ pha dam pa'i 'jam dbyangs/ chag lugs tshe dpag med dkar po/ klu dbang rgyal po/ u tsa ya/ sme brtsegs ljang nag
/khyung nag /dbyangs can ma dkar dmar/ rnam 'joms mthing kha/ seng gdong ma sngo dmar rnams kyi rjes gnang dang yi ge'i lung kha yar rnams gsan no/ /gsol bzhi'i cho ga ma
la ya klung nas/ /bag yod khrims kyi dri bsung rab 'thul ba'i/ /'dul 'dzin tsandan sdong po dar drag pas/ /phra rgyas tsha gdung bcil ba'i cho ga mkhan/ /rang

rgyud zhi byed 'phags bod sdom pa'i chab/ /rtsing spyod dug bral nyon mongs nad brgya'i sman/ /rgyal kun dgyes pa'i mchod sprin thun 'tshams gos/ /'chang ba'i tshul la mi smon
shes ldan su/ /thub pas lung bstan rje btsun e waM pa'i/ /lugs 'dzin dkyil 'khor spro bsdu'i byed po 'gas/ /nges gsang chos sgo brgya phrag phye ba'i tshe/ /auDDi ya
na sa 'dir 'phos pa bzhin/ /rim gnyis chang gis myos pa'i bde stong zung / /'jug pa'i mdza' mor rtse dgas rtag rol yang / /lus ngag sdom la phyi nang med brtson pa'i/ /rnam
'dren bstan pa'i rtsa bar da gdod 'khums/ /zha lur phebs/ chu phag gi dgun stod bar zham 'bring du bsnyen te mkhan chen sgrub khang pa byon pa'i dpon slob gnyis kar thos
bsam mang du mdzad/ rdo rje 'chang dgung lo re lngar phebs shing dbus gtsang gi bar sa khad 'gyangs par ma zad 'dar gyi mkhan po gnang gshis sku na dang bcas 'grul bskyod
gnang stabs ma bde ba'i mkhan chen gzhon nu blo gros kyi gdung zhugs 'bul dang rten bzhengs sogs bslab ston rgyas par stsal nas dbus su byon/ hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i nang
du rje btsun gzhon nu blo gros kyi sku pur dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor la brten nas zhugs su phul ba'i tshe sngar nged kyi pur su la'ang ma ston gsung ba'i zhal
chems yod pa la dpags grwa dmangs tshos go med kyis mdzad dka' zhus dogs tshogs pa rnams gdugs rol cha sogs mchod rdzas kyi phyag mtshan dang bcas

gsung chog ma tshar bar gtsug lag khang la ser sbreng gi skor ba dang pur khang gi steng thog tu gdugs dang g.yas g.yon du bkra shis khra ring btang zhing sbyangs zin nas zhag
shas bar rgyas btab pa zhal phye nas/ gdung rten bzhengs par bal po mkhas pa mi grangs bcu gcig 'bod pa gnang ba'i gser zangs kyi rnam rgyal mchod rten zla gnyis khongs
su grub par dri med kyi srog shing 'dzugs pa'i cho ga /ring bsrel rnam pa bzhi'i gzungs 'bul dngos gtsang brten bzhengs so'i snyan grags lhur blangs pa ma yin pa'i khungs
btsun yid ches su gyur par bcom ldan 'das dpal kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi sgrub mchod dang 'brel ba'i rab gnas kyi cho ga nyin gnyis ma'i sgo nas dam tshig pa la ye
shes kyi tshogs dngos su bcug pas lha rnams kyis mchod pa'i slad du 'ja' tshon sna lnga'i gur dang me tog gi char/ rgya spos bzang po'i ngad kyis sgrun du med pa'i dri
bzang pos phyogs kun tu khyab pa ngo mtshar ba'i ltas ya mtshan pa byung ba ni/ rje btsun bla ma rim par byon pa mtha' dag la dad pa sngar ma skyes pa rnams gsar du skye
zhing / skyes pa'i tshogs gong 'phel du 'gyur ba'i thabs khyad par can te/ mkhas mchog dpa' bos/ grags pa'i mtshan mar gyur pa bzang po 'di rnams kyis/ /bde bar gshegs gyur
lam rnams gang yin bstan par 'gyur/ /yid la dad pa med pa rnams kyang dad par byed/ /chos dang ldan pa'i gtam gyis rab tu dga' bar 'gyur/ /zhes pa'i don du mngon zhing
/ sde pa bkra shis rtse bas gsung ngag brgyud pa'i zhal thang

thog tshad ma skya ris grub cing tshon 'go tshugs tsam la lus par kha skong cung zad dang bcas grangs sum cu tham pa gong gsham zhal khebs tog ldan legs par bsgrubs par kye

chen dpal ldan don grub/ brang ti pa nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas gsum dang mjal zhing bris thang la phyag nas zhu ba mdzad/ rim gyis 'dar stod bla
ma'i gdan sar phebs/ rje rdo rje 'chang la phyi nang phyag rdzas yod dgu lta bu'i 'bul chen dang bcas gsung ngag brgyud par dam tshig pa la ye shes pa 'jug pa'i phyag
nas zhus/ de nas bdag tshe dang sgrub pa mnyam pa'i bug sgo 'dam sbyar byas chog pa'i gsol ba btab par/ khyod kyis sgom sgrub gcig pu mdzad pas ga la khyab/ thos bsam 'chad
nyan bya ba las kyi 'khor lo sogs tshang ma mdzad na bstan 'gro'i don rgya cher 'grub tshul bslab bya lung bstan gyi tshul du gnang bar brten bla ma dam pas ji ltar bka'

sdong che/ /rab tu brtson pa'i mthu

su 'khyil ba brgyud pa'i 'phreng / /snang srid ri mor 'dri la zla med pas/ /bskrun tshe sgyu ma'i khengs pa thung ngur byas/ /dregs ldan langga'i stobs las mi 'jigs pa'i/

o rgyan gling pa'i stag zhon gyi dbang lung yongs rdzogs/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod rdo rje'i rim lnga'i nyams 'khrid/ thugs rje chen po tshem bu lugs/ blo sbyong don bdun

mi mnga'/ chos phyir dka' spyad byang chub sems dpa' rtag tu ngu'i rjes su 'gro zhing / ji skad du/ sbrang rtsi 'dzin pa sbrang rtsi'i brtul zhugs can/

/sbrang bu min pas sbrang rtsi'i bcud ma myong / /gzhung lugs smra ba kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal/ /bzang po min pas shes bya'i bcud ma myong / /zhes 'jam dbyangs sa paN gyi

dam pa 'di nyid dang / de dang cha mthun pa ni glang phu nas chos rje tsam du mngon/ 'dar grang mo cher kha'u brag rdzong pa'i lugs srol thun mong ma yin pa'i shing rta'i

bi rU pa/ /gang gi thugs bcud gsang chen dbyar skyes sgra/ /thos pas 'phags bod skal bzang rma bya kun/ /bcu gsum rdo rje'i sa la grub pa'i mtha'/ /rab snyog mngal khur
'dzin la gcig tu brel/ /phyogs re tsam min thub bstan yongs rdzogs chos/ /tshogs slob bshad srol bzhed pa ches mang ba'i/ /snying po'i yang shun snyan brgyud bdud rtsi'i
bcud/ /snod ldan legs bris las gzhan skal ba phra/ /rin chen sgang dang rgyal tsha lung mang po'i/ /gdung rigs rim byon zhal brgyud gser gyi chos/ /mgon zung man ngag mkha'
'gro'i kha rlangs can/ /'dzin khyod zla med nam mkha'i zla ba 'dra/ /rgyud sde'i thig le kun bsdus lung rtogs bzhin/ /mthong mod

ches sgam tshangs pa'i yid 'phrog tshe/ /lha rnams ba spu ldang bar chun po'i thod/ /me tog 'dab ma 'dzum dbus ge sar rgod/ /tshogs gnyis sdong po dar drag a mra'i ljon/ /thos
bsam 'bras bu'i ro bda' smin pa'i zhar/ /bya ba las kyi grib mar skye rgu kun/ /bde ba'i ngal gso bsod nams gzugs can bzhin/ /de nas slar bsti gnas yar klungs bkra shis
rtser phebs/ chos sde lcags stag btab pa nas lo so drug las ma song yang bar skabs su sde pa dngos grub rdo rje bsam sdings nas dbon bcos pa'i grub mtha'i 'dzin stangs
gzhan du gzhol ba'i bstan sel chen po'i rkyen gyis chog gra sogs mang ba ma tshugs pa da lam gnyis su med pa'i rgyud kye rdor man ngag lugs/ bdag med lha mo bco lnga/ gur
rigs bsdus/ rdo rje sgrol ma/ ku ru kulle/ pha rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa 'phags lugs dang ye shes zhabs lugs/ 'jigs byed rwa lugs/ phyag rdor 'khor chen/ ma rgyud lo nag gnyis/
nA ro mkha' spyod/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor/ rdo rje gdan bzhi/ sambu Ti/ gur lha brgyad/ rnal 'byor rgyud/ kun rig /bya rgyud rigs gsum spyi/
mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu/ dze tA ri'i tshe dpag med/ 'od zer can ma rnams dkyil 'khor la brten pa/ rnam rgyal stong mchod rnams kyi cho ga nag 'gros su bkod nas 'dzugs pa'i
sta gon du rgyugs bzhes/ rnam bcad dang po sa chog /gnyis

pa sta gon/ gsum pa sgrub mchod dngos rnams la dgos pa'i gar thig dbyangs gsum sogs phyag len che phra mtha' dag sku ngos kyi phyag khrid du mdzad/ dkyil 'khor so so'i dbang
lung / rnam rgyal ma'i rjes gnang rnams nas dbang cha grangs su bcad par shin tu 'grus shing dngos gtsang ba'i sgo nas rgyas par bstar/ me yos hor zla dang po'i cho 'phrul
mchod pa'i dus chog gra rnams btsugs te 'dzugs ston dang bsnyen bkur sogs lha mchod mi mchod lhag par rgya che bar spel/ lo phyi ma rnams su rgyun mi nyams par bya ba'i
slad du sgrub mchod thebs kyi mthun rkyen sbyar bas mtshon gsang chen rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa rin po che srid mtha'i bar du nyams pa med pa'i thabs tshul 'di ni/ rgyal
ba gnyis pa bu ston rin po che/ byams pa'i rnam sprul bdag po kun bzang 'phags/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa dang gsum gyis mdzad pa'i rjes su 'jug pa'i ngo mtshar gyi
gnas che ba zhig tu snang / 'phags pa gang pos zhus pa'i mdo las/ byang chub sems dpas ma thos chos/ /thos na don du tshul bsam bya'i/ /bdag gis sngon chad ma thos zhes/
/de skad du ni smra mi bya/ /ma thos chos ni thos gyur na/ /yang dag dran pas sems byed na/ /rgya mtshor 'bab chu shong ba bzhin/ /de phyir shes rab 'phel bar 'gyur/ /zhes
dam pa rnams ni thos pas nam yang mi ngoms pas sngon chad gsan bsam rgya cher mdzad na'ang de tsam gyi kho bos mang du thos so snyam pa'i mngon pa'i nga rgyal gyi chog
shes shing 'dod yon la skom

pa ba tsha'i chu bzhin ngoms pa med par byed pa'i bshes gnyen du rloms pa du ma dang phyogs tsam yang mi 'dra bar bod 'dir chos rgyun yod pa rnams mi nub pa thugs la brnag
pa dang / rje mkhyen brtse'i gsung mgur las/ steng nas gnam rdib 'og nas sa rub kyang / /bod 'dir yod pa'i lam bzang 'khrul med rnams/ /ma lus len pa'i brtson 'grus mi rtsom
re/ /zhes pa'i don ltar yin cing / 'o skol gyi ston pa slob pa lam gyi gnas skabs su chos tshigs bcad gcig gi ched du sku lus la lcags gzer stong btab pa dang / rgya
bod kyi paN grub mang pos chos phyir lus srog thed la bor ba'i rnam par thar pa la rjes su 'jug pas rje rdo rje 'chang la chos 'phro don du gnyer bar ma zad sku na smin pa
la sri zhu'i slad du sa 'thug gtsang la chibs bskyod pa'i zhar du rje mar pa lo tsA'i dngos slob rngog chos sku rdo rje nas bzung mkhas pa dang grub pa'i bla ma zam ma
chad pa byung ba'i gdung las byon cing rigs tsam lhur len pa ma yin pa'i yab chos mtha' dag la mkhyen pa'i spyan yangs pa rngog ston 'jam dbyangs 'od zer gyi zhabs kyi rdul
dmar dbu'i gtsug tor du bsten nas/ dgyes rdor lha dgu/ bdag med lha mo bco lnga/ rdo rje gur lha zhe dgu/ rnal 'byor nam mkha' lha dgu bcu rtsa bdun/ gdan bzhi yum bka'
lha bcu gsum/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo lha lnga/ 'jam dpal gsang ldan lha nga gsum ma ste rngog dkyil bdun gyi dbang /

man ngag gi yi ge 'ga' zhig 'khrid bcas/ mai tri pa'i phyag yig dgu phrugs kyi byin rlabs/ dud sol ma'i gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang / gter ston nyi zla sangs rgyas kyi 'pho
ba 'jag tshugs ma/ tshe dpag med grub rgyal ma'i byin rlabs rnams gsan/ rim gyis 'dar du rdo rje 'chang gi zhabs drung du phebs nas dbang chos ci rigs gsan/ lo pa spyan snga
kun dga' don grub dge ba'i bshes gnyen spyan snga tshul khrims 'bar gyi rigs dbon bka' gdams kyi bstan 'dzin chen por ma zad phyis su kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bstan srog
mthud pa'i mkhas grub kyi snyan pas gdan sa gong 'og gnyis kyi rigs kyi bdag por bzhes te/ gtsang phyogs su lan kha yar phebs pa'i skabs shig dam pa 'di dang gdan 'dzom
nas bka' gdams lha bzhi'i 'khrid/ sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo/ mi'u thung gsod byed/ zhang blon dang bzhi'i rjes gnang / de dag gi yig cha thor bu'i lung sogs kha yar
gsan cing / slar yang bka' gdams sogs ma gsan pa'i rigs la thugs rtsol gnang bzhed che zhing zur thams cad mkhyen pa chos dbyings rang grol yang spyan snga rin po cher bka'
gdams skor gsan ma thub pa la thugs 'gyod che zhing kho bo'ang de ltar sems mod kyang yid srubs brlang spyod kyi lhongs chen pos gnas nges med du gshegs pa'i 'o brgyal
ba'i chos gegs su gyur te bla ma dam pa rnams kyi thugs bzhed ji bzhin byung ma song / kun mkhyen klu sgrub rgya mtsho dbyangs can mas rjes su

bzung nas shes bya'i gnas mtha' dag la chags thogs mi mnga' zhing khyad par gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad kyi skor la rtsal du bton pa'i bdag chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras
kyi ring lugs srol 'dzin bla na med pa yin rung / sku'i skye ba klu sgrub chos kyi rgyal mtshan du grags pa sprul sku kun snying par thugs dad de log pa'i bshes kyi mthus
rang bstan spel ba'i gong ma'i rnam thar ma 'khyongs kyang ma nas mdo sngags kyi gsan pa rgya cher mdzad cing / khyad par sprul pa'i sku mnga' ris pa chen po dang khri
srong rnam sprul dpal bkra shis stobs rgyal gyis gtsos dam pa du ma'i zhal slob/ bla chen sngags 'chang tshe ring dbang po yongs 'dzin du bsten pas sngags rnying ma'i phyogs
la gsan rgya che gshis snga 'gyur gtso bor bton pa'i zab chos mang du gsan pa ni byang gter rigs 'dzin gdung sgrub kyi chos skor/ gter ston gyi rnam thar/ thugs sgrub
drag po rtsal gyi dbang lung / rdzogs pa chen po rang byung rang shar gyi nyams 'khrid lung bcas/ bka' brgyad rang byung rang shar gyi chos skor/ phur pa che mchog dang
drag sngags gnyis kyi dbang / lugs gsum ga'i lung / lha chen stobs 'dul gyi chos skor/ stag zhon gyi chos skor bka' gter/ zhal chems lung bstan gyi skor/ rdor legs kyi srog
dbang lung bcas/ gter ston bal po a hung gi dzam la nag po'i chos skor/ sprul sku tshe brtan rgyal mtshan gyi bla ma rdo rje 'chang gi dbang lung / yang

gsang yaksha me dpal dbu dgu phyag bco brgyad pa'i dbang lung / gzhan yang las phran thor bu/ kun skyong gling pa'i rdor sems snying thig gi chos skor/ padma las 'brel rtsal
gyi mkha' 'gro snying thig gi dbang lung / padma gling pa'i tshe dpag med rdor phreng gi chos skor gyi lung / phyag rdor dregs 'dul gyi chos skor/ gu ru drag dmar thems
med kyi skor/ ratna'i rta mgrin gsang 'dus kyi chos skor nas thor bu/ bstan gnyis gling pa padma tshe dbang rgyal po'i 'jam dpal gshin rje drag sngags kun 'dus kyi dbang
lung la sogs pas thugs rgyud yongs su gtam/ rje 'di nyid/ glang phu chos rje/ zha lu mkhan rin po che gsum zha lu ri phug dang 'dar du snga phyi rdo rje 'chang gi sku zhabs
su chabs cig par bzhugs nas dam pa'i chos kyi gsan bsam rgya cher mdzad pa'i dus khyed gsum rdo rje'i mched po zla med pa yin pas dbon gyis sa lugs/ glang phu rje drung
gis rnying lugs/ sman khang nas kyis bu lugs rnams gtso bor bton pa'i thos bsam byas pa sogs chos rgyun gcig la med pa rnams gcig gis bsabs pa'i nyan bshad byed dgos zhes
gsungs pa ltar glang phu nas chos rje rin po che 'jam dbyangs chos skyong dbang phyug zhal ngo gong ma rnams kyi dus nas kha'u skyes lhas pa'i ring lugs la dbang rnon
chos rjes 'brang ba'i dad pa brtan pos sbyin bdag lhur len pa'i rgyun dang chos rje nyid sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin chen po 'gran zla med pas chos gsan pa'i yul du gyur pa
nas thog mar chos 'brel ci rigs gsan cing rting sor gsan pa

rags rim smos na bla ma dgongs 'dus kyi chos skor nas nyer mkho dang karma gling pa'i zhi khro dgongs pa rang grol nas thor bu'i lung / bstan gnyis gling pa'i rdzogs chen klong
gsal snyan brgyud kyi chos skor/ 'od gsal thig le nyag gcig gi chos skor/ phag mo zab rgya'i chos skor/ dpyal phur gyi dbang lung / klong chen pa'i bla ma yang tig dang
zab mo yang tig gnyis kyi lung sogs mang du gsan/ rje btsun rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po byang gling bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i yang srid zha lu mkhan chen rin
chen bsod nams mchog grub la rje bla mas tshig bkra'i khyad nas phun tshogs dngos grub ma'i lung zhus phebs pa ltar dang rdor dbyings kyi dbang gsan cing rjes sor rim gyis
thugs rtsol gnang bas 'khor lo sdom chen/ bde mchog /padma dra ba/ dril bu lha lnga/ chos dbyings gsung dbang / dpal mchog rdor sems/ mi 'khrugs pa lha bcu gsum/ phyag
rdor 'chi bdag 'joms pa/ shAkya seng ge gtsug tor dgu pa/ rnam snang mngon byang / phyag rdor 'gro bzang dang bcas pa'i dbang / rnam sras bka' mi 'dra ba bco lnga/ dzam
la dmar po sogs rjes gnang dang lung gi rigs kha yar gsan/ rje rdo rje 'chang dgung lo phebs par ma zad sku gcong gis ma lcogs pa'i gtsang sde srid du dgongs khrol zhu ba
mdzad pa grwa rigs sbyin bdag gi 'dod sbyar bzhin dbon rin po che nang bskos kyi bca' gzhi shar ba dkar po zhes pas sa sbrul gyi lo'i dus tshes dge bar rgyal ba kun

dngos tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i slob bshad 'jigs med seng ge'i rgyud kyi nga ro sgrog pa'i chos kyi khri chen por gdan sa gong dang gzhis ka rtse nas bsko 'ja'i gnang
skyes 'dar nas sogs sbyin bdag grwa rigs rnams kyis 'bul 'gyed tsha ra'i thog rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po dbang phyug rab brtan gyis bkra shis me tog gi char chen po phab nas
mnga' gsol lo/ /lcags mo lug gi lo la stod lho nas sprul sku 'jam dbyangs pa zhes pir thogs dbang po sman thang pa'i slob rgyun mkhas pa zhig bkug nas thams cad mkhyen
pa'i rnam thar zhing bkod thang kha gsum la tshang ba de zhor du gur mgon/ dud sol ma/ las gshin gsum gyi sku brnyan bzhengs te rdo rje 'chang la rab gnas zhu ba mdzad pas
bris bkod phun sum tshogs pa byung zhes dgyes pa'i rtser son 'di gras lcags stag lo skyid shong gung thang du bzhugs yul gnang skabs/ gnyan mgon zhal bzhi pa dang gnod
sbyin beg tse lcam dral gnyis zur kun mkhyen chen pos phyag bris gnang zhing beg tse'i skya bris kyi dus zur chen gyi 'od gsal du dur khrod sogs kyi bkod pa sna tshogs byung
ba mus srad pa'i thang rnying khungs btsun zhig gzigs 'dug pa de kho na ltar snang zhes thugs nges mdzad/ chu pho sprel lo gsol 'debs gnang bas rdo rje 'phreng ba'i dbang
bskur bar zhal gyis 'ches skabs gdan sa 'og gi bdag chen khri thog pa 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i drung
du mkhan rin po che ngag dbang chos grags kyis phreng ba gsan pa'i

gnas tshul byung bar brten bdag rgan po'i dge sbyor bcag pa las rin po che pa sku na gzhon zhing mkhyen pa'i klong yangs pas der zhus shig pa'i skabs dbye ba bka' bzhin sgrub
pa'i ched du grang mo che'i gtsang po byang kha bla brang rdzong du yongs rdzogs gnas lnga rig pa'i paNDi ta chen po thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa'i
zhabs drung nye bar bsnyen te rje btsun rdo rje btsun mo'i gnang ba thob par brten nas slob dpon 'jigs med 'byung gnas zhabs kyis rgyud sde bzhi'i dkyil 'khor mtha' dag
spyi bka'i tshul du dgongs pa bkral ba phreng ba skor gsum mdzad pa dang phyogs mtshungs par slob dpon chen po darpan A tsarYas kr-i yas munytsa mdzad pa gnyis kyi dbang
gi chu bo sa bzang 'phags pa nas gcig tu 'dres pa rdo rje 'chang e waM pa kun dga' bzang po brgyud par bcas pa'i phyag bzhes nyams pa med pa phreng ba zhe lnga ma'i dbang
/ kun rig dang bsrung ba lnga'i dbang / sa skya pa chen po dang slob dpon rin po che'i bka' 'bum/ glang ri thang pas mdzad pa'i blo sbyong gi rtsa ba rin po che rta ra ba'i
rnam thar sngags 'chang nyid kyis mdzad pa sogs snga phyir chos mang du gsan no/ /grangs med 'gro ngor gcig las du ma'i gar/ /snang tshul rgyud sde bzhi yi lhar shar
'ga'/ /lo paN bzhed pa ma nor sgrub mchod srol/ /legs btod snying po'i ring lugs srog gi zungs/ /phag mo'i byin rlabs tsam la dbang bskur du/ /re ba'i dug bral nA ro mai
tri yi/ /bzhed gzhung sman gyi chu bo arga'i rgyun/ /sbreng ba'i rngog ston a gastya yi spun/ /'gro kun bde ba'i dga'

ston la sbyar nas/ /'di phyi'i don gnyis yongs grub bka' gdams kyi/ /zab chos jo 'brom nying khu lha bzhi'i khrid/ /khyod thugs rin chen za ma tog tu bskyil/ /klu sgrub snyan
grags g.yu dmar 'dab 'phreng rgyan/ /sgra 'dzin mun pa'i mal nas slong ba la/ /ltos min snga 'gyur sgron me lam bzang gzugs/ /gzigs la dgyes pa'i zhal 'dzum tshar du dngar/
/'jam dbyangs 'khon ston chos tshul kunda'i tshal/ /skyong la thos bsam sgom par dbang phyug zlas/ /mgon khyod mnyes byed theg mchog mchod pa'i sprin/ /kun bzang rnam
par thar de ngal gsor gyur/ /mtha' klas rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i bang mdzod sgo/ /rnam dpyod yangs pa'i lde mig 'phrul po ches/ /'byed la phur bu'i blor 'gran zha lu pas/
/bzhed pa'i re bkang yongs 'duu sa brtol bzhin/ /tshogs bshad gcan gzan dregs pa'i ngar skad ltar/ /rab gnon slob bu mchog la gdams bya'i 'khrid/ /'jigs med seng ge'i nga
ro sgrog pa'i khrir/ /phyogs bcu'i rgyal bas dbang bskur legs so byin/ /ngag gi dbang phyug dbyangs can ngang mo dkar/ /rab 'byams mkhyen pa'i thugs mtshor rtag rol bas/
/chos phung mgrin pa'i dril chung sgrog pa'i glu/ /len pa'i grags snyan srid pa'i rtse las brgal/ /mtha' yas 'gro khams dang 'tsham thub gsung don/ /'chad mkhas gtam gyi
sbyor ba lag pa'i rjes/ /gtsug lag bye ba'i rtsig par legs bzhag pa'i/ /ri mo mig gsum pas kyang dbye nus min/ /rin chen sgang pa'i gdung brgyud rim byon gyi/ /rang bstan
sa chen gyen du rab bteg pa'i/ /snying stobs khyab 'jug khengs 'phrog yongs 'dzin 'dis/ /yab rje bla ma'i bzhed pa ci yang bkang / /

rje rdo rje 'chang gzhan snang du sku na cher smin cing spyan mi gsal ba sogs nas dpal dI paM kA ra shrI dznyA na dang 'brom ston chos kyi rgyal po dpon slob kyi rnam thar
bzhin yar klungs bkra shis chos sder phebs dgos sogs thugs brel gzhan rnams khyad du bsad de/ bla ma'i sri zhu'i zham 'bring la gal che bar dgongs nas bcar bzhugs gnang ba'i
lo sngon ma rnams su rdo rje 'chang gzhan don du gshegs grabs kha yar byung bar rje 'di nyid kyis gsol 'debs brtan bzhugs gnang bas zhal ngo ma bzlog par bzhugs shing
khyad par pha dam pa lugs kyi 'chi med mgon po'i sgo nas brtan bzhugs 'bul ba gnang bas tshe gtor dgu 'dren sgang la bdud rtsir zhu ba sogs rtags mtshan legs par byung /
chos sde'i grwa pa 'phyos pa 'phrin las rgya mtsho zer ba zhig la sems skyon ma chags rung rje bka' 'gyur ba dbus la phebs par yid gdungs nas rdo rje 'chang la da cha rdo'i
ngos rang yin 'dug yang na ni sku khams gzhi med du gdangs na legs shing / de min zhing gzhan gshegs na zhes gleng mo btang ba byams pas snyan du gsol ba na kho bden
dbon drung gis nan chags gsungs pa ma bzlog par bsdad pa ma gtogs sdod 'dod kyang med cing gzhan don mi nus pa'i lus 'di de ga rang du 'dug gsung chu bya tshes bcu zhig la
rje bla ma phyi rol tu mngon pa'i snyun sogs ye med pa'i ngang nas drung chen byams pa bstan 'dzin par kho bo 'gro ba yin tshul gsungs pa byams pas rje nyid la zhus par
brten drung du phebs shing nan tar gsol 'debs gnang bas zhal gyis bzhes te sku tshe byin gyis

brlabs nas lo gsum bzhugs pa'i bar mtshams su sku cung zad dwangs skabs tshe dbang rjes gnang 'khrid kyi rigs 'ga' gsan cing / rwa pod/ dpal 'dzin pod chung gis mtshon pa'i
lung du ma spyan tshab bcug nas gnang / snyan brgyud zhal bzhes gal che ba'i rigs sogs chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bzhin par bzhugs/ 'jam dbyangs rdo rjes dge slong rab 'dzin
bsad pa'i rkyen gyis rje btsun bka' 'gyur ba shing phag hor zla bcu gcig pa'i nang du dgon pa'i don skor la gzhis ka rtser phebs de dus yar 'brog tu sog po as lang gi dmag
rgyugs pas dbus gtsang thams cad zi chong de ba'i skabs dang 'grig pa'i gtsang sde srid nas sog bzlog la dmigs pa'i sku rim gnang dgos tshul phebs pa ltar mgon po khro
bcu'i gtor bzlog mdzad/ rdzong gi gtor rgyag pa phal cher 'chams sogs spros bcas lhur len cing gzigs mo'i khyad kyis cho ga rdzogs ma rdzogs la mi ltos par gcig rjes su
gcig 'don pa zhig yong 'dug pa drung yig bde rgyas pa 'ongs nas 'don dgos tshul dang 'chams sogs ji tsam yod kyi dri ba byung bar rdo rje slob dpon gyi chas zhugs tsam las
'chams byed kyin med cho ga'ang nyin 'tshams las mi grub 'dug gsungs pas gzhan tsho'i byad las dang ma mthun pas dgongs pa la 'thad rgyu rang ma byung 'dug /'on kyang
chos skyong bran du 'khol ba'i snyan grags la brten mthongs lcags rdzong du sku rim la rdzong bda' gnang ba'i phebs zhor nang so dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i jo jo thar pa'i gnyer
pas gdan drangs kun mkhyen dpyal pa'i gdan sa thar pa dgon gyi rten brten pa rnams zhib mjal

gyi tshe stag zhon yab yum gyi 'chams sku'i zhal ras las bdud rtsi babs/ lo lo bzhin tshogs brgya'i dus 'chams sku phyir 'don khar snum phyis sogs byed dgos pa la de nas lo
shas dgos pa ma byung zer/ 'dar du yul sar nang par byon pa'i stag sna nang pa'i sras mo tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i snag dbon byang sems lags kyis rdo rje 'chang gi
drung du mchi ma dang bcas mthongs lcags rdzong shin tu gnyan pa yod 'dug pas srung 'khor gnang dgos zhus pas de lta bu bsams pa dga' rab yin/ dbon rin po che gzhan dang
mi 'dra bas skyon mi yong gsungs/ mthongs lcags rdzong bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi snyen sgrub las sbyor gnang sa gsang ba'i mgon khang bod yul na gnyan pa der las sbyor
gyi bca' gzhi rnams kyang shin tu 'grig pa nas gsang ba yid bzhin nor bu nas bshad pa ltar gyi mngon spyod rgyas par gnang skabs bdag chen rin po che'i gsol phod re nag dang
dbu zhwa yang mchod cing rdzas la rta dang bya rog gi snying dgos pa ched du gsod pa ma 'gab pa'i rnyed dka' tshe mgon khang steng gi nam mkhar bya rog sder 'dzings byas
pas gcig shi nas lhung ba dang rgyal rtse'i ltag tu mi zhig gi rta nag la glo bur du btsan rgyab ste 'bad med du rnyed gdab las kyi dus sha tshil dri chen spos sogs kyi
dri nges med bsreg mkhan med par 'thul ba dang mgon khang mda'i bar khyams su skad ngan 'khun bu 'don zhing bshug glu len pa sogs tshub cha che bas gsol dpon dang mchod
dpon gcig pur 'gro mi nus pa byung zhing / dmigs bya as lang hung tha'i ji blon po dang bcas pa lo gcig tsam nas nang 'khrugs kyi

dmigs med du song ba'i rtags mtshan che yang rnam shes 'og min du rgyal ba'i sras su bskrun pa rgyud sde'i dgongs pa bla na med pa yin pas/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i gsung
mgur las/ e ma rgyu 'bras rten 'brel dgod re bro/ /dal med sngags smyon 'dren pa'i sngags 'chang la/ /'bad rtsol med par nus mthu shugs la 'byung / /chang 'thung 'ur gog
'thag pa'i sngags 'chang rnams/ /ban ling rnga brdung drag kyang ngal ba'i rgyu/ /zhes pa'i don thog tu khel bar bsam mo/ /'dar du phebs gdul bya rtag par 'dzin pa'i dngos
zhen ldog ste gtan mdun sgrub la brtson pa'i snying stobs kyi go bgo ba dang skal ldan rjes su 'dzin pa'i 'phrin las kyi sgo 'phar zhing khams gzhan du 'byed par dus babs
kyi 'dzin byed ces pa me pho byi ba'i lo smin drug zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi bzang po dang por rta bdun rgyal po nub ri'i phag tu zhugs par nye ba'i tshe zhing brje ba'i
rnam pa bstan pa na rje 'di nyid kyis gsol 'debs shugs drag por mdzad pas spyan hur gyis gzigs nas rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje dang thams cad mkhyen pa gnyis phebs
nas de la rig pa zhugs pa bzhin du bde cham mer yod pa de sang ba zhig byung / sngar khyed kyis nan tan mdzad par brten de tsam bsdad yod da cha de 'dra mdzad nas ci gnang
khyed rang la ltos bcas thams cad rjes su 'dzin zhes zhal gyis 'ches pa ni/ tshar chen gyi gsung mgur las/ lar nga rang tha mal snyoms las can/ /tshe 'di phyi gang 'gro'i
gdengs med kyang / /mi nga la blo gtad byas pa kun/ /pha kun spangs chos rjes mkha' dbyings nas/ /dus rtag tu skyong

ba'i bka' bzhes yod/ /ces gsungs pa'i don dang mthun par snang / gzugs sku chos dbyings su bsdus skabs byams pa'ang gling gseb tu song ba dang 'grig pa'i rje nyid las phyag
g.yog gzhan su'ang med pas mdor phebs te sgrub rnying slob dpon 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan rdo rje 'chang gi sku ber gyi gong ba la 'dra sku 'dri yin yod snang bar skor cig
las mtshams zhog la byams pa bos shog gsungs/ de'ang dam pa gang de/ ma pham pas/ /de bzhin 'khor ba ji srid bar/ /las ni rgyun mi 'chad par 'dod/ /ces gsungs pa dang
mthun par dam pa'i chos kyi 'phrin las nam mkha'i mtha' ltar mnyam mod/ mchod sbyin brgya phrag gcig gis lha'i bdag por 'gyur ba bzhin tshe rabs gzhan du sbyin shugs kyi
'bras bu tshe 'dir smin par blun po rnams kyi ngor 'phrin las 'phrin las zhes 'bod pa'i chen por grags pa rnams dang mtshungs pa'i 'byor pa mi mnga' na'ang bla chung 'gam
khums 'jungs pa'i ngang tshul can ci rigs ltar bre gsog phul gsog mdzad na de 'drar ma ltos pa'i dad 'bul la brten phyag rdzas 'khyil yong tshod du snang yang / thams cad
mkhyen pa'i gsung mgur du/ nor longs spyod 'bad pas bsags na yang / /tshe phyi mar mi phan lus sems sdug /de bsags pa snying po ma mchis kyi/ /da zas nor ci yod gang dgar
zhog /ces snying po med pa dang / chos thams cad sgyu ma lta bur gzigs pas 'dod sred kyi 'ching ba dang bral te dkon mchog gi mchod pa dang dbul phongs la gtong ba sogs
'phral dag mdzad pa'i gshis/ yab sras gnyis kar gnang bde'i bdog

pa'i mthu dman pas dgongs rdzogs kyi mthun rkyen sgrub rtsol khyad zhag bdun bar gsang ba'i tshul mdzad/ zhag gcig gi bar 'od gsal gyi ngang du mnyam par bzhag nas mkha' spyod
rdo rje btsun mo'i zhing du gshegs pa'i gdung yid bzhin gyi nor bu gdan gsum tshang ba'i rdo rje slob dpon dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bor gyur par/ dngos
su bshams pa dang yid kyis sprul pa'i phyi nang gsang ba de kho na nyid kyi mchod pa kun tu bzang po'i rnam par thar pa bzhin nam mkha' mdzod kyi sgo 'phar yongs su phye
ste bsod nams kyi tshogs rlabs po che bskrun pa'i mchod pa sna lnga brgya rtsa tshar re nyin zhag rer brje dgos la grogs gzhan med pas bla ma 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan
gnyid log long med pa lta bu byung skad/ grang mo cher kye rdor man ngag lugs dang rdo rje 'jigs byed/ 'dar bsam grub dgon gsar bas kun rig /mang mkhar cha lung pas padma
yang gsang khros pa/ shing mangs pas dpal mo lugs kyi thugs rje chen po rnams kyi chog grwa zhag bdun gyi bar btsugs/ gnas de gar dge 'dun 'dus pa'i ser tshogs kyi gral
dbur yongs rdzogs gnas lnga rig pa'i paNDi ta mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags gdan drangs pa'i mang ja/ 'bul 'gyed/ tsha ra sogs kyis bsnyen bkur/ nye skor phu mda' bar
gsum gyi skye bo'i tshogs la rtsam nas snam ras zangs lcags khro ja mar rta drel gyis mtshon pa'i zang zing gi bdog pas tshim par mdzad/ hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i tshes brgyad
kyi mtshan mo'i char kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi dkyil 'khor zhal phye nas rje btsun nyid kyis phyag dar te sku gdung rin

po che dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bo dang tha mi dad par mchod pa'i tshul du zhugs su phul ba'i tshe ye shes kyi me rang 'bar zhing sang nyin lha rnams kyis mchod pa'i phyir me tog
gi char dang 'ja' tshon sna lnga'i gur khyim za 'og ris su phub pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i cho 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab par mchis/ de nas gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar
phebs te bzhi thog tu khri rin po che 'jam mgon grub pa'i dpa' bo ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang por thugs dam 'dogs rten/ chos
dung dkar po rgyang grags btang ba'i dge 'dun tshogs chen la mang 'gyed/ lha khang tshor mchod pa snyan shal bzabs rgyas dang bcas rdo rje slob dpon dpal ldan bla ma
dam pa bstan 'gro'i phan bde rlabs po che bskrun par mdzad bzhed kyi smon lam gyi rgyas 'debs/ mgon khang rnams su mchod gtor bskang bshags bstod 'phrin rgyas par gnang ba'i
dam bsgrags shing khyad par bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes kyi dbu dpral nas zil pa khrom khrom byung ba je 'phel du song ba shangs rtser babs pa zhal du mchod cing sku 'khor
ba byams pa/ mkhan chen gzhon nu blo gros kyi snag dbon nang so dge 'dun rgya mtsho/ mchod dpon gsum la gnang ba zas gang dang yang mi 'dra ba'i zhim la bcud che ba
dri bzang chags pa byung zhing de'i shar g.yu thog tu bzhugs pa'i mgon po'i sku las bdud rtsi'i rgyun gong dang 'dra/ sa bzang sku 'bum mchod khang na mgon po'i sku thal
ba'i rdul gyis cher gos pa'i lta snang mi spro ba zhig la snyan dar 'bul grabs mdzad pa'i tshe sku 'khor

ba 'dras 'di la phul nas ci gnang zhus par ye shes pa gang na bzhugs mi shes zhes lha gos sgron pa dang dus mnyam du bdud rtsi babs pa gsum ga mchod dpon 'jam dbyangs rgyal
mtshan gyis thog mar ngos zin/ bdud rtsi babs par blo chung ba rnams ya mtshan gyi gnas su byed na'ang sku tshe mang por chos skyong bran du 'khol bar ma zad gsang rten
lus la sba ba'i rnal 'byor dang ldan na dam can grib ma bzhin 'khor bar dpal brtse ba chen po la dgag mkhan med pa'i dbu snyung bzhes par dpags na mtshar 'dzin gyi chen por
mi sems so/ /kha'u skyes lhas su phebs skabs dgon pa'i 'og tsam du chibs gshol nas spyan nam mkha' la hur rer gzigs te rgyang tsam bzhugs pa 'phral du 'di yin mi gsung
yang rjes su rdo ring rin po che man chad kyi bla ma rnams phebs dus gnyan mgon bram ze'i gzugs kyi bsu ba re nges par byung 'dug ces drung du 'khod par bka' stsal ba la
dpags na de dus gzigs snang khyad par can byung ba gor ma chag /skyes lhas kyi dge 'dun rnams la sger du mang ja mi rer zhal 'gyed/ rten gyi tshogs la mchod pa snyan shal
bskang ba 'phrin bcol dam bsgrags/ zhabs drung bdag chen rin po che mjal zhing dgyes pa'i gsung gleng mang du stsal/ bka' chos kyi snyan gsan gnang bas 'thum nad las grol
nas yun ring tsam song rung dpon tshang rnams kyis skor cig dpe lta sogs mi 'gab zer bas da lam mi thub 'dug slar long dang bstun pa'i byed ces dgyes pa'i zhal gyis bzhes/
zha lur mang ja tsha ra dang / ngor e

waM chos ldan gtso bor gyur pa'i sa lugs dang / gzhan yang grub mtha' ris med rags bsdus dbus gtsang gi sde dgon mang dag la mang ja bsngo rten rgya cher spel/ rje rdo rje
'chang zhi ba'i dbyings su gzhol bar nye tshe sku cung zad hreb pa'i tshul bstan par nyin mtshan kun tu skyo ngal med par gnang bas thugs dam chag med rnams la thang lhod
ci rigs byung bar brten me glang dbus su phebs zhor ngor e waM chos ldan du mkhan chen thar pa rtse ba nam mkha' sangs rgyas la lam dus sogs chag med gso ba mdzad/ rim gyis
yar klungs bkra shis chos sder phebs nas rtse tshogs/ rtses dang sa dge /dkon gnyer phyi nang / ri bo chos gling / bkra shis chos sde/ lam rim/ bkra shis bde chen/ ras
chung phug sogs kyi ser tshogs gral dbur thub bstan rdo rje brag nas dus gsum sangs rgyas dpal o rgyan chen po'i rgyal tshab byang pa ngag dbang rigs 'dzin rdo rje chos
rgyal bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po spyan drangs 'bul 'gyed mang ja tsha ra la brten pa'i rnyed bkur yang dag bsgrubs/ rigs 'dzin ngag gi dbang po'i drung du rdo
rje drag po rtsal gyi byin rlabs thugs dbang / lcags sdong ma dang tshe gur sbrags ma/ nyang gi drag po me'i spu gri rnams kyi dbang / rigs 'dzin chen po'i 'khor ba dbyings
sgrol gyi chos skor/ gu ru yon tan gter mdzod kyi dbang lung / sngags sdebs snying gzer nag po dang gter ston brgya rtsa'i gsol 'debs kyi lung / gru gu yang waM gi 'joms
byed nyi zla nag po'i chos skor/ padma gling pa'i gur phur zhabs can dang raksha'i zhal

gzi ldan dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs/ gdong bzhi pa'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi lung sogs snga phyir dam pa'i chos kyi bka' drin mang du gsan par gnang / dgongs pa rin po che
chos kyi dbyings su rdzogs pa dang phyi rabs gdul bya rnams kyi legs byas rgya mtsho'i zhing gi ched du e nas sprul sku mkhas pa chos 'phel can lnga bkug ste bzo gra btsugs
shing rdo rje 'chang gi sku tshab mgul pa yan rje bla ma dam pas phyag bzo gnang bas zhal khyim mngon sum lta bu mthong thos dran dang reg pas rnam par grol ba'i byin
rlabs kyi gzi byin 'od du 'bar ba gtso bor bzhugs pa'i mtha' skor du sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje bdag med ma/ grub chen bi rU pa/ brtse chen snying po'i zhabs/
slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa/ tshogs sgom rin po che/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/
dpal ldan bla ma dam pa/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun
kha'u pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /mtshungs med gzhon nu blo gros/ mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan bar gyi
lam zab brgyud pa'i snang brnyan gyi zhal khyim bzo bos dpe ma lon pa mi 'phyugs pa'i khyad nas phyag sor gyis bskrun pa dang bcas par gnas chen du ma'i sa sna rdo sna/
dam rdzas khyad par can/ sman sna/ dar sna sogs bsres pa'i sku rgyu la byad dbyibs bgres gzhon bzhugs stangs na bza' kha dog rnams dpe khungs btsun dang gsung rgyun las
byung ba ltar la de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'phel gdung gis gtsos yungs 'bru lta bu'i ring bsrel/ bla ma gong ma de dag gis mtshon pa'i dam pa du ma'i sku bal dang sku gdung gi
ring bsrel/ rgyud sde rnam bzhi'i gzungs chos sku'i ring bsrel gnod sbyin 'khor lo sogs gzungs bzhugs kyi rim pa rten bzhengs so byas so pa'i 'jig rten chos brgyad lhur
len pa dang mi 'dra bar dam pa'i phyag bzhes 'khrul pa med par thugs ru shin tu nga ba rnams kyi bzhugs khri na bza'/ mdun lcog /cang te/ rdor dril/ nang mchod ka pA la/
bum pa/ zhal dkar/ spyi blugs/ bzed zhal sogs rung mthun mkho ba'i yo byad rnams sla chos su ma song ba'i legs par bsgrig pa gnang ste bkra shis chos kyi 'dus gra chen por
lam zab bla ma lha khang ngo mtshar ba grub par gnyis su med pa dpal dgyes mdzad rdo rje man ngag lugs lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor dang rjes su 'brel ba'i rab gnas nyin gsum
ma'i sgo nas 'og min zhing khams rgya mtsho nas ye shes pa ganggA'i klung gis bgrang bar mi nus pa spyan drangs te dam tshig pa dang ro gcig tu brlabs pa de'i tshe 'chi
med kyi lam kun gur gyi dbyibs lta bu'i 'ja' ris sna lnga bkrag tu 'tsher zhing gsol gdab sems bskyed kyi dus me tog gi char babs pa thams cad kyi mngon sum pa'i spyod yul
du gyur/ bzo bo rnams kyang yon gyis tshim pa sogs lha mchod mi mchod rgyas par mdzad/ sa stag hor zla bcu gcig pa'i dmar chen gtor bzlog gi rdo rje slob dpon du phebs
skabs dge slong ye shes blo gros kyi mthong snang la/ gsol lcog gi khar skra lo dang kong rna btags pa'i

mgo zhig mi nag po zhig gis khyer nas bzhag song ba ring por ma lon par sde ba'i nang zan chos sder shin tu brnag pa/ khyab 'jug gza'i gdong thug gis skad cig la 'jig rten
pha rol tu song ba'i mi nag po de ni 'chi bdag gshin rje'i rgyal po pu tra nag por nges so/ /dwags po phyogs su bkag po'i zi bun la brten pa'i 'khrug zing cher song ba gra
dol yar klungs lho byang gi dmag dpon bkras sgang nas kyis byas nas phyin skabs sde pa bkra shis rtse pa'i sku rim du 'jam dpal gshin rje dmar po rlung sgrub kyi dgra mnan
gyi las sbyor bzhis kar gnang ba'i tshe gtor ma las khrag rgyun mang du 'dzags pas lcags slang khengs shing mchod dpon 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan gyi rmi lam du sa dong
ring por srog chags mang po 'jug pa dang 'gro ba rmis tshul zhus pa na las sbyor 'di rigs la rmi ltas de bzhin 'ong gsung / nub cig stob pa'i gtor ma phul dus mchod dpon
gyi rgyab dang mdun steng du gzugs mi mthong ba'i hab sha /cag cag /shab be shob be sogs kyi sgra thos pas 'jigs zhum zhum byed pa sogs ltas legs pa/ brag kha ba'i dmag
dpon skyer po gong 'og gis mtshon shor thal che ba byung yang bkra shis rtse ba dpon g.yog nyes skyon med pa'i dge mtshan du gyur/ rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal dus kyi 'khor
lo rwa 'bro shong gsum gyi 'gyur dang jo zhal sogs mkhas pa du ma'i bzhed srol mang ba'i nang nas gtso bor gyur pa rtsod dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa thams cad mkhyen pa bu
ston rin po che'i yig cha sor bzhag gi dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod 'dzugs par bzhed de sa yos hor zla dang por dpe rnams grwa pa tshor bkram pa'i blo 'dzin byed du bcug /zha
lu nas bla chen mkhyen rab pa bos pa'i dpon slob tshang mas gar thig sbyong bstar gnang / rjes sor slob dpon 'phel khyad nas deng sang gi sgrub rnying bla ma 'jam dbyangs
rgyal mtshan/ gzims khang shar bla ma dpal ldan rgyal mtshan/ nang so tshe 'phel gsum yang bskyar sbyong bdar byed du 'jug pa mdzad/ gar pa nyi shu'i gar gos/ pang khebs/
rus rgyan/ skra zhwa/ rtse phran/ rdo dril/ bsdus rgyud kyi bshad khungs dang 'brel ba'i rnam bum che legs bcu rnams thugs rtsol ba chen pos legs par bsgrig par gnang ste
grwa pa rnams sku gsung thugs yongs su rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor du smin par mdzad nas nam mthongs zla ba phyi ma snron gyis nya ba'i dus tshes gza' skar sbyor byed bzang
por btsugs pa'i sa gar gyi skabs rje nyid gar dpon du phebs pa'i sku rgyab kyi bar snang la yi ge dbu can gyi tshigs bcad 'dug pa zha lu bla chen gyis mthong zhing blor
zin na'ang rjes su ma dran/ sbyin sreg gnang ba'i sar mchod gar ba rnams 'gros dang bcas 'byor pa dang dus mnyam du nam mkha' g.ya' dag pa las me tog gi char babs/ zhag
sbrel gyi bar dpal ldan rgyu skar gyi 'khor lo'i gtso bor khyab bdag bla ma dbang phyug rab brtan bzhugs par sgrub mchod kyi dga' ston cha bsags kyi grong khyer la 'gran
par gyur/ 'di lo grabs gshoms stabs kyis snron zlar mdzad kyang lo phyi ma nas nag zlar btsugs so/ /e nas dpon yig mkhas pa kha shas bkug nas mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen
pa tshar pa chos rje'i gsung 'bum po ti bzhi/ bkra shis rtse'i dpon sa dbang 'dus rgyal mos sbyin bdag mdzad

de 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi gsung 'bum gsar bsgrigs kyi glegs bam gsum dang rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyi bka' 'bum pusta kaHgcig rnams bstan pa
rin po che'i btsas su dgongs te bla ma gong ma rnams kyi bka' bsdu'i tshul du legs par bsgrub par gnang ngo / /zhing mang skal ldan don la dgyes pa'i zhal/ /'dzum pa'i
gzugs brnyan sdud la nyer gzhol tshe/ /gsol ba'i re skongs 'ja' lus rdo rje'i sku/ /grub de lhar bcas 'gro la ston pa bzhin/ /spur rgyal bde 'phrog chom rkun du ruShka/ /sde

sku mngon gyur kyang / /rtag 'dzin srid zhen 'ching rgya las grol ched/ /rtag min zhing 'dir mdzad pa'i mtha' btul yang / /rtag tu phyogs 'di'i bstan 'gror gcig tu brtse/

su/ /'brangs te rigs kyi bdag por thod du bcings/ /mkhas grub gzhan gyi spyod yul ma gyur pa/ /sa skya'i bla chen kho na'i khyad par chos/ /lam zab bka' babs brgyud pa

mgon du bzhengs pa'i rdo rje'i 'gros/ /tshangs pa'i yul sa sor mo'i rdul gyis gnon/ /dus gsum 'dren pa gsung gi yang snying dpyid/ /brjod pa rnam dag ka 'phreng glegs bam
du/ /legs bsdus srid mthar rma med bstan pa'i srog /btsugs pas 'od srungs bgres po'i snyan pa phrogs/ /re zhig gdan sar stan chags mur gnyug mar gnas pa dang phyogs 'dus

bstan par 'phel 'grib cher byung mod kyi theg pa chen po gsang sngags ni deng sang gi bar nub ma myong zhes

gsung pa glang dar gyi bstan pa bsnubs zhes pa'ang so thar la dgongs pas/ ji skad du/ ji ltar 'di ni shing rtsa'i gtso bo ste/ /rnam par 'phel dang kun 'dzin gnyis kyi rgyu/
/de bzhin dam chos tshogs rnams thams cad kyi/ /gzhi dang rtsa ba 'dul ba yin par gsungs/ /zhes thub pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi ring lugs 'jig rten gsum gyi sgron
me yod med chos 'dul ba la rag las shing lhag tu dam pa 'di nyid tshul khrims mig gi 'bras bu ltar gces par 'dzin pas snga mo nas lung sde bzhi gsan bzhed yod pa ltar sna
