dkar rdo rje gdan gyi chos grwa chen po'i dpal 'byor gling du khu ston ngag dbang rnam rgyal la 'dul ba lung sde bzhi dang gzhan yang chos bka' ci rigs gsan cing snga
phyi mang por nyi ma gling du mthu ston 'jigs med dpa' bo'i ring lugs 'dzin pa la 'gran zla med pa mkhas btsun grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po bla chen tshul khrims bkra shis
par dus kyi 'khor lo'i sku gsung thugs yongs su rdzogs pa'i dbang gong dkar ba'i lugs kyi lam 'bras kyi 'khrid yongs rdzogs/ byin rlabs dang lung kha shas/ lam skor phyi
ma'i lung / yi ge med pa dang mchod rten drung thob kyi byin rlabs/ yo ga khams gsum rnam rgyal/ dpal mchog rigs bsdus/ rdor dbyings phreng ba'i nang gi bdud rtsi gsum/
sa phur stod las gsum gyi dbang / smad las drag po sgrol ba'i rjes gnang paN chen kun bkras par bde chen ral gcig /rdo rje rtse mo rigs bsdus kyi dbang sogs zab chos rgya
che bas thugs kyi bum bzang yongs su gang bar mdzad/ slar yang bkra shis chos sder phebs/ de'ang bstan pa spyi dang bye brag rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa dang ston
pa las gzhan du mi 'tshol ba'i thugs kyi dam bca' brtan po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i lam yig tu/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po dang mjal nas gsung ngag rin po che thob
pa man gzhan bla ma dang gdams ngag gang la'ang byang chub sgrub pa'i ched du mi smon zhing 'gram chu mi ldang ba'i nges shes gting tshugs pa zhig yod/ ces gsungs pa
ltar 'gyur ba'i go skabs ga la srid kyang / rje btsun grol mchog gis/ dam chos kun gdul bya'i blo brid las/ /phyogs 'dzin gyi grub mtha' skyong ma myong / /chos du ma ro
gcig gi rnal 'byor pa/ /grub mtha' rkang ma tshugs zer kyang 'gyod rgyu med/ /ces pa bzhin bdag cag gi ston pas kyang la lar gang zag gi bdag yod par bstan pa sogs gdul bya
rjes su 'dzin pa la thabs sna tshogs shig dgos pas ris med pa'i chos lugs la gsan bsam 'chad nyan mdzad pa'ang gdul bya rjes su 'dzin par dgongs shing khyad par/ kun mkhyen
mkhyen brtse'i gsung mgur las/ ngas sbyangs pa de sa skya pa'i gzhung lugs la sbyangs kyang / /mkhas pa de gsang sngags rnying ma la mkhas pa/ /'di ko sngon gyi las
'phro zhig yin nam/ /a ho ngo mtshar du che byung / /ngas bsgoms pa de gsung ngag lam 'bras bsgoms kyang / /rtogs pa de rdzogs pa chen po la shar ba/ /'di ko sngon gyi las
'phro zhig yin nam/ /a ho ngo mtshar du che byung / /ngas gsol ba de rnal 'byor dbang phyug la btab kyang

/ /byin rlabs de ayon padma khos gnang ba/ /'di ko sngon gyi las 'phro zhig yin nam/ /a ho ngo mtshar du che byung / /ngas bshad pa de dam chos phyogs med cig bshad kyang /
/'gro phan de gsang sngags rnying ma la byung ba/ /'di ko sngon gyi las 'phro zhig yin nam/ /a ho ngo mtshar du che byung / /zhes gsungs pa blo chung ci rigs kyi khong bar
mi shong yang 'khon klu dbang srungs nas dkon cog rgyal po yan la rnying ma bka' ma'i sngags 'chang sha stag tu byon zhing / de nas kyang yi dam yang phur dang chos skyong
dkar bdud la mdzad la/ mnyam med bsam gtan gling pa'i a ti yang phur gyi rdzogs rim khyad par can dang rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po'i sku thog tu'ang rnying ma ba'i
sngags 'chang 'ja' lus grub pa gnyis tsam byung tshul bla chen ru thog pa nam mkha' gzi brjid kyis gsungs pa ltar tshar chen yab sras bka' gter chos kyi gnad mkhyen pa'i
thugs gtsigs che tsam gnang ba'i rgyun bzhin rje bla ma 'di nyid kyis kyang klu sgrub rjer gsan pa tsam du ma zad nyang ting 'dzin bzang po dang mnga' bdag nyi ma 'od zer
sogs grub brnyes nyang rigs stod smad mang por gyes pa'i nyang ston sman lung pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i gdung rigs las son cing bla ma mnga' bdag gi byang las kyi mkha' 'gro'i
bka' babs gnyos zhig chen po nas rim brgyud khra tshang pa'i snag dpon rje khyab bdag blo mchog rig pa'i rdo rje zhes paN chen bi mA la mi tra'i sprul par lung gis zin
pa de la gter kha 'og ma bla ma yongs rdzogs kyi dbang lung / bka' brgyad gsang ba yongs rdzogs kyi chos skor/ rta mgrin dbu dgu phyag bco brgyad pa'i sgrub skor/ rta
mgrin nag po lcags ral can gyi dbang lung / 'char ka gnam skas ma'i sgrub skor/ thugs sgrub dregs pa tshar gcod du grags pa'i drag dmar gyi dbang lung / phyag rdor gtum po'i
seng ge sgra sgrog gi dbang lung / dregs pa dbu dgu'i srog dbang lung bcas/ dzam bha la dmar po'i chos skor/ gra pa'i 'dzam dmar gyi sgrub skor/ dung tsho ras pa'i rdzogs
chen yang ti nag po gser gyi 'bru gcig ma'i dbang lung khrid bcas/ ratna gling pa'i thugs sgrub yang snying 'dus pa'i dbang lung / gu ru drag po'i dbang che 'bring chung
gsum sgrub skor lung bcas/ nyang gi bla ma dmar 'khrid kyi chos skor/ gter rgyud snying po'i dbang lung / rta mgrin nag chung lha brgyad kyi dbang lung / snang rtse
ba'i rta nag gi dbang lung / gdugs dkar lha bcu bdun ma'i dbang / pha dam pa'i 'jam dbyangs chos skor/ sgrol ma'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad dang mthun pa'i rjes gnang / 'khrungs
rabs so bzhi pa'i lung sogs mang du gsan/ chos dbang rin po che'i gdung 'dzin lha bro sprul sku karma gu ru zhes lo chen bai ro tsa na'i sprul par lung gis zin cing
bka' gter chos kyi srog shing chen po gang de'i gdams pa'i bka' babs sgrub mchog chos dbang bsam grub kyi gdams pas thugs rgyud yongs su gang ba'i mthus srid pa'i phun
tshogs mtha' dag chu shing gi 'bras bu dang me 'obs lta bur gzigs nas chos brgyad kyi bun long thams cad rgyab tu bskyur te bas mtha'i dben gnas su lhun grub snang ba bzhi
khor yug tu 'da' ba'i mtshungs med chos dbang kun bzang la chos dbang gi bla ma gsang 'dus kyi dbang lung /

bla ma sku gsum gyi sgrub pa/ padma lam zab kyi gu ru khro bo rigs gsum gyi dbang lung / tshe dpag med rdzong chen ma'i tshe dbang / rdzogs chen sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi
chos skor/ thugs rje chen po yang snying 'dus pa'i dbang lung / rta mgrin nag po'i dbang lung / bla ma gsang 'dus kyi cha rkyen padma bcud bsdus kyi chos skor don tshan
bcu gnyis pa/ dpal mgon ma ning gi chos skor/ mnga' ris paN chen padma dbang rgyal gyi padma snying tig gi chos skor/ rdzogs pa chen po kun bzang snying tig gi chos skor/
rdzogs pa chen po'i rgyud bcu bdun sogs kyis mtshon pa'i zab chos mang du gsan/ gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir bstan pa dbu bsnyengs pa'i gnas chen pho brang yum bu bla mkhar
mjal bar phebs te/ chos rgyal tho tho ri snyan shal gyi mkhar byin rlabs can der bstan pa rgyas pa'i phyag mchod smon lam mdzad zhol der tshal dus bzhengs pa'i gyang logs
shig la mgon po gur gyi bal bris rnying pa byin rlabs can zhig yod par 'di babs chags shing zil che zhes snyan shal sgron pa'i tshe de 'phral zhal nas bdud rtsi zil pa
khrom khrom byung ba'i shul da lta yang yod/ de'i shar phyogs kyi bang so der gter mang po yod pa 'dra zhes gzigs rtog gnang bas gyang hrab tsam brkos shul gyi steng na g.yam
pa'i gnam sgo zhig 'dug par phyag reg pas khrol khrol byed par 'di rdo gas na gter yod nges rung re zhig gzhog gsungs pa zham 'bring pa sogs der yod thams cad kyis nges
shes su gyur na'ang rjes su bltas pas shul tsam yang ma byung snang / bstan pa spyi sgos kyi ched du 'jigs byed drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog gnang / skabs shig gzims chung
gi nang sha chen gyi gsur dud chen pos khengs pa bka' las khyod tshos sha bsregs pa'i dris nga'i gre ba 'gags gsungs par mchod dpon gyi nged tsho'i khrod na bsreg mkhan
med gzims chung nang rang nas dri ma byung zhus pas cang mi gsung / de nub bla brang thog nas gtor ma 'phen pa gnang bas sman lung gi mda' na chos sde la shin tu brnag pa'i
ma rungs pa zhig yod pa de srod 'khor la grir gum/ bla brang gi rgyab tu sngar nas btsan zhig yod pa gtor zor babs pa dpal ldan dus kyi dgra bo'i gzi byin ma bzod par
sne mo khang gsar gyi rgya lam mkhar spos pa da lta'ang yod do/ /chags bral tshangs par spyod kyang 'dod yon kun/ /lam byed rdo rje gdan mtshungs chos kyi sder/ /thub bstan
dgongs pa gcig pa'i 'gal med gar/ /bsgyur tshe klu sgrub snying po gzugs gzhan bzung / /dpal ldan chos kyi 'byor pa gling yangs por/ /khu ston smra la ngag gi dbang phyug
pa/ /rnam dpyod yid bzhin rgyal mtshan rtser bkod las/ /sde bzhi'i lung gi 'dod rgu char du bsnyil/ /tshul ldan khrims gnas mkhyen pa'i lha lam ngos/ /smin grol gzhung
bshad 'ja' tshon rab bkra ba/ /shis brjod glu yi nyi mas yongs khyab pa'i/ /gling 'dir nges gsang bstan pa'i bdag por bskos/ /gzhom med blo mchog yangs pa rdo rje'i khams/
/rnam dpyod g.yas 'khyil mgrin las legs bshad sgra/ /'dren pa'i snyan gyi dbang por ches dngar bas/ /dbyangs bdun tshang ba'i glu la yi rang bcad/ /chos brgyad tsha zer
spangs pa'i rta ldan snar/ /kun bzang chos kyi sa bon yongs zhugs 'bras/ /'od gsal snang bzhi'i lus rdzogs

tha skar skyes/ /'jam mgon mtho ris dbang po'i blo yi sman/ /gangs can 'dzin ma'i mngal du bstan pa'i dbu/ /thog ma sbrums pa'i pho brang yum bu ru/ /kun yid tshar du mngar
ba'i brjod pa'i mtha'/ /'tshol la khyab 'jug gom pas ma bgrod ngal/ /ris bral 'gro la rang bde gtong nus pa'i/ /rgyal sras spyod la bslab pa'i sems dpa' che/ /khrag 'thung
ye shes rdo rje'i mtshon rnon pos/ /brtse med dgra bgegs don snying 'bigs 'di ci/ /hor zla drug pa'i nang du chibs kha bskyod de gong dkar rdo rje gdan gyi lha gling spyil
por phyi rol rnam par g.yeng ba'i 'du 'dzi thams cad rgyang du bsrings nas sku gsung thugs lha sngags ye shes kyi rol pas khor yug tu 'da' ba'i bcad rgya zla ba brgyad
kyi ring mdzad pa'i skabs dam bca'i phyag bris su gnang ba sku'i bkod pa bsdus rjes rnyed pa las 'di ltar/ oM bde legs su gyur cig /rang byung lhun grub ye shes khyab
brdal las/ /ma 'gags rang rtsal sprul pa'i sku ru byon/ /'gro ba kun gyi skyabs gcig padma 'byung / /khyad par bdag gi 'di phyi'i mgon gcig pu/ /khyed la gsol 'debs snying
nas skyabs su mchi/ /rgyal ba gang de'i ye shes rnam rol las/ /sprul pa'i zlos gar bshes gnyen dam pa'i tshul/ /mdo sngags gsar rnying bka' gter ma lus pa/ /nyi ltar gsal
mdzad mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mkhyen/ /de yi rdo rje ye shes rnam gsum gyis/ /bskrun pa'i rgyal tshab grub dbang rdo rje 'chang / /bka' drin mnyam med dbang phyug rab
brtan gyi/ /zhabs la phyag 'tshal gsol 'debs skyabs su mchi/ /chos dbyings bde chen mtha' bral ngang nyid las/ /gang 'dul thabs kyis 'gro ba rjes gzung phyir/ /zhi dang
khro dang zhi ma khro yi tshul/ /rab 'byams lha tshogs bdag gis bsnyen cing sgrub/ /rdo rje 'chang dbang thugs las rnam sprul pa'i/ /rgyal ba'i bstan srung ma rungs tshar
gcod pa/ /drag shul mthu ldan dam can tshogs rnams kyis/ /byang chub bsgrub pa'i grogs mdzod bar chad sol/ /ji ltar 'dab bzang dbang po mkha' la bgrod/ /de la 'gran min
nyam chung bung ba'i tshogs/ /rang rtsal 'bad nas nam mkhar 'phur ba ltar/ /sngon byon dam pa rnams la 'gran min yang / /rang nyid 'khor ba'i 'dam las rab brgal nas/ /ma
rgan 'gro ba smin grol la 'god phyir/ /dam pa'i rjes zhugs go cha cher gyon nas/ /nyon mongs dgra tshogs g.yul las rnam rgyal te/ /sku bzhi'i rgyal srid 'thob phyir ngas
'dir 'bad/ /de la 'a zha'i rgyal rigs las byung ba'i btsun pa mkhas grub dam pa mang po'i dbon du gyur cing rjes su bzung ba/ dam pa'i chos tshul mang du thos pa/ rgyu
'bras kyi chos la bden pa'i dad pa thob pa/ bla ma rgyal ba sras dang bcas pa la mi phyed dad pas phyug pa ming gnas gsar dbon po mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan zhes bgyi ba
bdag yongs 'dzin bla ma mang pos thugs rjes su bskyangs pa'i dbang 'khrid gdams pa mang du thob kyang rang nyid kyi rgyud la ni ma 'byor/ lung rtogs dang sbyangs pa'i yon
tan ni med/ shes rab dang brtson 'grus ni zhan/ dka' spyad sdug rus ni chungs/ le lo dang snyoms las ni che/ sbyin stobs dang bsgoms stobs ni nyung / gnyid rmugs dang
rnam g.yeng ni mang / de la sogs pa'i skyon dang nyes pa ni brjod pas mi lang / yon tan dang dge ba ni btsal

bas mi rnyed pa'i tshod tsam du 'dug /mi tshe ni phyed lhag song 'dug /'tshang rgya bar ni spu tsam mi nye ba'i khar nyes ltung mang po zhig gis mar la en tsam nye ru song
'dug snyam pa'i blo la bde ba'i skabs ma byung bas slar yang yang bsams pas mtshams med byas pa'i sdig pa che yang gsang sngags kyi gnad gsang shes na myur du 'tshang rgya
bar gsungs 'dug /snying rus dang ldan na zla ba drug rtse gcig bsgoms pas phung po lhag med 'grub par yang gsungs/ tshul bzhin du bsgoms na zhag bdun gyis bden pa mthong
bar dus 'khor las gsungs pa sogs kyis spro ba slar rnyed/ da cha rang lo so brgyad pa 'brug lo zla ba dang po nas bzung ji srid 'tsho'i bar tshe 'di'i bde skyid snyan grags
ched du mi sgrub zas ster mi byung na byol nyog tu ma song bar longs spyod/ ma byung na bcud len la sogs pa'i ngan ngon la brten/ gos ster mi byung na gyon/ ma byung
na'ang chos gos rnam gsum ngan rnyigs dang gtum mo la brten pa byed/ chos bka' gter mdo sngags rnam dag zhu sa gang na yod kyang zhu/ khyad par khe dang rgyal kha gzhan
la bskur zhing / gyong rang gis len pa gang yong yong byed/ lhag par lha'i bsnyen pa rigs mi gcig pa brgya phrag byed/ rtags dang mtshan ma yong re med kyang grangs bsnyen/
dus bsnyen/ gtso 'bum/ 'khor khrir longs pa brgya phrag gcig lo zhe dgu tshun la grub pa bgyid/ de nas kyang ma shi na ci 'grub byed/ de dag gi khas len dang dam bca'
la rta ri ba dang nyams len lag thog yod pa la khyi mi ri ba byung gi dogs 'dug pas yang yang zhus dag byed/ grub na khengs rloms spangs te chos chos su song ba byed/ de
dag 'grub ma 'grub blta phyir yi ge bris pa yin/ sprang ban bdag gi dam bca'i tshig 'di dag /byas byung yi ger 'dri ba'ang mi 'os mod/ /'on kyang khengs dregs bzang 'dod
ma yin pa'i/ /ma 'grub tshe na rang la rang khrel 'debs/ /tshul bzhin 'grub na zhen med dga' ba sgom/ /des na bla ma yi dam chos skyong tshogs/ /bdag gi dam bca' tshul bzhin
'grub pa dang / /bsgrubs pa'i 'bras bu tshul bzhin 'thob par mdzod/ /ces gsungs pa/ rje mkhyen brtse'i gsung mgur las/ dus dang por 'jig rten bya ba thong / /dus bar
du tshe 'di'i bya ba thong / /dus tha mar chos kyi bya ba thong / /da ci nus bya btang rnal 'byor bgyid/ /lus sna tshogs rgyan gyis rab brgyan kyang / /rus sha dang pags
pas g.yogs pa 'dis/ /gos mdzes pas brgyan kyang snang shas rgyu/ /da cha lugs ngan ngon tsam la brten/ /zhes pa'i don dang mtshungs par ma zad ljongs 'di'i mkhas grub chen
po'i rnam thar ngo mtshar ba'i gnas 'gangs che shos su 'dug cing zhib tu brtags tshe zhal gyis 'ches pa kho na mdzad par yid ches kyi nges pa rnyed pas dad pa'i gsos bla
na med pa'o/ /de nas drang srong srin po ri'i gnas mjal la bya bral 'gros kyis phebs/ de'ang 'bri gung pas paN chen shAkya shrI gdan drangs pa'i tshe paNDi ta bi bhU ti
tsandras phyag rgya ba rdzun che zhes skur pa btab pa'i sgrib sbyong du rje btsun ma'i lung bstan ltar bde mchog gi lha khang bzhengs pa'i sku khyad par can de'i zhabs 'og
tu dar skud 'drongs pa sogs bar snang mar grags pa da lam khyud gang tsam sa la ma reg pa'i ngo mtshar gyi

bkod pa dkon gnyer dang zham 'bring pas mtshon der 'khod kun gyi 'dren byed kyi yul du gyur/ snyan dar dang lha bshos mar me sogs mchod sprin spros te bla ma dang dpal 'khor
lo sdom pa dbyer med ngo bo gcig pa'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang bzhi bzhes pa dang bstan 'gro rgyas pa'i smon lam rgya cher 'debs par mdzad/ de nas gong dkar chos sde brgyud
rim gyis hor zla bcu gnyis pa nyis brtsegs kyi lcags 'brug hor zla dang por rong khu lung du phebs/ rje btsun mi las lha rje gnubs chung par drag sngags gza' gdong dmar
nag gsan nas las sbyor gyi mthu khang lag mthus glags mi rnyed pa'i ched du thur du brus pa'i phug pa der byon te nam zla grang dus yin rung brag las sgrub chu glo bur du
babs pa phyag phyi ba rnams kyis lce thog tu myong zhing yid ches kyi gnas su gyur/ yum bgres mos gsol ba btab par brten gzhis kar zla ba lnga tsam gyi ring ljags bsnyen
kha gso'i sku mtshams dang phyogs 'dus kyi snod ldan rnams la dbang 'khrid lung man ngag sogs chos 'khor mtha' yas pa bskor/ de nas bkra shis rtse chos sder byon/ thub gsung
rin po che bka' 'gyur ro cog yongs rdzogs kyi lung rgyun nyag phra ba thugs kyis ma bzod pa'i phyogs gang dang gang du yod ces rtsad gcod gnang yang nges khungs ma chod
pa'i mur kong po gter ston 'ja' tshon snying por yod pa'i gnas tshul gsan par brten 'degs rtsis mdzad/ me byi byar dwags rnams kyis gtsang sde srid kyi zhabs 'dren byas
pa nas bzung bkag po mang du 'phel ba'i dwags kong phyogs su rgyu 'grul mi bde ba yod pas phebs pa mi 'gab pa zhu mi mang ba byung na'ang gsan 'jog ma gnang bar chos kyi
gdung shugs drag pos ltos med du phebs pa'i dwags po ru'i gru bton sgam po'i gzhis ka klu mkhar zhol du bzhugs nub sngar zhal 'dris med kyang gdung rgyud nas sne len dang
bkag po'i nyes sel la sde pa bkra shis rtse pa'i sku skye yin zer ba'i btsun pa drag pa zhig gis mgo byas mi bcu gnyis tsam phebs skyel du btang ba'i dwags la sgam po'i
phu gnyal la ma thebs tsam gyi byang stongs na chu chen pos bcad nas mi thar bar thug tshe bka' las yas mas tshor 'khyags zam yod 'dra ltos dang gsungs pa ltar bya rog
cig gis sna drangs pa'i rnyed nas pha rir byon pa dang 'khyags zam brdib pa na sna mo shag grub chen pas mchi ma 'don zhing phyag mang du btsal bla ma khyed la thugs rje
yod kyang yod byung yang byung / zhus shing jag pa kha shas 'ong pa'ang chur ma thar ba sogs chom rkun gyi 'jigs pa las grol te kun ya mtshan du gyur/ zhabs skyel ba dmangs
la la 'gro ma 'dod pa'i bros shing rgad bu zhig lus pas lam rgyus zhus gnyal la de kha ba ches pas khal rnams dbar skyel dang rkang lag 'phyid pa kha yar sogs tshang
ma 'o brgyal ba'i ngang nas phebs pa'i gnas mal du bzhugs nub phyag g.yog tsho sdod sa'i thog brdib ste 'ur zhogs che'ang nyes skyon ma byung bas gter gsar gyi srung ma rnams
gnyan pa'i 'tshub tu ngos 'dzin mdzad/ sang nyin bshul du bzhugs skabs phar gnas tshul gyi sngon phar gnang ba mda' rgyang do tsam nas mi zhig dang 'phrad de gleng mo
byas yar slebs byung ba gter ston gyis phebs bsur brdzangs pa'i nga la dbon po yin zer bas kha btags kyi phyag

mjal dang spos chag spar bzhin pas spyan drangs/ khyed dpon slob la sus zhus gnang bas skad cha mi dgos kho rang gis shes yod zer skad/ gter ston dpon slob dgun tshang du chos
thog la phebs pa dang 'grig par dngos po brgya phrag tu longs pa'i 'bul ba dang bcas mjal/ gter ston gyis bka' 'gyur thog mtha' bar gsum gyi lung las mtshan nyid pa gsan
tshod kyang min 'dug /gter ston rang gi phyag g.yas g.yon mdzub mo gnyis sbrel ba'i phyag rgya mdzad nas nged rang dpon slob gnyis 'di ga byung ba bka' 'gyur gyi lung
yin/ phyag sor rnams zlum po/ zla gam/ gru bzhi/ gru gsum du mdzad de spos phor nang du til btab pa'i zhi rgyas dbang drag gi sbyin sreg cig car du grub pa sogs snang tshul
dang gnas tshod mi gcig pa'i grub thob zhig po'i rnam thar rtogs dka' ba dang ma nas tshad thub kyi gter ston du thugs nges shes 'drongs pa'i gter gsar yang zab dkon
cog spyi 'dus/ tshe dpag med gnam lcags rdo rje dngos grub kun 'byung / thugs rje chen po ngan song rang grol/ zhi khro nges don snying po/ rta phag yid bzhin nor bu karma
gling pa'i zhi khro dgongs pa rang grol rnams kyi dbang lung / sgrub thabs gser chos ma'i lung / bi mA la'i snying tig gi chos skor/ yang rdzong snying tig gi chos skor/
mkha' 'gro snying tig gi chos skor rnams gsan/ phar sa lugs kyi chos skor kha shas 'bul ba gnang / gter ston gyi rnam thar du lam 'bras dgongs bstad ma gsan gsung ba dgongs
bstad dang thog mtha' bar gsum byed pas lugs la mngon sum mi dgos rmi lam du'ang mi srid cing rje 'di nyid kyi thugs la yang gnas shong phal cher kye rdor gyi dbang
dang zab lam gyi rnam 'byor lta bu gnang bar lam 'bras su ming btags pa'i rtag brtan sprul sku'i rnam thar zhig de ru slebs pa 'dra'o/ /gsung gleng zhig la/ gter gsar lung
bstan du/ nub nas byang sems 'gro 'dul nyi shu gcig: stag yos lo pa rang rtags dpral sme can: zhes pa nyid yin par 'dug ces ngos 'dzin mdzad pa ltar dgung lo yos dang dbu
dpral la sme ba nyis brtsegs yod par der tshogs rnams nges pa rnyed kyang rje bla ma bdag gir cher mi mdzad/ gzhan yang gter ston rje lcags zam par 'khrungs pa'i dus lcags
zam then pa'i sprul pa'i gyad du gyur pa dang rje 'bangs nyer lnga'i nang tshan zhig yin tshul khrom bsgrags su gsungs pa sogs thugs yid gcig tu 'dres/ gter ston gyi
dus tshod 'di gang 'dra yong mi shes pas yar mgyogs tsam phebs gsung ba zla shas nas gtsang sog gi bde gzar langs pa sogs mkhyen par snang / yar lam yang 'dul gyi gtsug
lag khang bu chur thugs rje chen po dang rta mgrin sogs gnas rten mjal zhing mchod 'bul dang smon lam gnang / dung mtshor tshong dpon bkra shis kyis gtsos pa rnams kyis ja
snam phrug gi 'bul ba dang bcas byin rlabs dang chos 'brel zhus/ gter ston sangs rgyas gling pa'i gdung brgyud kyi jo mo sgam po'i lcam gyis gzhis kar mjal nas gzhis len
bstab/ sang nyin phu'i gnas su byon shog ser dam rdzas sogs rten rnams zhib tu mjal/ nga lar phebs mtshams dgas po gro lung gi ayon zer ba'i rtsub spyod can de'i ma rungs
pa'i blo zhi ste zhabs 'dren ma zhus par ma zad byin rlabs zhu bas mtshon gus pa'i rnam 'gyur byas/ nyer 'tshe

cung zad kyang med bzhin pa nas yar klungs su bde bar phebs te gdan sa chen po nyid du stan chags/ bla ma bka' brgyad yongs 'dus kyi spyi lung mdor bsdus snying po las/ khyad
par gdug pa sbrul gyi lo shar dus: gnam rtags 'od dkar skya rengs yang yang 'char: gza' skar 'khrug cing byang du hor sog g.yo: 'ol dga'i phyogs su chos pas rkyen byas
'khrug: dbus gtsang sde 'khrug 'gro rnams nyam thag 'gyur: sa g.yos nad rims lo gsum lo nyes 'byung : lo dgu'i bar du dbus gtsang dbu rur 'tshog: ces pa dang / yol mo sprul
sku gter ston bstan 'dzin nor bu'i gter gsar du/ yos kyi lo la ngal gso byed: 'brug gi lo la 'brug ltar ldir: sbrul la sbrul shun lta bur 'thor: de phyir yos bu'i lo
la long : zhes pa'i lung bstan dus la bab pa'i gtsang sog gi dus 'khrug chen po langs par nye ba mchog dman mtha' dag blo 'tshub par brten gtsang sde srid nas sa rnying gi
sngags sde phal cher la sog bzlog gi sku rim btsugs pa'i rnam grangs mang tsam byung song ba dang phyogs mthun du bslab ston dang bstun pa'i dmar chen gtor bzlog gi tshe
zangs gri can gyi gtor ma sgo phyogs su 'chus shing yungs kar gang bzang rnams rang bzhin gyi sil sgra chad med sgrogs/ gtor ma 'phen sar gtor ma las me lhab kyi 'bar te
rtse mo nas btso byang shar phyogs su rgyugs pa sogs rdo rje chos skyong rnams bran du bkol ba'i mthu stobs rdzu 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab cing de lo lho byang kun tu dus
kyi chad pa'i brdabs gsigs sna tshogs byung na'ang yar klungs stod smad kyi sde dgon yul gru tshor gnod pa cher ma byung ba'i khar sgos su dmigs med kyi dbyings su rgyas
'debs pa'i gra bsgrig klungs su ma rgyugs pa'i nyes pa rnams rim gyis zhi bas nus mthu'i gzi byin 'od du 'bar/ 'on kyang lo 'di dang chu rta'i bar stod smad kyi bde gzar
gcig mjug gcig non lta bu'i rgya mtsho'i rlabs ltar yol ba med pas 'khor lo gsum gyi mdzad 'phrin ha cang gi rgya che ba gnang ma thub rung gdan sa nyid du stan chags
shing / gong dkar chos sder yang nyi ma gling du chos kyi gsan pa mdzad/ khra 'brug gi li ma rnams byin rlabs zhu mi mangs par brten dreg pas nogs pa chu lug sde pa bkra
shis rtse pas sbyin bdag mdzad de star bu sogs kyis bkrus nas gsar pa lta bur song bar zhal gser spyan 'byed dbu mthing gi zhig gsos/ rje nyid nas ras las grub pa'i stod
smad kyi gos zungs 'bul ba gnang / lcags sbrul bde gzar skabs rgyal khang bshig par brten gnas rnying rgyal po rten med du song ba'i e gnyal yar klungs lho kha phyogs su
'khyar ba'i gnod pa sna tshogs byas pa 'di dus khra 'brug gi phyag bzhi pa'i mgon khang mdor yod pa sna mo shag grub chen pas rab gnas kyi sbyin bdag zhus te rje nyid phebs
rgyu'i snga nub lha 'dre'i dmag sgar rnams 'ur ba'i chu byang khar song ba legs bshad gling pa'i grwa pa dge slong rje btsun zer ba'i mig mthong shin tu gsal bas nges
shes 'drongs pa'i ya mtshan du byed pa bcom ldan 'das he badzra'i rnam par rol pa'i gzi byin ma bzod par snang / de'ang gter kha mang por gnas chen rnams la rab gnas bskyar
na bod 'bangs kyi bde thabs la phan par gsungs pa bzhin mchod yon thams cad thugs rtse mthun te thog mar sde

brgyad cha mnyam pa'i phyir bsangs dang gser skyems/ dngos gzhi dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor la brten nas rab tu gnas shing me tog gi char chen po phab pa'i tshe lha sras
kyi phyag bzo'i dpal ayon chen po'i sku la rang nyid kyis nga 'dra gsungs te mkhur tshos la phyag mdzub btsugs shul rgyal blon gyi dus nas kyong tsam yod pa'i nang du
sngar med pa'i a 'bur dod gsal ba dkon gnyer gyis mthong ba sogs gangs can bde legs spel ba'i rtsa lag tu gyur/ sbrul lo bstan pa spyi rim sogs mdzad par bsnyad gzhan sbyor
phun tshogs mi bzod par phrag dog can 'dras snyan phra sna tshogs phul bar brten sa skyong bsod nams rab brtan kyang thugs kyi 'dzin stangs gzhan du gzhol ba'i gnang
sgo la gzhogs drud de dgon gnas la 'pho len sogs bka'i lung lci ba'i chad pa 'dra 'ong ngam zhes brjod rigs du mas phyogs de'i skya ser phal cher re dogs dang som nyir gyur

nas lha btsun bo dhi rA dzas/ jo bo chen po bsam yas su bzhugs par ma 'dod pa'i tshe/ gang na 'thab cing rtsod pa bas/ /dpag tshad brgya yi pha rol 'gro/ /zhes gzhan du

thor phu/ rnam sras sprin gseb pa'i rjes gnang dang sgrub skor/ byang gter gyi tshe dbang lcags sdong ma bkra bzang pa chos skyong bsod nams kyi phyag bzhes/ thang lha'i
srog gtad/ thang stong pa'i tshe dbang 'chi med dpal ster sogs zab chos mang du phul/ de yang zur kun mkhyen chen pos sngon chad gsang sngags gsar rnying gi chos bka'
mang du gsan mod kyang nye lam shin tu dgyes pa'i nged la'ang sku zhabs thugs rtsol gyis khyab par brten da cha gzhan la 'gram chu ldang mi dgos pa'i thob rgya byung zhes
bka' phebs pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsung mgur du/ smin byed dbang gi chu bo mtha' dag legs par thob nas/ /de dag rjes su 'brel ba'i rim gnyis nyams su blangs shing
/ /dam tshig sdom pa skyon med srog bzhin gces par bskungs pas/ /rdor 'dzin tshogs pa'i khrod nas mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug skyid do/ /rgya bod mkhas grub bla ma mtshan
ldan mang du bsten nas/ /mdo sngags gsar rnying smin grol bshad bka' mang du thos shing / /rnam thar thos

pa'i don mang tshul bzhin cung zad rtogs pas/ /mang thos tshogs pa'i dbus na mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug skyid do/ /zhes pa'i don 'di nyid kyi rnam thar du song ngo / /gung
thang pa rnams gtso bor gyur pa'i khrom la grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang dang / ma Ni ba rnams la thugs rje chen po gtso 'khor gsum pa'i rjes gnang stsal/ bar der mong bza'
khri btsun gyis btab cing slob dpon chen po padma saM bha wa dang mnyam med jo bo chen po dI paM ka ra sogs dam pa du mas byin gyis brlabs pa yer ba'i gnas mjal bar phebs
te rten brten pa rnams la yan lag bdun pa rgyas par phul/ 'tsho rgyal phug tu gsol 'debs le'u bdun ma'i skabs sku chos la tshe chu thigs pa re gnyis babs pa je 'phel
la song ba nas dpon slob thams cad la mchod rgyu byung zhing snod du blug ste bsnams phebs rgyu sogs ye shes mkha' 'gro'i gtso mo des rjes su bzung ba'i mtshan ma khyad
par can du gda'o/ /zur kun mkhyen chen por gsan pa bla ma nor bu rgyal mtsho'i sgrub dbang / bka' brgyad bder gshegs 'dus pa'i dbang / ratna'i klong gsal snying thig gi chos
skor/ dam can skyes bu'i srog dbang lung bcas/ gshin rje tshe bdag lcags 'dra dang lcags sdig /khro chu/ dri med lhun po'i don tig 'gro ba kun sgrol rnams kyi dbang lung
yongs rdzogs/ rlung dmar gyi skor/ rdor 'bum chos grags kyi bdud rtsi bum pa dang / g.yu thog snying thig gnyis kyi dbang lung / brang ti'i gdams ngag dngul bre'i drang
srong ser skya'i sgrub lung / sangs rgyas gling pa'i rnam sras ser chen gyi srog dbang lung bcas/ gra pa'i zhang blon las tshogs kyi lung / las 'brel rtsal gyi bdud mgon
gyi bka' gtad dregs dbang lung bcas/ 'bro lo'i khams gsum 'khrug byed rlung nag gi skor/ bram ze sdom bzang gi rlung 'khor/ bla ma zhang gi bka' 'bum pod bzhi bka' rgya
ma dang bcas pa/ snar thang brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang lung bcas sogs chos bka' mtha' klas pa gsan/ 'di dang lcags stag gi chos 'khor gyi 'dus pa dang gnyis kyi gtso bo skyed
tshal mkhan chen byams pa ngag dbang bstan 'dzin yod par snang ngo / /hor zla dgu pa'i nang du khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba 'bras spungs su phebs nas pha dam pa'i 'chi med
mgon por brten pa'i ring por 'tsho ba'i rten 'byung gi gsung chog rgyas par gnang / rje mkhyen brtse'i gsung mgur du/ yongs bla ma bsten pa mang na yang / /khong slob 'khor
rgyas pa'i 'ur rgyang can/ /sgrob gang che'i rjes su rgyug pa las/ /rje mtshan ldan bsten pa dkon na yang / /dpal rgyal ba kun dngos sgo rum pa/ /sras tshar pa'i zhabs
pad bsten lags pas/ /bdag sprang po bsams bzhin skyid du tshor/ /khyed mched grogs tsho'i thugs la ji ltar gda'/ /zhes pa'i don ltar sku gsung thugs kyi mdzad pa la gus
par byung bas/ /tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos zab lung bder gshegs 'dus pa'i sku brnyan drung du mdzad pa'i ayon rin po che'i gsol 'debs kyi lung dang tshar chen gyi phyag
dpe ngos ma'i ha la nag po'i be'u bum mgo thog tu 'jog pa gnang ba'i bka' bsgo zhig zhus phebs rdzongs gzabs rgyas dang bcas yar lam zur kun mkhyen bla ma dang zhal rgyas
ngos rgod dkar la brgyud dpal zan g.yang lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang chen por phebs te dbu rtse

rigs gsum yaksha bla 'og /gling bzhi/ gling phran/ jo mo'i gling gsum dang bcas pa'i rten brten pa rnams la dkar me snyan shal sogs kyi tshogs gsog /bshad sgrub kyi ring lugs/
skye rgu'i legs byas 'phel ba'i smon lam gyis mtshams sbyar ba'i dus mkhan tshang ba dang rab byung ba rnams kyis zhabs drung sgar chen zhing khams gzhan du gshegs nas
lcog tu rang lugs kyi bla ma phebs mkhan gzhan ma byung gshis da lam chos skyong chen po sku phebs dang 'grig pas ngos mjal 'gab zhus rung snyan dar dang dmod nas tsam
phul bas 'thus rtsis la smon grong gi dre'u g.yar po bcad 'bangs pa'i mdzos brdungs pa ma mjal na 'khren pa'i brdar dgongs te lcog la phebs pa dregs pa yongs kyi sde dpon
gnod sbyin tsi'u dmar po khog tu brlams pa rdo skyags mgor bsu bar phebs nas khrom pa rnams lha rgyal lan gsum then bcug cing dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur mdzad/ sde pa stag rtse
bas dung chen gsar brdungs spyan 'bebs zhus pa da res mkhan po byon pa dang 'grig pa rten 'brel gyi sgo yod pas phyogs bzhi nas 'bud du bcug pa/ ji skad du/ sngon gyi
rgyal po grags pa'i gzugs/ /ngag gi rang bzhin me long thob/ /de nyid nye bar mi gnas kyang / /rang nyid nyams pa med la ltos/ /zhes pa ltar rje bla ma dag zhing du gshegs
nas lo bco brgyad tsam slebs kyang sku gsung thugs kyi rnam par thar pa'i grags snyan phyogs bral gyi rna ba'i rgyan du je cher 'phel ba'i brdar mngon/ sngon dge slong
nag po sogs kyi skye rgyus bha ta hor gyi sgom gra nas byon te gu ru padmas gtsug lag khang gi srung mar bskos pa nas da bar ma nyams par mdzad lugs kyi rgyu mtshan rgyas
par gsungs pa'i tshe rje nyid kyis shin tu legs tshul dang dge rgyas 'di bye ma'i gnod pas 'jig par nye ba chos skyong chen po'i rdzu 'phrul gyis zhi ba byung na zhes zhus
pa'i lan du spyir 'gro ba'i las gtso zhing sgos su gzugs can gyi mis ma byas na nged gzugs med kyis dka' gsung / dmod nas dang bcas bstan 'gro'i phan bde sgrub pa'i 'phrin
bcol dang 'gro ba rnams kyang mi dge bar spyod pa shas che bas mi lus thob pa'ang dka' mor mchis pa zhing bcu tshang ba'i rigs ma gtogs skye 'gro'i srog dbugs la gnod
pa mdzad na mi legs tshul zhu ba gnang bar sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa srung ba'i bya ra byed cing bstan 'gro'i bde skyid 'phrog pa'i dgra bgegs ni sngar yang tshar bcad da
rung gu ru padma'i bka' las mi 'da' de min sdug 'dres sems can tshor gnod pa ga la byed/ 'gro ba rnams kyis sdig pa mi dge ba bsags pa'i 'bras bu sdug 'dre'i rnam pa shar
ba yin pas bya thabs ga la yod gsungs par rjes su'ang thugs nges shes 'drongs par snang / sngar khyed kyis mdzad zer rgyu min kyang sdug 'drer dmigs pa'i srung mdud mangs
na bar chad kyi rgyur 'gro bas mi 'gab tshul gsung ba'i shugs bstan ched du dmigs nas bskyed chog mdzad pa re gnyis la sngon rje btsun rdo ring pa chen por gnas rnying
rgyal pos khas blangs pa dang 'dra bar sems shing slar sku rim sogs blang dor gyi lung bstan zhib tu mdzad/ rdo skyags mgo'i bar phebs skyel zhus shing mchod rten dmar
po ba'i btsun pas stag lung zhabs drung phebs pa las 'tshub pa dang da res las 'jam pa ma dran zer ba ni/ rje

mkhyen brtse'i gsung mgur las/ phyi rol gyi dregs pa rgyud gsum po/ /rang sems kyi rtsal du rang ngo 'phrod/ /yin lugs kyi shes pa lhug pa la/ /bzo bcos med pa bla ma'i drin/
/zhes pa'i don bzhin gsang las yang gsang snying po'i man ngag gi che ba'o/ /rim gyis bkra shis chos kyi sde chen por phebs/ zhol nas nang pa shod pa pas spyan drangs
te nang mi dmangs la tshe dbang grub rgyal ma dang skyer sgang lugs kyi rta mgrin gyi byin rlabs/ tshong dpon phun tshogs khyo shugs gnyis la lcags sdong ma'i tshe dbang
brgya rtsa dang / rnam sras ser chen gyi rjes gnang stsal/ dbang gtor gyi khang brtsegs de lo 'khor du bzhag pa sos ka'i tsha ba dang gtor ma bzhag pa'i nang der lo ro ba
lnga tsam gyis mchod kong dang ting sogs blug pa'i me dugs rnams 'doms na'ang rgyan sprod kyi mar ma zhu zhing bag rdul gyis bkrag ma nyams pas mtshon skyon gang yang ma
byung gnod sbyin ngal bsos po 'dod rgyal gyi lcags kyus bcug pa'i rtags mtshan mngon sum du gsal ba de'o/ /sa mo glang lor khyab bdag khra tshang pa chen po lho bra nyi
lder dhI tsha sprul sku 'jig rten dbang phyug gi drung du sher phyogs skor gsan par rdzong bda' gnang / phebs sgo bzhin gsol chas rnams do bo rdzong nas 'tshems med du bstar/
dbyar zur kun mkhyen chen pos yar klungs su phebs par mgon po lha brgyad dang bcu gnyis ma thun mong ma yin pa/ dud sol ma'i rjes gnang nan chags ma/ pu tra/ ber nag
zangs gri can phyi nang / bran bdud thun mong ba/ las sbyor gyi mgon po glang gdong ma/ phyag rdor gos sngon can/ rnam sras ser chen smad lugs/ dkar bdud lcam dral rnams
kyi rjes gnang / yang gsang khros pa'i rdzong chung tshe dbang / byang gter 'chi med 'od snang gi dbang / drag po dbu dgu'i rtsa dbang / tshe dpag med grub rgyal lha gcig
bum gcig ma/ tshe sbyin dkar po zhag bdun ma/ tshar chen gyi bka' 'bum/ bla ma dam pa dang mus chen gyi kye rdor mngon rtogs/ dkyil chog bya bral ma/ sgo rum pa'i rnam
thar rje mkhyen brtses mdzad pa sogs dgongs bzhed kyi chos bka' mang du 'bul ba gnang / rje khra tshang pa chen po lho brag nas phyir phebs pa la brgyad stong pa ma gtogs
pa'i sher phyogs yongs rdzogs kyi lung gsan dus gsung ngag lam 'bras dang rdo rje phreng ba sogs spyi bka' zur bka' mang tsam zhu ba'i snyan gsan 'bebs par sde pa bsod nams
rab brtan gyis thugs khur bzhes nas rgyal rtse sman grong tshe dbang dar rgyas rdzong bda' mdzad/ sher phyogs kyi ljags lung 'phro gsan dgos dang phyag dpe gzigs rtog
sbrags pa'i thugs brel khyad kyi zla ba phyed gnyis tsam nas 'byon pa'i dus tshes bsgrigs/ hor zla bcu pa'i 'gor rgyal khab chen po pho brang po ta lar phebs te thog mar
rten 'brel gyi khyad nas tshe dpag med grub rgyal ma'i bskyed rdzogs kyi nyams 'khrid dang tshe dpag med dkar po chag lugs kyi rjes gnang stsal ba'i snga dro li ma lha khang
du gsung ngag gi khrid dang dgongs ja khar rang byung 'phags pa'i lha khang du dbang rjes gnang gi rigs rim gyis gnang bar gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad kyi nyams
khrid smin rgyas/ rgyu dbang / lam dbang / bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i dbang byin rlabs kyi skor rags rim/ nA

ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs/ rgyab rten gyi lung / rdo rje phreng ba zhe lnga ma/ bde mchog lU i pa'i dbang bka' babs bdun ldan/ nag po pa/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang
bka' babs bzhi ldan/ gshin rje dgra nag ra lugs bcu gsum ma/ gdan bzhi lha dgu bcu rtsa bdun ma/ bde mchog bong zhal can lha so bdun ma'i dbang / gsang ba 'dus pa sa lugs
lha bcu dgu ma'i dbang / gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang brgyud pa sum ldan/ 'jigs byed lha zhe dgu ma dang ro langs brgyad skor/ ku ru kulle lha lnga/ gur mgon lha lnga sindhu
ra'i dkyil 'khor la brten pa/ dam pa lugs kyi 'jam dbyangs smra seng gi dbang / dze tA ri lugs kyi tshe dpag med lha dgu rnams kyi dbang / de'i sgrub thabs dbang chog
bstod pa dze tA ris mdzad pa/ dkon cog lhun grub kyi dkyil chog dang bcas pa'i lung / 'dod rgyal gsang sngags sgra'i rjes gnang / bram ze nag po'i mngag gtad thun mong ma
yin pa/ 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na'i rjes gnang / de'i sgrub thabs sa paN gyis mdzad pa dang rjes gnang gi yi ge ngor chen gyis mdzad pa/ brtag gnyis/ tshe mdo le tshan
gnyis/ mi 'khrugs pa'i rgyud rnams kyi lung / gnyan sgrol yan lag drug pa'i rjes gnang / mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa'i lung dang bcas pa/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs
kyi cho ga tshar chen gyis mdzad pa dang rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i gur mgon gyi sku rten bzhengs tshul rab gnas dang bcas pa'i lung / tshe dpag med grub rgyal lugs kyi
nyams 'khrid/ sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo 'od zer drug sbrags thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang rnams thugs dgyes pa chen po'i sgo nas stsal zhing gser dngul gos dar ja
ras 'bru sogs zang z-ing gi maNDal chos yon du bteg /de yang / kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i gsung mgur las/ sprang po las ngan gyi dbang gis snyigs dus mtha' 'khob tu skyes
kyang / /tshe sngon dag pa'i smon lam gyis mtshan ldan bla ma dang mjal nas/ /thos dka' rtogs par dka' ba'i zab lam du ma zhig thob pas/ /shi yang 'gyod med kyi blo bde gzhan
las lhag pa zhig gda' bas/ /dga' dga' skyid skyid mo gzhan la yid smon med pa zhig gda'o/ /zhes pa'i don bzhin/ sngon chad rdo rje slob dpon mang du bsten pa'i skal
ba phra zhing cung zad rnyed pa'ang zhabs pad bsten yun thungs pa dang gzhan rkyen gyi 'jigs pas gsang thabs rkun nor ltar spyod dgos pa la nye lam de rigs kyi skyon dang
bral zhing thos bsam gyi cha spyod yul yangs pa sngon bsags legs byas kyi 'bras bu dus su smin par ma zad dam pa 'di nyid kyi sku gsung thugs kyi mdzad pa mtha' dag sngar
dam bca' gnang 'dug pa'i don dang cha mtshungs pa'i zhal gyis 'ches pa la dpa' ba tsam ma yin par don mthun kho nar snang ba sha stag tu mthong pa dper na 'phyong rgyas
zhabs drung dmag dpon lha'i dbang phyug gis bka' shog gtan tshigs thams cad ras su bor ba'i 'phyos lam rim pas bkra shis chos sde pa'i dkor sa'i gral khungs sogs phrogs
pa chos sde pa rnams kyang re ba che zhing phyi yul nas bltas pa yang babs 'brel 'dug rung phebs sgor kho rang tshor dkor skal za rgyu ni 'dug gral gyi rgyab mdun gang du
bsdad kyang khyad ci yod ces zhu ba'i rtsom pa tsam yang mi mdzad cing sku sger don du gtogs pa rje sman lung

ba sher phyogs gsan pa'i gsol phogs dang dbon mkhyen rab rnam rgyal phyag phyir bsdad chog pa'i dgongs khrol tsam ma gtogs zhu don mdzad pa ma mthong zhing dgon gra rigs sbyin
bdag sogs re ba mkhan po du mar yang nged rang pher pher dang yong yong ba de 'dra lar mi dga' zhes zhu don gyi sna len ye mi gnang / bstan pa 'phel ba dang 'gro ba'i
bde skyid sogs spyi la phan pa'i zhal ta lhur bzhes shing / shes rab sdong bu las/ 'gro ba shin tu grangs med kyang / /sems can yon tan ldan pa dkon/ /yul ljongs dpag tu
med mod kyi/ /rin po che dag 'byung ba dkon/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ khyad par dbang byin rlabs rjes gnang rig gtad nyams 'khrid la da lam long chungs pa'i dgag bya dgos pa
yin zhes mtshon don tsam gyi bsdu ba dang 'di'i tshab 'dis 'ong 'di'i dod 'dis byed ces chos la dbang mi za bar so so'i lugs bzhin ma 'dres pa kho na dang ljags lung gi
skabs dpe rnam grangs phra mo mang du yod pa'i rigs la bsnyel tho dang bstun nas gsan ma gsan gyi dbye ba 'byed pa las yi ge lhogs pa rgyu mtshan du byas te byung tshad
ljags sgrog mi gnang / phyag len gyi rigs gang la dogs gcod zhus kyang 'di ni 'di'o zhes shig mdzub sprad pa'i nges shes kho na las mun nag 'dom 'jal gyi zol sbyor ci yang
mi srid pas dbang rnon chos rjes 'brang ba'i dad pa brtan po'i gting tshugs so/ /thugs rje 'od kyi sbubs gur bde ba'i lam/ /sa spyod rigs pa'i khye'u chung dag zhing du/
/drangs tshe dge sdig gcig tu dkar ro zhes/ /las kyi me long lta ba'i ngal ba btang / /mkhas pa'i gzhung lugs sa ha ka ra yi/ /snye ma nam mkha'i pha mthar yongs dud kyang
/ /sa bon thub pa'i gsung rab gces pa'i nor/ /bstan 'dzin phal gyis dor bas dgun chu bzhin/ /de tshul bzod min snying stobs ri rtse'i chab/ /brtson 'grus shugs kyis 'bab
pa le lo'i rigs/ /sdig to'i 'phrul gyis mi ldog chos 'tshol bar/ /mi zhum rgyal sras spyod pa 'di rmad byung / /bcos min nges par 'byung ba'i chos brgyad las/ /log pa'i
thugs kyi sna de rab thung yang / /shAkya seng ge'i ring lugs spel ba'i blo'i/ /zhags ring brkyangs mtha' bskal par rdzogs nus min/ /nyang ston rigs sngags 'chang ba'i
dbang phyug de/ /dam pa'i bzhed pa skong ba'i maNDa la/ /bteg tshe srid zhi'i yon tan nor bu'i dpya/ /phyur bur spungs te chos bzang mdun sar gleng / /gsar rnying nyi zla
zung 'brel 'od po ches/ /'khor mun mthar byed las smon mthu btsan pos/ /zur chen rje dang stabs cig stan 'dzom pa/ /phan bde'i snang ba 'dren pa'i shing rta bzhin/ /ma
rig las 'khon 'jam mgon rim byon tshos/ /ma dag 'khrul pa'i drwa ba gcod pa'i mtshon/ /ma lus 'gro gnyen sa skya'i bla chen gyis/ /ma smad snyan brgyud gser 'khor mkha' la
'phags/ /gnyags ban dznyA na'i sbrul pa'i zlos gar des/ /mgon khyod padmA ka ra'i gdung 'tshob khrir/ /theg mchog nor bu'i cod pan dbur bcings nas/ /bkod tshe phyogs bcu'i
rgyal kun me tog gtor/ /bde chen 'dren pa'i las rgya mkhar chen bzas/ /'chi med bdud rtsi'i rgyun gyi bcud byin tshe/ /gnas 'di las gzhan DA ka DAkki'i tshogs/ /'du ba'i
ayon yul de 'tshol rnams ngal/ /snang srid dregs pa'i sde dpon tsi dmar bas/ /mgon khyod 'phrin las sgrub

par zhal 'ches pa/ /lhun grub rten cing 'brel 'byung dung chen sgra/ /phyogs bral bu mo'i rna lung mdzes pa bzhin/ /bshes gnyen mngal du ma sbrums stong pa'i sgra/ /grang drod
las btsas khye'u dkar min 'bras/ /drang srong u pa'i re skong rgod ma kha/ /gtan mdun rgya mtsho skam pa'i cho ga ltar/ /'on te srid mang 'phrang bgrod dka' spyad kyi/
/bsod nams dzam bu'i shing 'bras mtshor lhungs pa/ /dal rten don ldan gser gyi phung po la/ /spyod pa'i skal bzang 'di la gcig tu rangs/ /snyan brgyud rim bzhi'i rten 'brel
yongs 'grig pa/ /ma nub dbang bzhi'i lam las 'bras bur smin/ /rgyud sde rnam bzhi'i chos kyi thems skas la/ /khrid nas sku bzhi'i grong du bcug 'di mtshar/ /khu lung
du yum bsnyun pa'i gdan 'dren byung bar brten lcags stag gi lo gsar gdong rong phyogs su thegs nas zla gcig gi bar byin rlabs sku rim dang 'phrod bsten gyi zhal bkod dang
bcas zhal ngo rnams kyi dgongs pa bkang ste zhang 'gro ba'i mgon po'i bsti gnas su phebs pa'i dbyar ston gyi ring bzhugs/ gsol chas dgos cha rnams byi lo'i skabs ltar phul
zhing zur kun mkhyen chen pos dbu mdzad don gnyer can du ma la gang blo ma/ dbang gi sgrol ma dmar mo/ dus 'khor gyi thun mong sgrub pa'i lha gsum/ sman bla bder gshegs
bdun/ phyag rdor u tsarYa/ ba ri'i rnam 'joms/ sme brtsegs/ mi g.yo ba dkar sngon/ rta mgrin ras chung lugs/ rta nag lcags ral can/ seng gdong nag po/ dzam ser nag /spyan
ras gzigs gtso 'khor gsum pa/ dur khrod bdag po/ rnam sras drag po bka' shin tu gnyan pa/ gsang sgrub ljang ser be con can/ drag byed rta sngon srin mo bzhi skor/ nang
gsang ltar sgrub pa lha dgu /drag byed sed zhon klu brgyad kyis bskor ba/ drag byed rkang thang lha brgyad/ mdung dmar can lha bcu gsum/ yang gsang drag po srin po bzhi
skor/ mthing kha zhal gsum phyag drug pa las mkhan mdung dmar can dang bcas pa'i gtso 'khor gnyis/ gar mkhan mchog ljang gu zhal gsum phyag bco brgyad pa lha brgyad/ gar
mkhan mchog dmar smug zhal gsum phyag bco brgyad pa/ dkar po tshe 'phel lha dgu/ yang gsang mdung dmar can phyag mtshan bzhi pa/ gur gsang 'khrid rnams kyi rjes gnang /
bran bdud kyi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa/ zhal sgrub dus thun mong ma yin pa/ khyung zhal can/ seng gdong nag po/ lha mo rdo rje rab brtan ma rnams kyi rjes gnang / phag
dkar shes rab gsal byed dang rta mgrin skyer sgang lugs kyi byin rlabs/ rdo rje nam mkha' lding gser mig 'khyil ba'i rjes gnang lung bcas sgrub thabs rgya mtsho las sku'i
rnam 'gyur dang sngags mi 'dra ba brgya bzhi bcu'i rjes gnang dang rgya gzhung gi lung / dus 'khor gyi bdag po chen po ma gtogs sku gsung thugs yongs rdzogs/ gshin rje
gdong drug /rnam snang mngon byang / rnam 'joms mthing nag lha bcu dgu /rigs gsum spyi/ gdugs dkar lha bcu bdun/ srung ba lha nga gcig /mi 'khrugs pa lha mo brgyad kyis
bskor ba/ sa phur lha khra'i stod las rnams kyi dbang dang smad las drag po'i rjes gnang / e ka dza tI'i srog gtad dang lung / ma Ni ka nA thas 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtser
gnang ba'i gsar 'gyur ayon sku gsum sgrub brgya 'gyur/ de'i lo rgyus 'grel pa dang bcas pa 'jam dbyangs mkhyen

brtse'i zin bris kyi lung / dkar bdud lcam dral gyi sgrub skor/ lam skor phyi ma brgyad kyi lung yongs rdzogs/ tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs/ gsung ngag slob bshad kyi chos
'byung zin bris 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses mdzad pa/ tshar chen gyi kye rdor bskyed rim sogs chos sbyin rgya cher mdzad cing rje bla ma zur chen la snga 'gyur gtso bor
gyur pa'i zab chos mang du gsan/ dran pa nam mkha' dang gnubs chen gyi rnam par sprul pa dar rgyas chos sdings pa 'phrin las lhun grub byon par dpon slob gnyis kas lhan
du paN chen padma dbang rgyal gyi rigs 'dzin yongs 'dus kyi dbang lung / lho brag gu ru lha khang nas yang gter gyi skor/ ratna'i phur pa yang gsang bla med/ rta phag gsang
sgrub/ thugs rje chen po zhi drag lam gyi cha rkyen gsang ba snying po 'dus pa/ sku gsum yongs rdzogs rtsa gsum 'bras bu'i don 'khrid/ phyag rgya chen po mun sel nyi ma'i
snying po/ skyes rabs lung gi lde mig sogs zab gter kha thor ba'i skor/ mnal lam dag snang gi skor/ rigs 'dzin rgod ldem gyi gu ru mthing kha spyan mangs kyi sgrub lung
/ las 'brel rtsal gyi dregs 'dul sgrub thabs chig brgyud ma'i lung / kun mkhyen klong chen pa'i yid bzhin mdzod/ shes rab me 'bar gyi rdzogs chen 'khor 'das rang grol
gyi dbang lung / spa gro gter ston tshe ring rdo rje'i rdzogs chen ci ti'i gsal byed nor bu'i dbang lung / dri med kun dga'i thugs rje chen po ye shes 'od mchog /lho las
'phro gling pa nam mkha' rdo rje'i rdo rje sems dpa'i thugs sgrub kyi dbang lung / e spel lcog las 'phro gling pa'i bla sgrub phyi nang gsang gsum gyi dbang lung / gter ston
'jam dpal rdo rje'i tshe sgrub thugs kyi yang snying gi chos skor/ snang rtse pa'i tshe 'khrid yang snying 'dus pa/ 'jam dpal nag po'i yig sna gnyis/ gter ston shes rab
'od zer gyi 'chi med sku gsum 'dus pa/ spo bo gter ston padma rig 'dzin rtsal gyi nor bu padma'i 'phreng ba'i gsang sgrub kyi skor/ zla ban gzi brjid 'bar gyi sngags sdebs
snying gi me long zung gi lung / rgya ban rdo rje dbang phyug gi bcud len gyi gdams skor/ sprul sku dam pa dmar po'i bdud rtsi bum pa'i bcud len skor/ bal po badzra
ma ti'i rims srung / gu ru khyung nag gi gshin rje'i sku gsung thugs kyi za yig /gter ston bon po drag rtsal gyi rA hu la shis bstan pa dang rus sbal ser srung / lcang sman
don grub dar gyi dug sman gyi gdams pa/ g.yu thog snying thig gi sman lha mched gsum ye shes khye'u dang bcas pa'i rjes gnang / de bzhin du gsung sprul tshul khrims rdo
rje la bla ma snying tig gi dbang lung sogs gsan zhing khong dpon slob gnyis la phar yang bka' chos ci rigs stsal char 'bebs la zur kun mkhyen chen po dang chabs cig par
tshal yang dgon du phebs/ zhang rin po che'i gzigs snang dang phyag bzor grags pa'i ye shes mgon po phyag bzhi pa'i sku la khrus gsol dang bcol dam gnang bas mgon po'i
zhal las bdud rtsi babs pa der 'khod rnams kyis mthong nas rgyu mtshan gsol ba na dpon slob rin po che phebs pas yin gsung / skyid shod ba lam nub she ma mkhar pa'i bu nad
tshabs chen pos btab ste sman pas mi 'tsho bar thag bcad pa'i dus byin rlabs gnang bas nad las grol/ lha gdong

shan kha ba'i ma 'chi bar thug par sngon gyi pha mes chos gcig dpal 'byor gyis bsgrubs pa'i dur khrod kyi bdag mo 'dre mo ngan ne ma'i sgrub khang yod pa de'i 'khrin dogs su
mkhyen nas dur khrod bdag mo la thun rdzas dang bcas bka' bsgo gnyer btad gnang bas de 'phral gzhi med du bde/ gzims khang shar tu rtsis mgon gyi 'dzin gtor btsugs pa 'jig
par nye ba gsang du brje ba'i sta gon gyi rnying pa bton pa'i shul gyi gtor snod bdud rtsis khengs pa mchod dpon 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan dang zhu lu sher rin pa gnyis
kyis longs spyod rgyu byung bas mtshon ya mtshan gyi ltas mang po zhig byung tshod du mchis so/ /shis rtse'i dpon sa bsam yas chos skyong gi 'khor du skyes pa mkhyen pa'i
tshe byang bzhu gnang bas khugs zin nas rjes snyegs la btsun pa dang a tsa ra 'dra ba 'ongs te phyir khrid song ba a lags bsod nams kyis zhus pa sang nyid glud sngon
dus kyi srid pa'i dbyibs ji lta ba bzos pa byin gyis brlabs/ rnam shes khugs 'phral glud sngags rgya ting nge 'dzin gyis bsngos pa'i mthus lha 'dre'i pho nya rnams rab tu
tshim nas log rjes lam ston rgyas par mdzad de dag zhing du bskyal lo/ /gung thang gi bka' chos rnams grol ba'i rje bka' 'gyur ba chen po 'bras spungs su phebs/ ring 'tsho'i
rten 'byung gi gsung chog gnang / rje btsun rdo ring pas mdzad pa'i gur gyi gsang 'khrid/ tshar chen gyi brag rdzong dang gsang 'khrid rgyun khyer gnyis/ rab gnas don
gsal sogs kyi ljags lung dang / rgyal sras rin po che'i blo sbyong don bdun ma'i steng nas nyams 'khrid mdor bsdus/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga mang po'i phyag len dang phyag
rgya 'ching tshul gyi skor sogs la dogs gcod zhib tu zhus/ bsam gtan par rlom pa'i tshul 'chos mkhan 'dras gzhan 'byor phun tshogs ma bzod par byad rbod kyis rje'i sku
la sdo ba'i sbyor ngan yod 'phros thos pas/ brag rdzong ma'i srung bzlog gi thugs dam gtso bor gnang dgos tshul zhus par snga sor gnad bsnun kha yar byas par bsam sbyor ngan
pa yod 'dra bsam pa 'ga' zhig 'das song bas rnam shes 'dren pa'i nus pa dkar bas de rigs kyang las gsog par song dogs byed 'dun med gsung / dgun yar klungs phyogs su
thegs/ bong bu zhes pa lcags yos kyi dpyid gong dkar rdo rje gdan du phebs nas sku mtshams kyi bcad rgya yun ring du bsdams/ nged rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang tshogs chen la
'bul ba'i grabs yul gyi skabs su slebs pa sngar phyag len rnams la rtog 'jug dang dogs gcod zhib bar zhus khul yin na'ang gsang sngags kyi phyag bzhes ches zhib cing phra
ba dang rang re blo gros dman pa'i gshis kun rtog gi spros pa ban bun du shar ba'i yid gnyis rnams la dogs sel gyi shog dril phul bar bka' mchan zhib par stsal/ 'di lo
char dkon pa'i lo tog rnams than pa'i 'jigs pas nyen pa thugs kyis ma bzod par rdzas sngags ting nge 'dzin la brten pa'i char 'bebs kyi phyag len gnang yang lha 'dre'i tshub
lhongs lta bus phebs dka' bar dpal ayon chen po la gdung shugs drag pos gsol 'debs gnang bas klu dbang gling gi rgya dang mnyam pa'i sprin las char babs shing gzhan du
sprin ma 'khrigs pas de lo tshos las kyi bud shing la kha reg gi nags bcad pas khyung btsun khros pa'i de phyogs

su yams dang lce 'bab pa sogs byung snang bas de dang dbyibs mtshungs par dgongs te rdo rje dpal gyi yum la gtor bsngos dang bcas dam bsgrags pas kha reg gi ri rtse las chu
'dzin dkar po lang long du g.yos shing thog mar drag char gyi lhongs che tsam dang bcas rim gyis sprin phyogs kun tu khyab pa'i char gyi rgyun chen pos myu gu'i tshogs kyi
bskyed rab tu bsrings nas yul khams mang por 'bru'i mchod sbyin don gyis stsal lo/ /chos sde 'di ga dang phyogs 'dus kyi don gnyer can kha shas la gshin rje gdong drug
/sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor/ 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma/ mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu rnams kyi dbang / tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang brgya rtsa/ gur lha bcu bdun/ bcu gnyis/ brgyad ma
gsum gyi dbang / brag rdzong ma'i phyi 'khrid dang zhal gyi gsang 'khrid gnyis kyi nyams 'khrid/ rin chen gling pa'i na ga raksha'i rig gtad/ dbyu gu spun gsum gyi sgrub
skor/ mgon pod nas kha shas kyi lung / mgon po ma ning gi char 'bebs/ dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed spyan ras gzigs kyi dmar 'khrid/ rab 'byams smra ba rin cen rgya mtshor
g.yu thog snying tig gi dbang lung / khro bo sme brtsegs dang khro mo sme brtsegs kyi rjes gnang / dmar chen skor gsum/ skyes rabs so bzhi'i lung sogs chos bka' snga phyi
du mar gnang / dga' ba zhes pa chu 'brug hor zla gnyis pa'i nang du nged rgya nag la 'gro ba'i ngos 'phrang la phebs nas gzims chung mgon khang lcang lo can du ring por
gnas pa'i rten 'brel gyi cho ga rigs mi gcig pa gsum tsam zhig gnang / tshe dbang kha shas dgos tshul phebs pa bzhin 'chi med dpal ster gyi sgo nas phul ba bcas de ka'i
steng nas nged rang gis kyang tshar gcig zhus shing 'phral yun gyi bslab ston mang du gnang bar rgya nag nas ring por mi thogs par ldog pa'i 'dun pa yod pas de bar rdo rje'i
rnal 'byor mchog las mi g.yel ba'i srung 'khor dang 'chad nyan la thugs rtsol gang che'i ngos gtso bor bstan 'gro'i gnyen du 'tsho gzhes gyi thabs tshul lhod med dgos
pa'i snyan 'bul dang brtan bzhugs phul/ de nas gung thang du thegs pa'i zla ba phyed gnyis tsam gyi bar zur chen chos kyi rgyal por gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang dang spros
med kyi nyams 'khrid/ rwa chen gyi sgrub dkyil la 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i lhan thabs sbyar ba'i rwa lugs thun mong ma yin pa lha bcu gsum ma'i dbang / rwa 'khrid mkha'
'gro snyan brgyud kyi nyams 'khrid/ rwa chen shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi dkar chag tu gsal ba dang der ma 'dus pa'i kha skong bcas pa'i rwa pod/ 'bri gung dpal 'dzin gyi
pod chung / bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa'i 'khrid yig za ma tog la 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i kha 'byed lhan thabs sbyar ba'i rim lnga'i dmar
'khrid/ kha che paN chen lugs kyi bde mchog dkar po'i nyams 'khrid/ rigs 'dzin chen po legs ldan rdo rjes chu bo ri nas gdan drangs pa'i bla ma sku gsum gyi nyams 'khrid/
'khrid yig so so'i lung / gtsug tor dri med lha lnga'i dbang / bir srung nang ma'i byin rlabs/ jo bo'i chos chung brgya rtsa/ rtogs brjod dpag bsam 'khri shing / gsar ma
rgyud 'bum nas rgyud che chung bsdoms pa re lnga dang bcas pa'i ljags lung 'bul ba gnang / de nas la mor tshangs

pa dung gi thor tshugs can gyi gnas khang du phebs/ chos skyong khog tu brlams pas bsu ba mdzad/ tshogs 'khor spyan gzigs gya nom pa bstab/ spyi sgos kyi dri ba gnang bar mkhan
po rang gi thugs la lkog gyur gyi chos kun gsal bzhin du dri ba mdzad spyi sgos sogs bstod bsngags dang bcas sku rim gyis mtshon pa'i blang dor gnang rgyu'i lan zhib
tu phul zhing khyed sngon rje 'bangs nyer lnga'i nang nas gnubs nam mkha'i snying po'i rnam 'phrul yin zhes ngos 'dzin mdzad pa gter ston 'ja' tshon snying pos rje 'bangs
nyer lnga'i khrod nas gcig yin gsung ba'i rgyab chos su song bas yid ches kyi gnas su nges/ bka' 'gyur gyi ljags lung gnang ba'i sbyin bdag sde pa rnam sras gling pas mdzad
pa'i sa dpyad grub na'ang / mtshungs med nyi ma gling nas kyis gong dkar rdo rje gdan rang du btsugs na gnas bzang zhing tshogs 'du che ba dang / bstan pa phyogs mthar
rgyas pa'i rten 'brel yod tshul gsungs pa ltar nam mthong sa zla ba'i tshes bcu skor la kun mkhyen 'jigs med dpa' bo'i gdan sa gsang ba sngags kyi chos sde chen por thegs/
thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po'i gzims spyil klu dbang gling du rdo rje brag nas rigs 'dzin sprul pa'i sku mchog /skyed tshal gong 'og gi mkhan po/ sna mo shag grub chen
mi pham karma sangs rgyas sogs phyogs 'dus kyi don gnyer can du ma dang rdo rje gdan gyi gra tshang khag gi slob dpon 'ga' zhig brel bsam 'byor zhing / rin po che nyi
ma gling pas bskal bzang / dkon brtsegs/ 'jam dpal rnam par rol pa/ rnam par 'phrul pa/ pad dkar rnam gsum sogs kha shas las tshang mar bsnyun nas 'byon ma thub/ de phyin
chos 'chad pa rnams kyis gtsos pa'i gra pa rags bsdus la 'o skol gyi ston pa rgyal ba zas gtsang gi sras po rdo rje gdan gyi spor bdud bzhi las rnam par rgyal ba'i byang
chub brnyes pa'i tshul bstan te mchog gi sprul pa'i sku'i rnam par rol pa'i dus chen tshes bco lnga la thog mar rten 'brel khyad kyi mdo sde bskal pa bzang po nas rim pa
bzhin dbu 'dzugs pa gnang ba de'i tshe nam mkha' thams cad dri ma dang bral ba'i g.ya' dag par chos sde'i khyon dang mnyam par chu 'dzin gyis nyi 'od mi sgrib pa zhig nas
rgya gar skad du gsung ba dang lhan cig par sa sbangs pa'i char shar gyis babs shing sngar phan char dkon pa yod pa la de nyin nas dkar phyogs kyi lha rnams dga' ba'i chos
yon gyi ched du phab cing thag ring ba tshos mthong ba na klu dbang gling la 'ja' zug pa sogs bla ma dang chos kyi che bas gzur gnas rnams mi phyed pa'i dad pa la bkod/
mdo sde za ma tog gi skabs tshogs pa rnams la yig drug gsung ba/ ye shes rgyas pa'i mdo'i dus sangs rgyas kyi mtshan re 'dzin dgos tshul gyi bslab bya dang bka' 'gyur
lce thog nas tshar re sgrog pa'i dam bca' 'bul mi kha shas byung / de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa la thub pa 'od srungs kyis gdul bya rnams gtad pa bzhin du nga'i bstan
pa la rab tu byung ba la sogs pa byams par yongs su gtad pa yin no sogs gsung skabs bdag cag la ston pa bde bar gshegs pa thugs brtse/ zhes spyan chab rgyun ring bar snang
/ des mtshon khyim pa byin rlabs zhu mkhan gyi rna bar byams pas dam bcas pa'i gzungs tshar re sgrog par

mdzad/ sa skyong bsod nams rab brtan la g.yar po zhus pa'i bka' 'gyur mtshal par ma dang / chos sde'i bka' 'gyur gnyis la zhar byung du zhus dag pa'i yi ge'i 'du byed dge slong
'phrin las rnam rgyal dang / gong dkar gyi glegs bam khrod du ma bzhugs pa 'dra mtshal par ma'i steng nas lung gnang ba zhal snga nas brag sna bas sde par snyan phra
phul na'ang yar bzhes rgyu thugs kyis bsnyel nas ljags lung gi bgegs su ma song bar gda'/ mdo mangs thor bu/ dkon brtsegs/ phal chen/ sher phyogs skor grub nas/ de yang
sngar ngor du bsgrubs pa gnang ba de phyag len mkhan slob kha skong tshang ma khungs btsun na'ang shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis yar klungs rnam rgyal du tshag mig mkhan
chen dka' bzhi tshul khrims rin cen la bsgrubs pa'i sdom rgyun yin la/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan gyi sdom rgyun la sa paN brgyud par bzhugs pa dang / phyogs de'i gdul bya
rjes 'dzin la dgongs te smin drug zla ba'i tshes nyi shu'i gza' lhag pa dang skar ma rgyal 'dzom pa'i nyin snga dro sdom pa 'bul ba gnang ba'i brda chad tsam du tsar mo'i
steng na bza' dkar po zhig bzhes/ phyi dro gnas brtan 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po tshul khrims bkra shis bas mkhan slob sbrags ma/ gsang ston skyid tshal 'og mkhan po ngag
dbang bstan 'dzin/ dus sgo ba rab 'byams chos rje rin cen rgya mtsho/ kha skong ba brag thog pa shAkya mchog ldan sogs dad pa'i dge 'dun grangs tshang ba'i dbus su tshigs
snga ma dge bsnyen nas bzung ste sdom gsum rim gyis mnos pa'i nyi ma ri rked la yod dus bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i sdom pa thugs rgyud la bstar/ de nas zhag lnga tsam na
'dul lung khyim pa'i spyod yul du ma 'os shing rab byung sha stag dgos pa chos sde gnyis kyi gra rigs nyi shu skor gyis nyi ma gling du sku ngo sbran pas rje tshul khrims
bkra shis kyis da lam bskyar bzhes gnang nas yun ring ma song yang mkhan po'i bya ba mdzad dgos par gsol ba bzhin rje nyid kyis mkhan po/ mtshungs med nyi ma gling pas las
slob bstar te rtses dang chen mo byang ma pa ngag dbang bstan 'dzin gyis gtsos pa'i bsnyen rdzogs pa kha shas dang rdo rje brag sprul sku rin po che dpon slob lnga dge
tshul du bsgrub pa gnang ba'i chen mo byang ma pa'i mtshan la slar byams pa bsnan te 'dogs par mdzad/ chos zhu ba po rnams kyis dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i dbang thob gshis
gsang sgrog gi nyes pa mi 'byung yang rgyud dang 'brel pa'i lha'i rig gtad lta bu byung na phyag len gtsang ba'i dbang du mdzad zur bka'i dkyil 'khor la rjes gnang gi srol
mi 'dug rung / sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i kye rdor/ gsang 'dus 'jam rdor/ he ru kaHphyag gnyis pa/ bdag med ma/ gshin rje'i gshed dmar nag /phag mo lha lnga/ phyag rdor/
mi g.yo ba/ spyan ras gzigs gtso 'khor gsum pa/ gur mgon/ mgon po phyag bzhi pa/ zur bka' sna tshogs yum/ khro phu'i 'jam dkar/ phyag rdor 'gro bzang sogs spyi bka' zur
bka' skabs su gang babs nas rgyud sde tshan du phye ba phal cher dang 'brel bar sngon du rjes gnang re mdzad pa'i rgyud 'bum nas bde mchog mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho la sogs
pa'i sngags yas mas dkrugs pa rnams bsdebs pas mtshon mdor na chos bshad pa'i dus tshod snga phyi sogs gang la'ang

thugs brel gyi rjes su mi 'brang zhing dpon slob rnams kyi kun tu spyod pa'ang mdo rgyud las/ ji ltar byung ba ltar bstan rgyun la dgongs pa'i thugs ru shin tuu nga ba'i sgo
nas chos sde'i rigs gra dang rnal 'byor rgyud kyi sgrub mchod sogs la rta ma chag tsam dang gzhan ma nyi khyongs su gnang ba hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i tshes bco lnga la legs
par grub cing rten 'brel khyad kyis bstan 'gyur gsan khrod nas po ti gsum tsam dang / chos zhu ba'i tshogs la nyin re bzhin mang ja gnyis re chad med dang / kun mkhyen
bu/ rje rdo rje gdan pa/ tshar chen/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse khu dbon rnams kyi dus dran la bka' 'gyur rin po cher rgya mchod/ tshogs su mang ja 'phar ma/ skabs 'gar chos
ston mdzug tu grol ston gyis tshim pa sogs bsdu ba rnam pa bzhi'i sgo nas rjes su bzung zhing gnyug mar gnas pa dang glo bur du lhags pa'i khong nas rdo rje brag sprul
sku rin po che'i yab gzhis nas bsnyen bkur gzabs rgyas lan gnyis/ gzhan phal cher gyis mang ja'i thog 'byor pa dang bstun pa'i zang zing gi bdog pa maNDal du bteg /mtsho
sngon po'i sgar thog nas dharma kho ya tha'i ji bod du btang skabs nged rang nas 'phrin gsol dngul gyi rten ldan brtan bzhugs kyi tshigs bcad dang bcas phul ba chos zhu
ba rnams kyis shes nas 'phral du btsugs te nyin star gyis gsung ba sogs rten 'brel 'grig cing gzhan don du dgongs nas brtan bzhugs gsol 'debs su bsgyur te deng sang kyang
tshogs 'don chag med du yod snang / chos grol rjes rten 'brel gyi khyad nas skya ser gyi khrom chen po tshogs par phyi rol gyi rdo cal bzhugs khri'i thog tu phebs shing
'jam dbyangs sa paN gyi dbu zhwas zhu mchod/ grub rgyal lugs kyi lha gcig bum gcig la brten pa'i tshe dbang / da lam gyi chos 'khor 'di la brten pa'i 'chad nyan zhabs tog
mthun rkyen sgrubs so cog kun gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams byang chub chen por bsngo ba'i yon bshad/ bkra shis kyi mtha' brten dang bcas rgyas par stsal ba ni/ kun mkhyen
mkhyen brtse'i gsung mgur las/ gang 'di'i thub bstan tha mar gyur pa'i mthus/ /ji snyed chos kyi bka' babs chad gyur cing / /cung zad lus rnams 'chad la nye ba 'di/ /bsams
bzhin snying nas ma dga' shes par 'phyo/ /rgyal ba'i bstan pa mchog la dad pa dang / /mar gyur 'gro la brtse ba'i lhag bsam gyis/ /phan bde'i 'byung gnas thub bstan rin
chen sgron/ /spel ba'i thabs la snying nas spro bar gyur/ /zhes pa'i don dang mthun par mchis so/ /rin cen tshul khrims bkra shis dang gsung gleng la ri phug tu lo gsum
ma'i skabs sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i lha rnams kyi bsnyen pa tshad du 'khyol ba khyad par bya rgyud la legs grub kyi dgongs pa bzhin g.yal dang sbrid pa sogs byung na phreng
skor gcig pu de grangs su mi brtsi bas mtshon phra mo rnams la'ang thugs rung tshul gsungs pa dpyod ldan 'phrin las rnam rgyal gyi thos 'dzin du gyur par ya mtshan du
'dzin zhing kho bo'ang rjes su yi rang ngo / /nye skor nas zhing 'khyar kha shas gzigs pa hor zla bdun pa'i rnal 'byor rgyud kyi sgrub mchod thebs su nyin gcig 'phar ba'i
spyor 'jags gnang / de nas mi ring bar rnam snang mngon byang la nyer lngar gcod mi dgos pa rgyud kyi dgongs

pa dang dam pa'i phyag bzhes bzhin chos sde yas mas kyi gra pa bzhi bcur dbang / gtsug dgu'i dbang cha/ grangs bco lngar dril bu lus dkyil gyi dbang / rnam sras sprin gseb
ma dang dzam la dmar po yum bcas kyi rjes gnang / skyed tshal 'og gzhi pa slob dpon pa sogs la spyan ras gzigs tshem bu lugs kyi dmar 'khrid kyis mtshon 'dod chos kha shas
stsal/ sngon chad yongs 'dzin mang por mdo rgyud kyi gdams pa rgya cher gsan yang lo chen ratna bha dras/ chos pa'i so nam yin pas thos bsam byas/ /chos kyi rtsa ba yin
pas gnas lugs bsgoms/ /chos la 'bras bu dgos pas smon lam btab/ /sgo gsum tha mal nam yang bzhag ma myong / /sngon chad gdams ngag brgya phrag du ma bslabs/ /'on kyang da
dung gzhan la 'tshol bar 'dod/ /ces pa ltar slar yang ngoms pa med par thos bsam mdzad bzhed kyi chu mo sbrul lo shar nas gtsang phyogs su gshegs zhor lcags zam sprul pa'i
sku kun dga' bsod nams dbang phyug gi drung du 'khrid brgya sogs zab chos kha yar gsan zhing / ngor e waM chos ldan/ gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skya/ slob dpon chen
po'i sgrub gnas ri bo bkra bzang sogs su zhabs pad kyi phreng ba bkod na'ang / rje mkhyen brtse'i gsung mgur du/ bdud kyis dbang sgyur skal ngan ches mang bas/ /dam chos
'tshol la 'gal rkyen char bzhin 'bab/ /mthun rkyen mi 'byung phyung yang stobs zhan pas/ /ji ltar bsams pa bzhin du grub ma gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ ngor mkhan chen shar
pa shes rab 'byung gnas dang / bkra bzang pa chen po nam mkha' rigs 'dzin gnyis sku na ha cang smin par ma gyur rung bstan pa'i gegs chags lta bus dag zhing gzhan dag
tu sgyu 'phrul gyi bkod pa bsdus pa dang 'grig cing sngags 'chang bla ma sems dpa' chen po khri chen 'jam dbyangs ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams rtsa dkar gyi bsten babs
lci ba sogs gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi bdag po nyi ma'i gnyen gyi ring lugs la bi nA ya'i cho 'phrul cung zad nus pa'i dus dang 'grig pas chos gsan rtsis rnams bzhed pa
dang mthun pa ma byung na yang bzhi thog tu bdag chen khri chen rin po che nas bdag rkyen tshad med pa dang bcas lugs gnyis dang 'brel ba'i bka' mchid kyi rim pa zhib rgyas
su stsal/ mchod khang dang mgon khang ches mang ba mtha' dag mjal bar phebs pa'i tshe dngos bshams yid sprul gyi mchod pa dang / 'jig rten khams su bde skyid rgya cher
'byung ba'i smon lam mdzad/ nged gong nas phyir 'khor ba'i hor zla bcu gcig pa'i nang du ngos 'phrad la dga' ldan pho brang du phebs te thugs dgyes pa'i gsung gleng bag
phebs par mdzad/ byes lam du yul dus gnas skabs kyi rang dbang 'du mi 'du dang gtso bor le lo dang snying rus gnyis tshong thebs pa'i kha ton dge sbyor byed blo rnams mos
'dun tsam du lus gshis chag med bzhi gsos shing / bsam mi khyab kyi byin rlabs/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yi ge brgya pa/ phyag btsal ba'i phan yon 'ga' zhig /gdugs dkar gzhan
gyis mi thub pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses mdzad pa'i dri med kyi srog shing 'dzugs chog rnams kyi lung dang / sngar gung thang du gnang rtsis kyi gtor gshoms grub mtshams
gnam ngo chen po glo bur du byung ba 'ong gseb tu bshor na dpon slob gnyis kar skur 'debs byung dogs kyi

gshol ba gnang 'dug pa da lam zhal gsang 'khrid dang shis bstan pa'i rjes gnang yang zhus/ rje bla ma dam par byang lugs phyag len gyi tshe dpag med lcags sdong brgya rtsa/
rigs 'dzin ratna gling pa klong gsal gyi tshe dbang / chos rgyal bkra shis stobs rgyal gyi mtsho skyes rdo rje sku gsum rigs 'dus kyi dbang lung rnams phul zhing gter gsar
gyi tshe mda' rtse sor gsum tsam 'phel bas sku tshe'i rten 'brel 'grig /rgya nag nas 'khor ba'i skyes ma dang chos yon sbrags pa'i maNDal rgyas par bteg cing yar lam gung
thang du zhag shas bzhugs te rim gyis bkra shis rtse chos sder thegs/ da dung tshe 'di'i che thabs bsgrubs kyang 'grub par dka' zhing / /grub kyang skyid mod ngang nas
gnas ngan du mar 'khrid pas/ /ci byas dam pa'i chos dang yang yang rjes su bstun nas/ /chos brgyad spong ba'i thabs la 'bad pa bgyid pa ma gtogs/ /tshe 'di'i mdun ma sgrub
pa'i zhe 'dod med pa zhig gda'o/ /zhes rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung mgur las byung ba ltar/ lo sngon ma 'bras spungs su phebs skabs gsung gleng la da cha lo'ang mang
du lon cing de bar sde dgon gyi kha 'dzin sogs ban bun gyi g.yeng ba'i ngang du zad pa zhig byung ba tshe mjug 'di la dben pa bsten nas dge sbyor la chig sgril byed 'dun
yod gnang bar da dung dgung lo sogs ha cang gi mtho bar ma zin cing sku gzugs kyis rkyen mi theg pa'ang mi 'dug pas re zhig spyi sgos kyi chos rgyun spel bas mtshon par
thugs las chung ngur ma song ba dgos tshul zhus shing shing rta chos sde pa tshor de mtshungs kyi bslab ston gnang bar gra rigs sbyin bdag skya ser thams cad kyis mgrin
gcig tu gsol ba btab pa sogs gang ci nas thugs dbang ma 'dus par brten da cha tshe dang sgrub pa mnyam pa ma thub tshe g.yeng ba byed rin chog pa bgyid gsung thog babs su
bka' 'gyur bzheng ba'i dgongs pa bstad nas shog bu sgrub pa'i sta gon dus sde pa blo bzang mthu stobs kyi gcung gsung rab rgya mtshos snag tsha dang smyig rgyu'i sig phul
bas rten 'brel 'grig ces dgyes par gyur/ shog bu sgrub mi slebs pa dang mon nas shog tshong pa gtos can yongs pa 'grig pas gnas po yang dus gcig la bka' 'gyur ldangs 'di
'dra yong ba thugs rje rang du go ba'i dad pa lhag par skyes te 'bras kyi skyes phul zhing srung ba zhus/ la la dag thugs rig la steng shod med dam phyag rdzas stobs che
ba med par thugs gra 'di 'dra bsgrig zhes thugs lhus ma things pa'i skur zhus byed pa byung na'ang rgyal ba tsong kha pa chen pos rdzing phyi'i zhig gsos kyi tshe dpon
slob bcu gnyis kyi sku chas la zi gong brgyab par gser zho bcu gnyis las ma byung ba de nub rnam sras la 'dzin gtor zhig gnang bas sang nas yo byad 'bad med du byung zhing
thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun grub pa/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / paN chen shAka mchog pa lta bu'ang snyoms chung bya bral gyi ngang nas bkra shis lhun po/ e waM chos ldan/
gser mdog can gyi chos sde btab pas mtshan 'phags bod kyi gang zag khyad par can rnams gnas skabs su 'dod yon la mi dgyes pas gsog 'jog mi mdzad kyang chos ldan gyi
mdzad pa rgya chen po'i dus nam mkha' mdzod la mnga' 'byor ba'i shugs kyis 'bad rtsol la mi ltos pa'o/ /'jig

rten mthun 'jug zang zing bdog pa la/ /phan tshun skyes su bstar ba don ldan du/ /byed pa'i ngang tshul mthong na dam chos nor/ /gtong len 'di ko dam pa'i rnam par thar/ /sngon
'dus lo paN mkhas grub mang byon nas/ /rgyal bstan dar tshe rtsol bar ci zhig ltos/ /'chad nyan dgun gyi chu bran ltar gyur ding / /thos bsam khur gyi ljid la lhag par
rangs/ /snga phyir 'gyur ba'i smin grol man ngag lung / /padma'i skud par rdo rje bzhu blugs pas/ /srog 'tsho'i rig byed dran pa'i mkhyen dpyod kyi/ /tshangs ris grub
pa'i lha de gzhan min drang / /sprul zhing lta na sdug nas 'ongs min par/ /skye rgu'i srog 'tsho sman gyi bla ma dngos/ /ging chen tshangs pas bsnyems btang gang gi zhabs/
/nam mkha'i snying por nges te gtsug tu blangs/ /lha min dmod pa'i lcags tims ma skyes par/ /gzur gnas blo yi dpal be'u snying ga ru/ /ri mo rab bkra'i skal ldan nabs so
skyes/ /khyod zhal bdud rtsi 'thung la lhag par rings/ /rnam gsum chos 'khor dus gcig yongs bskor bar/ /dkar phyogs lha rnams dga' mgur lta ba la/ /manda ra yi smin legs
phreng mdzes dang / /khor yug dbang gzhu'i dra bas sbrel phyir brdzu/ /g.yas ru'i 'dzin mar 'khrul med lam ston shes/ /nyung zad tsam yang ma bzod lus med mdas/ /re zhig
bzhed pa'i dka' thub 'jig nus pa/ /ches cher lnga bdo'i shugs de gang gis bzlog /'dam skyes 'dam gyis ma gos padma ltar/ /'khor nas 'khor ba'i rgya las yongs grol yang
/ /slob lam slob pa'i ched du zhi bde la/ /nges par nges 'byung tshul gyis 'drid de ci/ /nam mkha'i ska rags ma des 'ching dka' ba'i/ /grangs med 'gro 'dren thugs bskyed
rdo ba'i ngos/ /bris pa'i ri mo sems can zad pa'i mtha'/ /de srid mi yal rgyal sras spyod pa'i gshis/ /myos byed ces pa shing lug zla ba gsum pa'i tshes dgu la chos sde chen
po dpal ldan 'bras spungs su phebs pa'i zhar byung du gra dar rgyas chos sdings su gdan grangs yab rje gnubs chen sprul pa'i zlos gar dang gdung brgyud bgres pa chos
rgyal gter bdag gling pa gnyis la dpal kye rdo rje man ngag lugs dang dze tA ri'i tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang gnang / tshur rig 'dzin phrin las lhun grub la gter chos ci
rigs pa gsan te rim gyis dga' ldan pho brang du zhag dgu'i bar stan chags pa'i dus 'khor bdag po chen po'i dbang / sindhu ra la brten pa'i bdag med lha mo bco lnga/ bde
mchog dkar bo/ tog tse ba'i bsam mi khyab gsum gyi byin rlabs/ aShta'i bzlas lung / gur sprin gseb ma'i rjes gnang / sum pa lo tsA'i blo sbyong dang tshem bu lugs kyi dmar
khrid gnyis 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i zin bris steng nas nyams 'khrid snga dgongs so sor smin rgyas/ rje btsun grol mchog gi 'khrid brgya'i skor yongs rdzogs/ dam chos
dgongs pa yang zab kyi chos skor phal cher/ bstan gnyis gling pa'i rta glud/ kye rdor dbang chog gi lhan thabs tshar chen gyis mdzad pa/ de'i sbyin sreg dang sAtstsha
'debs chog kun mkhyen mkhyen brtses mdzad pa/ rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i byang gter skye bdun sgrub thabs/ sambhu Ta rgyud phyi ma dang bcas pa/ gsang ba ring bsrel/ byang
chub rgyan 'bum/ las sgrib rnam sbyong / rten 'brel snying po/ 'od zer can ma/ dug sel ma/ gdugs dkar mchog grub/

rnam rgyal ma'i gzungs rtog pa dang bcas pa/ ngan 'gro sbyong ba'i rnam rgyal/ gtsug tor dri med/ mchod pa'i sprin gyi gzungs/ rgyal mtshan rtse mo'i dpung rgyan/ mig nad sbyong
ba/ gzhang 'brum zhi ba/ nad thams cad rab tu zhi ba/ chi rgod rnam 'joms/ byams pas dam bcas pa'i gzungs/ gza' yum/ nor rgyun ma/ tshe dpag med kyi snying po/ mi 'khrugs
pa'i rgyud/ stobs po che/ rgyal po mdo lnga sogs mdo phran kha shas rnams kyi lung zhus shing 'phrang 'go gter ston gyi tshe dpag med sku gsum rigs 'dus kyi dbang
phul/ rim gyis gung thang brgyud de bkra shis chos kyi sde chen por phebs pa'i e rig pa'i 'byung gnas chos lung dkar po nas dbon yig mkhas pa don bdun bos par dbu ma lugs
kyi sems bskyed dang thos grol gyi ljags lung / sa ga zla ba sku bltams pa'i dus chen yar tshes bdun gyi res gza' lhag pa dang skar ma rgyal gyi 'phrod dge bar bka' 'gyur
rin po che bzheng pa'i dbu btsugs pa'i tshugs ston rtses dang nas sna mo shag grub chen karma sangs rgyas kyis bsnyen bkur brgya 'bul bzabs rgyas su bstar/ de skabs yar
shar nub tshor bshal rims mched pa'i shi chad kha yar byung bar sha brgya zan brgya gtong ba gnang bas yams nad rnams ring por ma lon par chad cing lhag par bkra shis rtse
zhol du nad pa mangs par yig mkhan rnams tshab tshub tu gyur tshe srung ba gnang bas 'dzem med du phyin kyang 'go ba gtan ma byung bas mos pa lhag par 'phel/ hor zla lnga
pa'i nang du khyab bdag zha lu pa chen po slob bshad zhu ba la phebs par bka' 'gyur ma grub pas 'dzugs pa gnang ma thub pa'i de'i ring sgrub thabs rgya mtsho/ gsar ma
rgyud 'bum/ gshed dmar spros med kyi 'khrid sogs 'bul ba gnang zhing / tshur yang 'khor lo sdom chen sogs dbang lung mang du gsan/ rnam sras gling pas gtsos sbyin bdag skya
ser rnams kyis dus ston gyi thog legs 'bul gyi bdog pa rgya cher bstabs pa'i tshogs gsog la brten phogs ja thug gi gtong chas mtshon dgos cha mtha' dag ngang gis 'grub
pa'i sgo nas zla ba phyed bdun du nye ba hor zla bcu pa'i tshes bco brgyad la zhal khebs gdong dar glegs shing glegs thag glegs chab sogs cha 'grig legs par grub/ gong
dkar du ljags lung gnang skabs bka' 'gyur gyi nang nas byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi mtshan zur du phyung ba khri lhag bcas thor bkod pa 'di dang dus mtshungs su sa le sbram
zhun ma'i khu bas bris legs phun sum tshogs pa gong gsham zhal khebs tog bcas/ shing par la brten nas zhal bkod gnang ba'i byang chub mchod rten bcu tshar mi tshad tsam/
nang bzhugs gzungs sngags sAtstsha phyag dar ba'i 'bum phrag gnang steng nas gang 'gro dang gsol phud kyi sAtstsha sogs kyis gtams par lhang tser btul ma'i na bza' gsol
te bla g.ye'i sgo'i g.yas g.yon gyi thog 'og tu bzhugs su gsol ba rnams kyi smon lam gsung rtsom 'di lta ste/ lha rigs 'a zha'i dge slong byang chub sems/ /gsang sngags kun
'dzin mgon po bsod nams kyis/ /sngon byon mkhas grub rnams kyi rjes zhugs nas/ /rgyal ba'i bstan pa yun ring rgyas phyir dang / /mtha' yas 'gro la phan pa lhur len phyir/
/rgyal ba'i gsung rab dam chos 'gyur ro 'tshal/ /dka' ba du mas kun nas lung nos shing / /bstan 'gror phan

phyir lung yang 'bad pas bgyis/ /glegs bam thams cad dus gcig 'bad pas bsgrubs/ /bka' 'gyur nas bstan rdzogs sangs rgyas pa'i sku/ /khri phrag brgal ba'i gser gyi bris sku
dang / /sAtstsha 'bum phrag byang chen mchod rten bcu/ /de sogs rnam dkar dri med dge ba'i mthus/ /bdag dang pha ma spun zla ming sring dang / /bran g.yog las byed khal khur
dud 'gror bcas/ /phan thogs yi rang dkar nag 'dres pa kun/ /sgrib byang tshogs rdzogs rnam mkhyen myur thob shog /ces pa mdzad/ de ltar sku gsung thugs rten rnams la
rgyud thams cad kyi rgyal po gnyis su med pa dpal dgyes pa rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi sgrub mchod dang 'brel ba'i sgo nas rab gnas bkra shis rgya mtsho la rje rdo rje 'chang
dbang phyug rab brtan gyi phyag bzhes kyis brgyan te rab tu gnas pa nyin gsum ma mnga' dbul gyi dus rgyas pa dang cho ga'i mthar lhag chad kha skong ba'i zhi ba'i sbyin
sreg dang bcas rgyal kun gsang ba rab 'byams kyi 'khor lo ma lus pa rten brten pa lha'i tshogs chu dang 'o ma bzhin ro gcig tu mdzad pas phyogs kun bkra shis dang bde legs
kyis khyab par gyur/ bris pas gtsos bzo bo'i tshogs yon rdzongs su gser gos dar ja ras g.yu byu ru spos shel go khrab khro zangs rta drel pho mo'i gos sna snam phrug
sogs kyi rnyed pas blo'i re ba yongs su bkang ste tshim par mdzad/ zla ba de ka'i tshes nyi shu'i rgyal phur gyi 'grub sbyor nas bzung mkhan chen zha lu pa khyab bdag rin
cen bsod nams mchog grub/ 'bras yul skyed tshal mkhan po byams pa ngag dbang bstan 'dzin/ rtse tshogs dum bu chos 'khor sogs phyogs nas 'dus pa dang / gnyug mar gnas pa
bcas dge 'dun du ma'i tshogs la dus gsum bder gshegs rnams kyi bgrod pa gcig pa'i lam mdo rgyud man ngag kun gyi yang bcud/ 'phags yul grub dbang birWa pa chen po la rje
btsun rdo rje btsun mos mngon sum du gnang ba'i lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa/ 'bras bu lam dang bcas pa/ gcig shes pas mang po grol ba/ skyon yon tan dang bar chad dngos grub
tu blang ba/ ltas ngan g.yang du len pa/ ting nge 'dzin ngo shes pas bsam gtan gyi gegs sel ba/ bar chad ngo shes pas bdud kyi gegs sel ba/ sde snod gsum gyi de nyid shes
pas gser 'gyur gyi rtsi lta bu/ mchog thun gyi dngos grub ma lus pa 'byung ba'i gsung ngag rin po che'i 'khrid bod yul 'dir 'jig rten gyi mig gcig pu 'brog mi lo tsA ba
chen pos legs par bsgyur ba nas bzung bshad srol mi 'dra ba mang du byung ba'i gtso bo rdo rje 'chang dang zhal gnyis pa rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras la bka' babs pa tshogs
bshad dang slob bshad gnyis las rjes 'brangs mkhas grub phal cher la ma grags pa rin cen sgang pa gdung brgyud sgos kyi zab chos lta bu gsang chen slob bshad kyi nyams
'khrid zab mo dbang byin rlabs rgyab brten lung dang bcas pa mtha' dag zla ba phyed bzhi lhag tsam gyi bar gnang rjes dgyes pa rdo rje'i rgya gzhung so gnyis tsam gnang
ba'i dus kho bos ngor rdzong tshar lugs gsum ga'i lam 'bras thob pas rgyun gsum ga yod gshis gang 'dod kyi rjes su 'brangs chog ces bka' stsal zhing / me sprel hor zla
gnyis pa'i tshes brgyad la gegs med du grub pa ni/ sbyang gzhi dkyil 'khor rnam bzhi'i zhing sa mchog tu gshin

po/ /sbyong byed smin grol rnam bzhi'i chu lud rkyen gyis sbyangs te/ /sbyangs 'bras sku bzhi'i sa bon gang btab mchog tu legs pa'i/ /sa zhing mchog de'i 'dul sbyong bdag rang
mkhas snyam bgyid pas/ /tha rangs thul med kyi zhing la yid smon med pa zhig gda'o/ /zhes thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung mgur las byung ba ltar shin tu smin pa'i grol ston
dang rdo rje chos skyong rnams la gtang rag gi bskang bstod gnang ba'i mjug tsam du gzhan gyis bsreg pa po med par sha chen gyi dris bla brang steng shod med pa khyab
pa'i dam can dgyes pa'i cho 'phrul ci yang mdzad/ zha lu mkhan rin po che yang zhag shas bzhugs par bla ma bka' brgyad yongs 'dus kyi dbang sogs kha yar 'bul ba gnang zhing
rje bla mas kyang nyer mkho'i dbang lung ci rigs gsan/ tshogs la bka' gdams kyi chos skor 'ga' zhig gnang skabs me tog ser po dang dmar po lag pas zin la khad pa'i char
babs/ sgo khang du khra 'brug chos skyong gi rten gtor yod pa lha mi'i bar du sel cung zad byung ba/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyi rten khra 'brug rgyal khang
rang du skyel ba mdzad pa rje 'di la chos skyong gis sngar ltar dgos zhus pa'i lan ras gzhir kho rang ji ltar bzhed pa'i rta glang pags rigs sogs bris pa sngags drug phyag
rgya drug gis brlab pa gnang bar dgyes te mkhan pos 'di ltar byung zhes mi thams cad la ston par mdzad/ sde pa blo bzang mthu stobs 'ol dga' chu tshan khar 'dred brdabs
la gegs kyi rnam pa'i yar klungs su 'byor nas kyang skyed che ba ma byung ba dam pa 'di nyid kyis dbang byin rlabs mang du mdzad pas tsher ma dbyung ba ltar gzhi med du
bde/ nub cig mchod dpon gyis zhabs byug zhu skabs tsid sgra chen po byung ba gang yin nam gsung bar khyi lta bu srog chags shig gi skad yin nam zhus pa na min pa 'dra thug
gi skad yin nam gsung ba ltar phyin pas gzims chung steng du thug gsum yod pa'i dkyil ma rtsis mgon gyi thug de tsi sgra chen po rgyag gin 'dug rung mun pas sgra tsam
las gzhan ma mthong sang zhogs ltas tsa na rnga ma nas khrag 'dzags pas sa gzhi la 'thor zhing rtsa bar khrag snyim pa gang tsam 'khyil ba chos skyong 'di shin tu 'go zhing
bka' gnyan pa yod 'dug pa nas bstan pa spyi sgos kyi dgra bo zhig bsgral ba'i rtags su mchis/ sna mo shag grub chen pas bsam gtan gling gi spyil por sri zhu'i ched du
spyan drangs pa'i phebs zhor tshe chu 'bum pa mjal ba gnang dus tshe chu cher babs pa zla ba brgyad pa yin pas de dus yong ba'i skabs min rung byung bar ya mtshan du 'dzin/
me bya gtsang phyogs su chibs kha bsgyur te gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar phebs/ sngags 'chang bla ma sems dpa' chen po'i zhabs rdul dbu gtsug tu bzhes nas sgrub
thabs brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang / zhabs drung nyid kyis mdzad pa'i phur pa'i chos 'byung sogs ljags lung mang du stsal/ gtso bor gsan bya rnam sras kyi be'u bum yin na'ang
bsam yas kyi sdig khrab sgrog par phebs rings pa'i slar yong ba'i bka' bzhes gnang / zhabs drung khri thog pa ngag dbang bsod nams dbang phyug dang rje btsun ma gnyis la'ang
bka' chos kha yar gsan/ gdan sa dang kha'u bsam brling sogs kyi gnas gzigs gnang / rigs 'dzin lha khang

gi 'gag tu ngor zur 'chad chos rje dpal gling pa dang lhan cig tu 'dzom pa da res rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i khrir 'byon pa'i rten 'brel byed dgos pa 'dug pas ja sngon
la mchod gsung pa de skabs mkhan po yong ba'i dogs pa tsam yang med pas thugs khrel bzhin min nam bsam rung de nas ma 'gyangs par mkhan po byed dgos byung ba mngon mkhyen
du 'dug ces thugs yid ches pa'i dper 'dzin/ bzhi thog tu zhabs drung rin po cher mkha' 'gro bsun bzlog dang 'brel ba'i brtan bzhugs rgyas par phul nas dgung lo brgyad
