cu rtsa lnga'i bar du bzhugs pa'i bka' bzhes zhus par mkhan po rang bstan don la dgongs nas de tsam bzhugs na ni nga yang de ga bgyid de min nged rang gnyis lhan du 'gro
ba yin phebs pa'i gnas tshul rje bla ma 'bras spungs su phebs dus gsung 'phros gnang 'dug cing sa phag hor zla dgu pa'i tshes bcu bzhi la dam pa 'di dang bcu gnyis pa'i
tshes bco brgyad la bdag chen rin po che me tog 'thor ba la dpags na bla ma rnam gnyis sprul gzhi gcig las bstan 'gro'i ched du spro bsdu mdzad dgos par sems/ ngor mkhan
chen rgyal rtse zhabs drung byams pa ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi drung du ne gu nas brgyud pa'i dbang byin rlabs/ rtsa ba ne gu chos drug /sdong po phyag rgya
chen po/ yal ga lam khyer rnam gsum/ me tog mkha' spyod dkar dmar/ 'bras bu 'chi med rang grol rnams kyi 'khrid lung sogs tshang ba gsan/ de nas rim bzhin khu lung du phebs/
de yang bla ma sog bzlog pa nas brgyud pa'i mdo dbang ches dar na'ang / sog bzlog pa'i zhus rigs 'dzin g.yu 'brug rdo rje shangs rta nag pa'i yul mi rnams la rgyus med
pa'i dpyod ldan tsho the tshom gyi gzhir mdzad gshis rigs 'dzin chen po mnga' ris pa nas brgyud pa bla chen chos rgyal rdo rje la khyab bdag sman lung pas gsan pa'i bskul
ma'ang bla ma dam pa 'di nyid kyis gnang zhing nye char rje sman lung pa gdan drangs te rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor la brten nas gsan la spel ba'i bzhed pa ma grub rung
rjes su rdo rje brag nas rigs 'dzin sprul sku rin po ches khyab bdag khra tshang pa chen por gsan nas dbus gtsang khams gsum du dar rgyas kyi bstan pa'i me ro bslang ba
yang rje 'di'i bdag rkyen las byung bar sems so/ /zur thams cad mkhyen pa hor zla bdun pa'i nyer lnga la padma 'od kyi zhing khams su sku'i bkod pa bsdus pa'i thugs dam 'dogs
bcas 'bul ba dang rten bzhengs kyi gzungs bzhugs rab gnas la phebs dgos pa'i snyan gsan phul zhing zhal gyis 'ches na'ang sa skyong bsod nams rab brtan gyis byung na
dge lugs pa zhig rab de min rnying ma pa zhig byung na mngon chung ba yong / sa skya pa'i rigs bos na mi yong ba'i bkag cha mdzad par brten skor cig phebs mi dgos pa'i rgyu
mtshan 'bul mi mngags pa gam pa lar mjal bas bka' las nged dpon slob gnyis sngon la su song yang rjes kyi bya ba byed pa'i cha don yod pa nas da lam nga la babs thob
yod kyang rten 'brel 'phyugs gsungs nas ma mnyes pa'i tshul mdzad/ rngog zhabs drung mkha' spyod kyi gnas su gshegs pa'i gzhung sbrel shing du shar mar phebs/ rje btsun 'jam
dbyangs 'od zer gyi sku gdung dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bor gyur pa la me mchod dang gdung tsha bzhugs pa'i thugs

rten gyi ljags bkod dang bcas skor cig stan chags/ ngor pa'i khams pa bsnyen chen nyer gcig song zer ba gnam rab bsam gtan sgrub sde pa dge slong shes rab dpal bzang mjal bar
'ongs pa khyod kyi ga'u'i nang du ci yod kyi dri ba gnang bar/ byin rlabs min pa gzhan med zhus pas/ spyan cher gzigs nas de min pa zhig yod pas ga'u ston dang gsung nas
kha phye bas kho rang lag nag pa'i dgra la las sbyor byed bsams pa'i dug khrag gi rdzas thum yod pa bton nas mer bsregs pa gnang ba dge slong gi bsam par ngan sems de
mkhyen song snyam pa'i blo 'jigs zhum pa byung skad/ mar lam rgyal grub gling 'og gi 'obs rags bsam grub sgang pa'i bu mo 'jig rten pha rol tu 'gro bar nye bar byin rlabs
gnang bas nad gdon las grol te gzhi med gyur ba'i ming shi lhogs su 'dogs par mdzad do/ /bdag rgyud tha rangs zhing sar blo sbyong dang / /dmar 'khrid gdams pa'i myu gu
ci yang bskyed/ /nges gsang byin rlabs rjes gnang bklag lung gi /bka' drin byang chen de srid 'khor nus min/ /zas gtsang sras kyi rnam gsum 'khor lo'i bka'/ /rgyal blon lo
paN mthu las 'gyur ro cog /bskrun la bya dka' kun bzod khur mthong tshe/ /mi sngon rus sbal gzugs sprul gtam du zad/ /thub gsung las rnyed khri phrag brgal ba'i sku/ /byang
chub mchod rten bcu phrag gzungs bzhugs can/ /sman ljongs yar klungs skye rgu'i legs byas su/ /grub 'di tshangs pa min pa byed po su/ /lus med thul dang de sras slob
mar bcas/ /dag zhing rgya mtsho'i gnas kyi ye shes sems/ /spyan drangs mchod bstod me tog char dbab par/ /lhun pos nyi zla'i sgron me bteg nas lta/ /bzo rig gtsug lag yangs
por sbyangs pa'i mig /dri med gsal ba'i dpyod ldan der tshogs kun/ /gtong ba'i phyag ring brkyang tshe ngal gsos bu'i/ /bang mdzod phye zhes legs bris mdun sar sgrog
/bkra shis rgyal mtshan 'chang ba byang gling pa'i/ /yang srid rin chen bsod nams mchog grub sogs/ /snod ldan du ma'i sgra 'dzin dbang po ru/ /tshad ma bzhi ldan snyan brgyud
pi waM brdungs/ /tshul 'di'i ched du dgongs rtse nyer gtod pa/ /ma 'ongs brtse chen bla ma'i khyad par gyi/ /zab don bka' babs chu bo mi nub pa'i/ /dri bral ye shes
gzigs par da gdod khums/ /legs ldan dgra srog la rngam khus sgra dang / /lhan cig dmar chen argha chal chil 'dzag /rab smin 'bras bu khur du dud pa'i tshe/ /'dzad med bdud
rtsi'i chu rgyun ci yang 'bab/ /'khon rigs 'jam dpal dpa' bo'i zhal gyi lung / /ro bda'i bu ram snyan gyi bcud du mngar/ /bsod nams rgyal mtshan rje btsun e waM pa'i/ /khrir
'byon lkog gyur gnas de mngon sum mkhyen/ /bskal brgyar tshe byin brlabs nus sa chen gyi/ /yon tan khyod kyis gzhan la dngom pa'i tshe/ /sngags 'chang che des spangs
rtogs mnyam mo zhes/ /gang gi sbas pa'i rnam thar sgrog la brtson/ /mkha' 'gro'i dbang phyug ne gu'i thugs kyi bcud/ /zung 'jug gar mkhan khyung po'i chos drug lam/ /rdor
'dzin byed ba'i gtsug rgyan rgyal rtse bas/ /legs bshad mchod yon sbrengs pas zhal sgo 'dzum/ /theg pa rim dgu tshang ba'i dkyil 'khor du/ /theg tshul 'khrul pa med pa
nyang rigs rjes/ /theg chen byang sems 'byongs pa gnas gsar ba/ /theg mchog bstan pa'i bdag por mnga' gsol mdzad/

/mkhas grub chad med gdung byon rngog pa'i zhabs/ /dpa' bo'i grong du zhugs tshe rags pa'i pur/ /sri zhu bskrun pa'i bzhugs gnas mchod sdong che/ /rab bzhengs chos sku'i klong
du thugs dgongs rdzogs/ /de nas bkra shis chos kyi 'dus pa'i gling chen por phebs nas sa khyim rdzogs par stan chags/ de yang rnam thar gyi sa bon la lo tshigs zhib cha
yod med sna tshogs dang yod pa la'ang snang la ma nges kyi dpyad mi bzod pa 'ga' mthong na'ang bla ma rags rim gong smos ltar yin la/ zhib tu ma 'tshal bar phyogs gcig
tu bsdoms par rtse gdong khri chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya sgar chen mthu stobs dbang phyug /sa skya khri chen ngag dbang kun
dga' bsod nams bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ de sras kun dga' bsod nams dbang phyug /lcam rje btsun ma/ zhwa dmar mchog gi sprul sku/ ra lung zhabs drung
mi pham bstan pa'i nyi ma/ sger pa'i rin po che nyi ma ba/ sngags 'chang tshe ring dbang po/ chos rje 'od mchog pa/ chos sde'i zur 'chad pa kun bzang rtse pa kun dga'
bkra shis/ chos rje mi pham blo gros sogs kyis mtshon pa rnams la sngags gsar rnying gi dbang rjes gnang 'khrid lung sde snod gsum gyi chos tshul mang du gsan pa dang ches
nyung ba la lar bla ma'i rnal 'byor tshe dbang tshigs bcad re gsan pa yan chad la 'brom gyis se btsun dang mi las mar pa bsten pa'i rnam thar bzhin mnyes pa gsum gyi sgo
nas gus pa lhur len pa las log sgrub dang bla ma'i skyon phra mo tsam yang mi 'tshol zhing thams cad yon tan du 'char ba lo chen 'brog mis gsang sngags kyi chos zab pa'i
brdar bdag med ma'i dbang rdzogs re la 'bri bco lnga dang lha mo ral gcig ma'i rjes gnang re la 'bri g.yag re dgos kyi yod tshul mar pa'i rnam thar du gsal ba ltar/ bla
ma dang chos kyi che ba 'don slad du sri zhu kho na mdzad cing chos gsan pa tshor yang thos lo byung lo'i ming tsam la mi 'chel bar rgya bod kyi grub mtha' so so'i bzhed
tshul gyi phyag len dang bshad thabs mtha' dag yod rgyu ba dang shes rgyu ba'i zag zog sbub ldir gyi rdzong gog ye mi 'dzin par mkhyen dpyod rnam par dag pas dpyad bzod
kho nar gnang ste dper na rngog lugs dang sa lugs kyi dbang gi dril bu dkrol lugs kyi mtha' brten pa spu ris phra mo tsam yang ma 'dres pa so sor dbye la/ ris med pa'i chos
kyi rgyun dang gdul bya'i khams dang bsam pa tha dad pa'i dbang gis gsan pa rgya gang cher gnang ba las gtso bor thugs nyams bzhes su dgos pa dag byas so byung ngo tsam
ma yin pa'i yi dam lha'i zhal mthong ba/ gsung gis gnang ba thob pa/ dam can bran du bkol ba/ rdzogs rim gyi lam la drod thob pa mdzad cing gzhan dag kyang gsan pa tsam
du ma lus par so sor blo dang 'tsham par rgya cher spel ba'i zhal slob kyi grangs thams cad brjod pa lta ga la zhig bstan pa 'dzin pa'i bshes gnyen rags bsdus tsam brjod
na/ dpal zha lu gser bkang gi gdan sa pa khyab bdag rin cen bsod nams mchog grub/ glang phu chos rje 'jam dpal chos skyong dbang phyug /zur thams cad mkhyen pa chos dbyings
rang grol/ khra tshang pa chen po khyab bdag blo mchog rig pa'i rdo rje/ rdo rje brag nas rigs 'dzin mchog

sprul padma 'phrin las/ rgyal rtse bdag po byams pa ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ ngor mkhan po thar rtse nam mkha' rin cen e waM mkhan chen dpal gling pa bsod nams rgyal
mtshan/ bye rdzing tshogs mkhan po sangs rgyas dpal bzang / gsung sprul tshul khrims rdo rje/ bang ri gter ston hU~M nag me 'bar/ skyed tshal gong mkhan po byams pa ngag
dbang bstan 'dzin/ skyed tshal 'og mkhan po ngag dbang bstan pa/ dar rgyas chos sdings pa rigs 'dzin 'phrin las lhun grub/ de sras sprul sku gter ston chen po 'gro 'dul
gter bdag gling pa/ rigs 'dzin chos dbang kun bzang / rje dpal 'byor gling pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ mtshungs med nyi ma gling pa rin cen tshul khrims bkra shis/ kun bzang
rtse pa paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ rje kun dga' bkra shis/ rab 'byams chos rje rin cen rgya mtsho/ mdo pa chos rje dge ba'i dbang po/ shar lung rab 'byams pa/ dge
slong 'phrin las rnam rgyal sogs rdo rje gdan slob dpon dang zur 'chad pa tshang ma/ do sngon chos sde'i slob dpon paN chen lung rigs/ rigs 'dzin karma gsang sngags/ sna
mo shag grub chen/ sman sgom 'brang rgyas pa/ kre bo bla ma/ sgrub rnying bla ma 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan sogs mang du byung ba phal cher gyis gsung rgyun bzung ba'i phyogs
kun tu spel nas bstan pa rin po che'i srog legs par 'thud cing la las tshe 'di'i rnam g.yeng mtha' dag rgyang du bsrings te bsam gtan gyi ro myong ba/ 'ga' zhig gis
'phrin las rnam bzhi'i sgo nas 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa sha stag byung zhing chos zhu ba po mchog dman su 'dra zhig gis kyang na yam tsam ma yin pa'i don du gnyer ba rnams
la dmar 'khrid bshad bka' phyag len gang la'ang blor ma chud bar du skyo ngal med par yang yang bskyar nas ci chud mdzad/ dam pa 'di'i yon tan gyi khyad par ni sku mthong
na mi mthun pa med pa'i mdzes shing brjid chags pa gzhan snang zil gyis gnon cing gang zag gcig la'ang mthong tshul ma nges pa sna tshogs su shar ba mthong ba tsam gyis
nyon mongs pa dang sdug bsngal gyi rtog pa thams cad rang shugs kyis 'gags pa/ yid bde zh-ing bag phebs la dge ba dang mngon par rtogs pa'i yon tan ngang gis 'phel ba/ rang
gi mnga' thang dang longs spyod kyi ched du gdams ngag mi mdzad na'ang sems can gyi don du 'gyur na der ma zad lus longs spyod la chags pa med par gzhan don sgrub pa
la mi skyo ba rgyal sras 'phags pa ngan 'gro'i gnas kyang mtho ris kyi dga' tshal du gzigs pa'i ngang tshul can/ chos zhu ba'i tshogs la phogs zur gsos mthun rkyen 'tshems
med dang rang gnas su 'gro ba'i tshe gnang sbyin dang thos bsam sgom sgrub kyi bslab ston blo dang 'tsham par gnang bas dpon slob 'bral mi phod pa lta bu byung / tshul
khrims kyi dri ngad 'thul zhing gshegs bzhud dal brel ran pa sogs spyod lam rnams lhun chags pa/ gsung gi gdangs che chung snyoms shing ha cang dal ba dang bul ba ma yin
pa'i snyan zhing 'jebs la tshig 'bru gsal bas chos gsungs pa mtha' dag nyan pa po'i tshogs kyis tshig don rtogs par sla zhing blo 'khul bas thos pa'i mod la tha mal gyi snang
ba 'gags shing mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob ste rang dbang med par rje nyid ma gtogs mi re ba'i gus pa skyes

pas 'brel tshad don ldan gyi sgo nas thar pa'i lam du 'dren/ rang bzhin gyi gsung gleng rnams kyang bstan pa 'dzin pa'i bshes gnyen/ gra pa chos byed kyi rigs su ma zad sde
dpon sbyin bdag tha na skyes pa bud med rang bzhin pa tshun la yang so so'i blo dang 'tsham pa'i ngos dge ba la bkri ba'i thabs min pa/ dmag /tshong / gshags/ grub mtha'
sna tshogs kyi chos dang bla ma sun 'byin/ 'brel med kyi nyog gtam/ rdzun/ phra ma/ tshig rtsub/ ngag kyal sogs mi gnang / chos gang gsung yang rang lugs ma 'dres pa ston
pa las gzhan gyi lugs la zur mi za/ gsol ba 'debs mkhan ma byung bar bstan na chos btsongs pa lta bur 'gro zhes 'di bzhin yod pas nyon cig ces bskul ma mi gnang / thos
bsam sgom pa 'chad nyan sku gsung thugs rten bzhengs pa dgon pa'i 'dzin skyong nad ba dbul phongs la phan btags pas mtshon mdzad pa gang la'ang ngas 'di byas so ba'i yus
mi 'dren/ bsnyen sgrub las sbyor gyi rtags mtshan bla ma yi dam chos skyong gi zhal gzigs lung bstan dbugs dbyung mngon shes grub rtags sogs yon tan khyad par can byung ba
skad mi gsung zhing gzhan nas de 'dra'i dogs gnas kyi dri ba zhus par mi dgyes pa'i sne tsam yang mi len cing dman cha kho na gnang / thugs dam zhal gzigs ngo mtshar ba'i
bsnyel tho 'di sa bon tsam las dngos su zhal lung zhu thub na zab cing rgya che ba zhig yod rigs su snang na'ang da sgos 'di'i don 'grol bar ma nus shing rtog bzo'i na
yams byas na skabs su ma che bas gang 'dug bkod par/ tshes bcu bzhi la bde mchog nag po pa'i sta gon tshugs sgrub cing mchod pa thengs gcig dang gzhan sgrub mchod bdag 'jug
bcas par rdul tshon steng nas tshar bcu gsum dbang tshar gnyis yid ches par song / tshugs pa'i nub zhal bzhi pa li ma'i sku dang / grol ba'i nub sa chen/ sems dpa' chen
po/ zha lu pa/ buddha bha dra sogs kyi bris sku dang skad cha za zir mang ba legs pa tsam yin rje bla ma gsung pas tshe gcig nyams len byas na/ byin rlabs yong ba e yin
nam gzhan nam ring gi rmi lam la tig tig med/ med rang med/ rje btsun grags pa'i thugs dam mtsho skyes/ mi g.yo ba phyag g.yon rang mgo bag dro ltas bzang / chu sprel padma
saM bha'i bsnyen pa yid ches par song / gzhung gi rtags cung zad dngos rmir mthong / khye'u bla ma shes mchod rten/ bya zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes gsum bzhi de pa la/
dbang phyug rab brtan bka' gter chos kyi mdzod/ hU~M nag me 'bar thugs sras dam pa dang / sogs dang shog dril gter gnas dang ras thums gsol 'debs la brtson na lo gcig gi
nang du mjal zer ba dang / sprel lo dpyid zla'i tshes bcur yang zer/ tshes bcu gcig la mkha' 'gros gdan 'dren/ dbang lung man ngag ston pa yin zer ba dang / drag po'i zhal
gyi sangs rgyas bstan pa la dgyes sogs mang ngag go srin po'i 'jigs pas sngangs pa las gu ru me tog dmar po la bdag dang sems can thams cad bdud dang gshin rje'i 'jigs
pa las skyob tu gsol bas je bder song ba dang / yid kyis nas bur thud sogs phul ba dang / bla ma rin po che'i thugs dam zhal sngo skya dang / de rjes mgrin snying sgrub dus
mtheb tshigs tsam bdun/ gzhi nas tsam la g.yung rgyal sngo skya nas tsam gsal ba mi rtog ting 'dzin la gnas

nas/ ra tri ta hUM phaT/ Dombhi ni hUM phaT sogs dang / gdong brnyan can nag po bdag chen thugs dam dang / rdo rje gdan pa'i thugs dam sgrub dus mda' gang tsam mo/ /mkha' sngo
sangs rang du bud med sngo nag dpral bar mgron bu btags pa zhig gis da dung sgrib pa ma byang ba 'dug zer sdigs mdzub nam mkha' la bstad do/ /bi rU pa shin tu che gsal
ba dang / sa chen na bza' 'od 'phro ba sngon po zhal ras dmar mdangs che ba gwa dang bcas pa/ shangs su tshe dpag med dang / drag dmar yongs rdzogs/ bsam grub tu dbu dgu
pa shin tu gsal ba/ 'dar mgon khang du nA ro pa mi tshad tsam/ yang ayon gyi thugs kar kye rdor lha dgu mkha' spyod drug /zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes bcu'i tho rangs ayon
da lta ji lta ba rang la yang gter sogs yin snyam/ sgam/ pag shi /'ja' gur 'ja' skya 'dug /sa skya pa chen po gos sngon dwangs gsal rnyog med/ shangs su lhan skyes/ 'jam
dpal bshes gnyen las gu ruu rgya dang bcas pa'i gru bzhi sgor mo gsal/ 'dar du tshe dpag med/ skye bdun grol 'phral ayon che zhing gsal/ padma ni mi gsal/ thugs rje chen
po zhal bcu gcig dang bcas shin tu gsal/ yang sa chen gyi rnam thar yin yang zer ayon rnam thar yin pa'i khul gyi byang shing / dkar thal srab mo yod pa la yig 'phreng bzhi
bris pa rten khebs kyis gril ba zhig byung / de'i sang zab brgya'i po ti dwags po nas 'byor yang lan cig gtor bsngos kyi skabs chos skyong thams cad zang nge dang zing
nge nyams snang du byung / chos rje tshar pa zha thul ser po bzhes pa zhig kyang byung / 'di bzhin la dpags na zab gter bzhes rgyu zhig kyang yod par mngon/ kun mkhyen bus/
rang nyid rgyal 'dod pha rol dma' dbab 'dod/ /g.yo rgyu'i rtsod pa tshig rtsub ngan sems can/ /ngag kyal sna tshogs smra zhig gzhan gter sgo de rgyud bsreg /da lta'i
rtsod pa 'di yang dmyal ba'i rgyu/ /zhes pa'i don ltar rtsod pa 'di gzhan dag rang gi nyes pa khas blangs nas spang blang mi byed pas phrag dog dang kun slong ngan pa 'phel
te bstan sel gyi rgyu las med gter rtags/ kha byang btab 'dug brag phug ces mi mdzad/ thugs rab kyi klong shin tu yangs pas tshigs bcad lhug gang la'ang phun sum tshogs
shing dper na dus kyi 'khor lo'i mngon dkyil dang rnam sras lnga phrag lnga'i chog sgrigs ltar chos rgyun mi nub pa'i btsas su nges par 'gro na yang mi dgos kha med re
gnyis ma gtogs gsar pa mangs pa dam pa gong ma rnams kyi gsung rab nub pa'i rgyur 'gro zhes brtsams chos po ti du mar longs pa yod skad kyi rang che mi 'byin/ skya ser mang
po tshogs pa'i sar rang nyid mkhas so'i grags pa sgrog ched dgos med du bshad pa mkhas nyams mi gnang zhing khyad par gsang sngags kyi chos snod ldan ma gtogs nor dang
ngo bsrung gi slad du ston pa dang khrom sgrogs mdzad par ya shin tu nga ba'i gleng brjod dang de dang mthun par bka' dam par mchis/ thugs phra rags kyi bskyed rim la brtan
pa thob cing rdzogs rim gyi lam bzang po'i grub mtha' snyogs pa rnal 'byor dbang phyug dang lo chen 'brog mi lta bu'i bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gnas rnams brjod pa'i yul
las 'das mod mdo rgyud kyi chos tshul gang la'ang tshegs chung ngu tsam gyis thugs su chud pas dus 'khor dang

mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho sogs dkyil 'khor shin tu che ba la nyin bzhi lnga/ bde mchog lo nag gur rigs bsdus kyis mtshon par nyin gnyis tsam/ dkyil 'khor chung ba'i rigs la nyin
re'i bsnyel gsos mdzad pas slob ma rjes su 'dzin pa'i dus tshig zur phra ba la yang skyon med pa'i rgyun gyi zhal 'don ltar byang chub pa dang thugs 'dzin gsar du gnang
dgos la'ang sa glang 'phreng pa'i snyan gsan phul ba zla ba gsum tsam gyi khongs su sher phyogs kyi lung gsan pa sogs dang 'dom pa'i srubs dbar la paN chen thar rtse bas
mdzad pa'i phreng ba'i mngon dkyil shog bu nyis brgya lhag tsam de shin tu byang ba thos lo zer lo ma yin par kho bo'i mngon sum du gyur cing mdor na byin rlabs rjes gnang
/ rig gtad/ 'khrid/ man ngag gang gi skabs su'ang chags thogs mi mnga' ba blo chen tshangs pa rgan pos kyang 'gran par ga la nus/ chos mthun 'tsho ba med pa/ ya rabs dmangs
su babs pa/ rgas shing khogs pa/ ngan song / nad pa/ dbul 'phongs nyam thag gi rigs rnams la rang gi bu gcig pu ltar rjes su brtse zhing sku la bsdo ba'i drag por chos
skyong gis 'phrin las rang shugs kyis bsgrubs na min pa 'khon 'dzin dang las sbyor dmigs su phug pa mi gnang bar theg pa chen po'i blo sbyong ba 'ba' zhig gis ltas ngan
g.yang du len/ skye ba dang 'jug pa la dbang thob pas byang gtsang rong gsum/ gra dol yar shar nub nas rgyal nad smyo 'bog sogs gdon drag pos zin te sman pas bor ba du
ma'ang bka' bsgo rjes gnang byin rlabs tsam gyis nad gdon rnams phyir 'pho ba dang rtsa log rlung log gi gegs sel/ 'du ba rnam bzhi 'khrugs pa sman gyis ma snyoms pa dag
kyang gzhil te 'chi bdag gi kha nas phyir slog pa grangs mang ba thugs rdo rje'i ting 'dzin las su rung ba'i mthur sems/ dbang gi ye shes 'bebs pa gnang tshe lus kyi gar
byed cing 'phar g.yo/ ngag glal zhing smra nyams/ sems bde stong gi ngang du lhan ner 'gro ba sna re nges par 'ong gshis da lta rang ye shes phebs byung snyam pa'i dga'
spro mos gdung tshad med pa 'byung / sgam zhing dul la ngo lkog chung bas lan cig mjal ba dang rgyun dus 'dris pa gnyis la khyad par med pa bka' gdams jo bo yab sras kyi
rnam thar dang mtshungs/ phyogs phebs kyi 'chad nyan gyis gtsos pa'i gzhan phan gyi 'phrin las skyong dgos pa'i skabs ma gtogs don med kyi 'du 'dzi'i rjes su mi 'brang bar
so sod lkog nyal gyi ci bder gnas pa la mtshams kyi ming btags pa'i chen po rnams kyi spyod tshul bug sgo 'dag dbyar gyi khongs nas yig 'grul dang mdun gshoms/ mtshams
yun ring du bcad kyang da lam dmigs bsal gyi gal chen byung zer ba tsho dang mi 'dra ba'i thog mar ji tsam bcad pa nas bzung grol ba'i dus la ma sleb kyi bar du dam bca'
las mi g.yel ba lhur mdzad/ thugs brel dang sku bsnyun pa gang gi'ang rjes su mi 'gro bar bskyed rdzogs kyi rnal 'byor theg pa chen po'i blo sbyong sogs kyi spros med dang
cho ga /ljags bzlas/ gtor chog /dus gtor bla ma rnams kyi dus dran gyis mtshon pa/ zhag re dang zla re'i star chags rnams la thang lhod ma shor ba'i ci mdzad rgya bod kyi
paN grub kyi rnam par thar pa dang mthun par snang ngo / /'di lo'i dbyar sngar dang mi 'dra ba'i me tog la

shin tu mnyes shing de'ang rten gyi drung du mi bsgrig par sku'i rgyab mdun g.yas g.yon khor yug bskor ba la spro bar mdzad pa ni 'og min sogs kyi gnas rnams su me tog gis
brgyan pa'i bkod pa bshad pa dang mthun pa'i zhing khams gzhan dag tu gshegs pa'i brdar snang / mchod dpon 'jam dbyangs la nyin gcig kyal ka'i tshul du nga shi na skye ba
blangs pa dga' 'am/ ma blangs pa dga' gsung bar de 'dra mi gnang ba zhu/ rnam rtog kyang za de bzhin byung na skye ba bzhes pa rang los dga' zhus pas khyed rang tsho bsam
blo legs po zhig thong dang bsams bzhin srid par skye ba bzhes pa ni ngo mtshar che shas kha gzhan ma skye ba zer tshad ni ya mtshan rgyu rang ci mchis 'khor ba thog ma
med pa nas 'khor bzhin par 'dug khyog khyod tsho dang nga mi 'dra bas ltos zhig gsung pa dang gzhan yang thengs 'ga' re de dang dbyibs mtshungs pa kha yar gnang ba lo rting
ma gzugs sku rags pa'i za ma tog bsdu ba'i brdar snang yang phyag phyi rnams la rtog pa 'phros chod du mi gda'o/ /rang che khengs pa'i ri bo mthon po'i rtser/ /legs bshad
gtam gyi chu bo ga la 'drongs/ /gzur gnas thugs kyi gshong bur mdo rgyud kyi/ /mkha' glang gzegs ma phyogs brgya nas 'bab 'khyil/ /'jig rten mthun 'jug gtan bde'i don
po cher/ /rloms na chos nyid bden ston thub pa yi/ /bzhed 'bras gsung las skyes pa'i slob bu'i tshad/ /rgyu skar grangs kyis gzhal yang rtogs nus min/ /mthong bas mtshan
dpe'i mdzes sku mi mthun bral/ /thos pas drug cu'i dbyangs snyan rna ba'i dpyid/ /dran pas srid zhi'i 'jigs skyob chos kun gzigs/ /rnam 'dren yon tan tshogs rnams gcig
bsdus 'dra/ /chags bral tshul khrims dri ldang nyan thos gzugs/ /gzhan phyir lus srog gtong phod rgyal ba'i sras/ /bdag med gtso mos mgrin par rtag 'khyud pa'i/ /sgyu ma'i
rol rtsed 'di ko su yis bskrun/ /'jig rten spyod pa'i rjes 'gro chos brgyad gdon/ /phra mo'i shas kyang gang thugs ma gos pas/ /ci mdzad dam pa'i chos su nyer 'gro bar/
/shAkya seng ge'i rnam thar dpe zlar 'os/ /mthon po'i grub mtha' snyogs te zung 'jug skur/ /bzhengs par nges kyang da dung slob lam la/ /sbyongs zhes dman cha 'dzin pa'i
zol sbyor 'di/ /cher snyigs gdul bya'i snang ngor dgongs sam snyam/ /zhing gzhan bzang po'i skal ba can gyi 'gro/ /'dren la spro ba'i rtse 'jo rgod pa'i brda/ /rtogs min
yid srubs mthu las kun dga' bo'i/ /gsol gdab rtog tshogs rags pa 'gags pa'i spun/ /sgyur byed ces pa sa phag hor zla dang po'i nang du dpal ldan 'bras spungs su gdan drangs
te mdo dbang gis gtsos pa'i gsang sngags gsar rnying gi zab chos mang du zhu ba'i rtsis yin na'ang gnas chung chos skyong chen po khog tu brlams te da lam chos bka' sogs
rgyas par tshugs na khyed dpon slob su rigs la gegs che ba 'dug pas skor cig 'then pa'i slar rim gyis btsugs chog tshul gyi zhib cha sde pa blo bzang mthu stobs la gsungs
'dug pa bzhin rje bla mar yang de ba'i rgyu mtshan phul zhing zhag bdun tsam bzhugs ring ljags lung thung thung 'dra dang chos dang 'brel ba'i gleng mo gang 'phel zhus
legs ldan rje'i shangs mtshal gyi khu bas brdzis pa'i tshe dpag med kyi sku khyad can de gnang / da lo sku

dog yod par sku rim dang chos sder sku mtshams gnang rgyu yang tshe sgrub dang bsun bzlog la ched gnyer mdzad dgos tshul gsol ba na/ rje mkhyen brtse'i gsung mgur du/ tshe
ring lo brgya thub pa dang / /tshe thung da lta shi ba gnyis/ /rnam pa'i sgo nas khyad par che/ /ngo bo'i sgo nas bzang ngan med/ /thams cad sgyu ma rmi lam yin/ /tshe ring
thung gang dga' ma dgar zhog /nga 'chi ba la 'jigs pa mi gda'o/ /zhes pa'i don dang mtshungs par bka' las da cha blo sbyong ba'i lugs yin pas/ na ba dga' na na ba byin
gyis brlab tu gsol/ zhes sogs lung 'dren dang bcas na shi gson par ci byung yang dkon cog la blo bkal nas shi dogs pa'i rim gro byas na dkon mchog la yid ma ches par 'gro
ba 'dra gsung par gcig tu de bzhin yin kyang rgya bod kyi dam pa tsho'i rnam thar la brtags tshe dgag bya dgos dbang gis nges pa mi 'dug pas re zhig gi bar du 'tsho zhing
gzhes nas spyi sgos mtha' dag gi bstan pa'i srog shing du 'gyur nges pas thugs sna bstungs pa de ltar mi legs tshul nan tar gsol ba na bka' bzhin bsgrub gsung ba rjes
su byas tshe gzhan ngo bsrung bar 'dug /rje rdo rje gdan pa'i dus kyi mkhyen brtse chen mo'i phyag bris mdo dbang gi tsa ka li rnams ras bse las grub pa'i ljid che ba nas
slar bka' dbang la phebs dgos phyin da lam 'di gar bzhag pa 'gab 'dra zham ring pa rnams kyis zhus tshe khong dpon slob mthong chen po yod bas da res khyer nas rtsis 'bul
zhu gsung / chu kha par sman sgom 'brang rgyas pas gdan 'dren la phyin skabs bka' las da cha rgyun ring po rang sdod pa mi 'char nges yin pas slar chos sde nas 'phros shig
gtong bas de dus cis kyang yong thub pa dgos tshul gnang bar da dung bstan don la rgyun gang ring bzhugs dgos zhus pas zangs mdog dpal rir ayon chen po'i g.yas g.yon
du bzhugs khri rim par bshams 'dug pa la rje rdo ring pa chen po nas rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan yan bzhugs pa'i mthar khri stong pa zhig mchis pa bdag gi yin 'dug
ces zhal gyis ma bzhes/ des na sku skye phebs dgos zhus par rje btsun kun spangs pa chen po dang sgo rum pa gnyis zangs mdog dpal ri kho nar bzhugs pa la tshar chen sogs
bla ma yab sras gcig la gcig thugs chags pa'i 'bral mi phod pa lta bur yod gshis bdag kyang de mtshungs su sdod pas skye ba mi len/ 'phros 'di rnams bdag ma shi bar su
la'ang bshad na mi yong ba'i dpang por dpal mgon 'khor bcas nged rang gnyis ka'i mdun na yod do/ /zhes lhug par stsal snang / de nub sne'u zhol gyi bzhugs 'tsher gyi thog
nas 'bras spungs phyogs su zhal gzigs te ring 'tsho'i smon lam dang mchog gsum dam par gsol 'debs gnang / sang nyin se mo de'i thang la phyag g.yog dmangs ma rnams sngon
du brdzangs/ chibs shol nas mchod dpon dang byams pa gnyis kyis phyag phyi zhus nas sku ngal gsos shing de nas chibs thog tu khyon pa dang lhan du lam khyod la da lam tsam
min pa yong mi dgos pa 'dug gsung ba byams pas slar sku mtshams grol nas phebs dgos pas de 'dra mi gsung ba zhu zhes zhus song ba bka' las khyed tsho mi glen par 'dug
da lo nga rang gi snang rtags dang sku zhabs chen mo'i bka' gang la dpags kyang mi sdod par 'dug gsung zhing

der ma zad zha lu mkhan rin po che sman khang nas la yang gtsang du rjes ma phebs dus gsung bgros byung tshor du mchis/ chos sder phebs nas nged rang gis rgyu mtshan gsol ba
dang phyag g.yog sogs phyi nang mang po nas bskul ma zhus pa ngo ma bzlog pa'i gong dkar chos sder mang ja sbyor sbrel thog tshe gzungs sher snying gi bzlog pa/ bkra shis
rtse chos sde'i mgon khang so sor bskang gso brgya rtsa/ bka' 'gyur sgrog pa/ sAtstsha 'bum ther sogs bsgrub pa gnang / rdo rje gsum mi 'da' ba'i sku mtshams dam pa'i
ngang nas thun mtshams tshor gsan yig gi zin bris phyag dper 'bebs pa'i yig mkhan chos sde pa'i gra pa chos mdzad rgyal mtshan bzang pos byas pa chig dril du gnang ma thub
gshis po ti thung nge ba zhig gi rtsis las lhag ma rnams 'phror lus pas da lam rnam thar skabs su zhib par 'dri ba'i rngo ma thogs/ sku cung zad ma bde ba'i rnam pa la
sman sgom 'tsho byed 'brang rgyas pa sku'i 'phrod bsten du 'bod pa gnang song ba rje btsun yab dang thun mong ba'i rtsa dbu ma'i nyams 'khrid sogs zab chos 'ga' zhig gnang
bzhed pa'i bsnyad btags las 'phrod bsten 'gangs can 'bul ma dgos shing gsol sman kha yar phul nas gzhi med du song na'ang zhing 'dir bzhugs bzhed med pa'i mdangs kyi gsung
gleng 'ga' zhig byung tshod du 'dug kyang yar 'byor nas sku khams bde ba'i gnas tshul las de rigs kyi zhib cha ma byung / lha rje 'brang rgyas pa rdzong bda' grub rjes
nas bzung sku zo mdog sngar las bzang zhing yang zor che ba'i tshul mdzad na'ang / gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir bstan pa rin po che 'chad nyan bsam sgom gyi sgo nas spel ba'i
'phrin las rgya cher grub pa dang snyigs mar spyod pa'i 'gro ba'i ngang tshul la gzhan snang tsam du nges par 'byung ba'i thugs sun snang skyo shas che zhing grangs med
pa'i zhing khams rgya mtshor yid can rnams kyi don rlabs po che 'grub pa'i dus babs la gzigs te lo sngun ma'i hor zla bcu gcig pa gshol ba'i dbang du byas na hor zla dgu
pa dang ba nged kyi smin drug zla ba'i 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta mngon dga'i zhing du gshegs pa'i dus chen yar tshes bcu bzhi'i nyin phan snyun du mngon pa ci yang med

gsol ba thob/ /kho bos snying nas brtse ba'i bsam sbyor gyis/ /dus kun rjes su 'dzin no skal ldan tsho/ /brgyud pa bzang po sa skya pa yis zin/ /mes po mtshan ldan tshar
pa chos rjes bskyangs/ /ban rgan nga rang bslu med yin nam snyam/ /bu kun tsab tsob ma mang gsol ba thob/ /'di phyi bar dor bslus na kho bo zhan/ /byin rlabs che chung

chos dang 'brel ba'i bslab ston shugs 'byung dang nged rang la thugs mnyes pa'i bka' 'phros kyang kha yar

gnang zhing so so'i mgo la phyag gis byil byil dang dbu thug gis byin gyis brlabs te gnas so sor btang / gtor gzhis rnams yun rings pas gsar du spo dgos 'dug ces bstab pa dang
tshang ma chab gcig par sbal gyi yang thog tu rgyas par 'bul ba mdzad nas byams par sang zhogs thor ja mi dgos da dung ja zhim po skol gsungs byams pas snyung ba bzhin
med dam chab skol e bzhes zhus par na tsha med par chu skol ga la dgos zhes bzhad/ de nas srod thun la tshugs pa'i sgang mjug tsam la 'da' kha ma'i rnal 'byor gyis mtshams

pa'i zhing khams gdan gsum tshang ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i rigs kyi bdag por gdan drangs/ de'i dus byams pa gzims chung du nyer len la bsdad pa'i gnyid thum pa zhig
gi gseng la hig gi sgra byung nas bltas tsa na sku gshegs zin 'dug zer/ de skabs sde pa brgya tsho ba'i chos rje bkra shis lhun po'i sngags gra ba'i sgrigs 'grim pa de gsung

mi la mdang nga la rmi lam 'di 'dra byung ba ci yin zhes blo ma bde ba'i rnam par byed cing / dus mtshungs su zha lur khyab bdag rin cen bsod nams mchog grub kyi 'od gsal
du rje 'di nyid dgyes pa'i tshul du phebs raksha'i phreng ba 'di thugs tshags gnang ba zhu da nged la mi dgos pa 'dug gsung bar byung gnang / zhag kha yar gyi sngon tsam
la stong ra ba'i mna' ma sde pa 'phrang 'go ba'i tsha mor gtogs pa rtsa sgo yangs pa de'i rmi lam dkyus ma dang mi 'dra ba'i gsal por byed pa zhig la rmi lam du nyi ma
bzhud la khad lho nub kyi nam mkhar bla ma rdo rje gdan pa yin zer ba legs par btags tshe rdo rje 'chang gi sku'i dbyibs la sa zhu bzhes nas bden bral gyi mtshams su 'ja'
'od dang bcas yer gyis phebs song rjes nyi ma'ang bzhud de nag thum byed pa rmis tshul de ga'i ma rgan mo 'phrang 'go ba'i spyil por sdod mir bshad pa zhing brjes pa'i skad

bar mngon/ dpon slob kyi sku zhabs nas 'ongs zer ba'i bang chen byung ba'i rten gyi dril kha bshig pa'i nang du li sku kha btags sman tse dang bcas sum mtshan yod pa

'gyed btang / bzhi thog tu bdag chen rin po cher 'bul bar rna ro'i bande gshin rje grags kyis bzhengs pa'i rje btsun rin po che'i sku brnyan gzhis ka sne'ur bzhugs pa rjes

bdag tu/ /dpal ldan rdo rje sems dpar bzhengs de ci/ /thub bstan cha shas bcu gnyis yongs rdzogs shing / /mkhyen brtse nus pa'i tsha zer stong 'phro ba'i/ /bshes gnyen chos
dbyings thun 'tshams gzhon nu'i phag /gzims pa'i dus kyi skal ngan kye ma hud/ /baiDUr zhun ma ltar 'phos

mkha' ngos la/ /sna tshogs 'ja' sprin 'od dra'i ri mo'i mdangs/ /legs bris bkod pa bskrun pa'i sgyu ma yis/ /rjes 'jug mya ngan gdung ma gzhil lam ci/ /'on te ganggA'i klung
gi rdul snyed kyis/ /bgrang bar nus min dag pa'i zhing khams su/ /mtha' klas sprul pa ston pa'i thugs rje'i spyan/ /bdag sogs gdul byar gzigs tshe yid dbang spro/ /tshogs
gnyis nyal 'gro'i phung po'i chu gter la/ /dge ba'i klung gis gang bar ltos min kyang / /rjes 'brang legs byas zhing gi so nam du/ /'dzad med rnam dkar char rgyun chal
chil phob/ /rigs brgya'i khyab bdag rje btsun zha lu pas/ /dus dgra 'jam dpal dmar po lha lnga dang / /sku gdung rin chen dbang gi rgyal po gnyis/ /dbyer med ngo mtshar
mchod pa de rmad byung / /de ltar dus gsum rgyal ba thams cad kyi spyi gzugs bka' drin mtshungs med dpal ldan bla ma dam pa khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa' dang gnyis su med
pa gang gi rnam par thar pa ches phra ba ni spyan dang mngon par shes pa la chags thogs med pa rnams ma gtogs 'jig rten gyi byed po tshangs pa lta bus kyang brjod par mi
nus na gzhan dag gis lta ga la zhig thun mong ba'i gdul bya'i spyod yul du gyur pa'i mdzad pa rags pa'i lo zla tshes grangs yul dang gnas sogs rjes 'jug rnams le lo'i mal
du 'du 'dzi'i gnyid la g.yur bas zhib par ma rtogs kyang rgyus yod kyi tho thor bu dang yid gnyis su gyur pa mang dag khyab bdag mkhan chen zha lu pa chen po/ /sgrub rnying
slob dpon 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan/ /gong dkar chos sde'i zur 'chad pa dpyod ldan 'phrin las rnam rgyal sogs 'ga' zhig la dpyad cing gsan yig dang dam pa gzhan gyi
rnam thar lo rgyus/ dus dang lo zla lung rigs kyis bsgrub nus pa dang la lar rung mthun kyang 'ga' zhig sbyar ba'i go rim bsgrigs par so skye'i snang la ma nges kyi 'khrul
bar tshad bzung dka' na'ang phyogs 'gro tsam la yid brtan du rung ba'i lugs su bgyis te rtogs brjod kyi rim pa cher long tsam bshad zin to/ /blo chen mes pos rig byed gtam
gyi sbyor ba ma lus gcig tu bsdus/ /dbyangs can lha mo mgrin par byon te brjod pa rnam dag tshig 'phreng spel/ /brtan pa'i 'khor los gsang gsum mi zad yon tan bang mdzod
sgo phye nas/ /bla ma mchog gi rtog pa brjod las bdag 'dra'i blo gros mthu yis ci/ /lha lam gser ldan ri bo mthon po'i khyon/ /rab phra bug pa'i nang nas lta ba bzhin/
/'phags chen dam pa'i rnam thar ches brling yang / /rang blo dang 'tsham brjod la klan ka su/ /zas gtsang sras kyi brgya phrag mdzad pa la/ /bsngags pa'i dpal ldan ma khol
bsod nams kyis/ /phung po srid rtser 'phyur des yid drangs nas/ /ngal ba'i dka' thub len la gcig tu spro/ /rgyal sras spyod pa'i spangs rtogs mtsho ltar zab/ /ldugs snod
tshig don a mra'i tshig gu tsam/ /kho bo'i blo gros ku sha'i rtse bzhin phra/ /de phyir ma rtogs 'khrul pas nongs kun 'chags/ /de ltar na yang rje btsun bka' 'gyur ba'i/
/mdzad pa'i cha shas mthong ba'i shing rta yis/ /mi phyed dad pa'i nor gyi dpya drangs tshe/ /srid zhi'i dbul phongs gdung ba pha mthar byed/ /'di la sgo gsum 'bad ched
ngal bsten tshogs/ /mgon po khyod kyi dpal chen he ru ka'i/ /grong du nyer khrid kha sbyor bdun ldan sku/

/ring por mi thogs 'grub par bdag byin rlobs/ /spyi dang khyad par tshar chen yab sras kyi/ /snyan brgyud tshad ma bzhi ldan ring lugs bstan/ /ma pham dbus 'gyur 'chang du
'byon min par/ /thos bsam bsgom pa dar zhing rgyas gyur cig /de ltar 'a zha rgyal po'i gdung las bka' drin mtshungs pa ma mchis pa'i dpal ldan bla ma dam pa khyab bdag rdo
rje sems dpa'i ngo bo mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam thar dad pa'i rlabs phreng 'di ni rdo rje 'chang chen po mkhan chen zha
lu pa rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyis ring po zhig nas bka' gnang zhing dbon mkhyen rab rnam rgyal dang mkhyen rab blo ldan gnyis kyis reg zig dang bcas snga mo nas bskul
ba dang / rdo rje bra nas rig 'dzin sprul pa'i sku mchog sogs dad 'dun can du mas mtshams sbyar ba ltar 'dun pa rtse gcig pa yod na'ang kho bo don med rnam g.yeng gi
yang bran du gyur pas mos pa lam byed du song ba nye lam rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab rin po che'i dbon rigs rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag bco brgyad chos rje byams pa ngag
dbang lhun grub/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen po'i dbon rin po che nam mkha' bsod nams dbang gi rgyal po/ grub pa'i dbang phyug lcags zam pa chen po'i gdung rigs rjes
drung ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phun tshogs gsum gyis thog drangs skal ldan gyi gdul bya nyi shu skor la zhwa lu mkhan chen kun spangs pa chen pos skyid shod dogs bde lho
mos gzhis kar mdo rgyud rgya mtsho'i yang snying nges don snying po'i dam chos gsung ngag slob bshad rin po che rdzogs par stsal ba'i tshe dpon slob gsum gyis bla ma brgyud
pa'i kha skong du cis kyang rtsoms shig par gsung gis bskul ba la brten nas slob bshad 'dzin pa'i za hor gyi bande ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho 'jigs med go cha thub
bstan lang tsho'i sdes A na la zhes pa me 'brug nag pa zla ba'i tshes bcu bdun lhag pa lha mtshams kyi 'grub sbyor nas dbu btsugs na'ang zin bris la dogs gnas mang ba'i
phyogs kun tu dri mol gyi sgugs sdod la brten dal 'gros kyi ngos snron gyi zla ba'i yar ngo'i tshes gnyis rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyi dus dran gyi nyin rgyal
khab chen po dmar po rir sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni gnas brtan rig pa 'dzin pa 'jam dbyangs grags pas bgyis pa slob bshad zab mo'i bstan pa rin po che phyogs dus gnas skabs
thams cad du dar zhing rgyas la yun ring du gnas pa gyur cig /manggalaM//
